samujjvalānuṣṭhānena kṣaṇāya āhūtā bhavanti pratyeka vyaktiḥ karmaśaktiniyamitasāmājikasasthāne vidhṛtā tiṣṭhati pratyeka naraśca tathā ubhayabalo jīvaḥ ekataḥ sāskṛtikādarśaiḥ niyantritaḥanyataścavyaktigatāstitvapravāhe rūpagatakammabalena niruddhastiṣṭhati sāmājikapaṭabhūmikāyā manuṣya prati dṛṣṭipāte kṛteida spaṣṭa bhavati yat sa sāmājikadaśā prati tasya carmaṇi ca asthisu ca asvastikarīmatha ca sambhāvanāmayīmubhayabalatā vahati sāmājamātreṣu asmābhiḥ kiñcidvastu jñāyate  yatra mūlībhūta āśayo hi bhangasakalpatāsāsūyatāduḥkhasvapnabhaṅgatābhagnāśāḥ catatra ca nikaṭastha dūrastha vā tamasācchannāgādhamṛtyuvilam śiśavaḥ kathamapi jāyantesvastijanake pariveśe eva śīghrameva te āviṣkurvanti yat śiśujanā ākāṅkṣāpūraṇāpekṣayā pṛthivyā anyatara lakṣya varttate tataḥ para sa jñātumarhati yat jīvana prāyaśaḥ bhagnasakalpatvādapūrṇākāṅkṣātvācca krandanasya sthānam śiśuḥ kramaśaḥ tattathyena ātmāna samādhātu śikṣate yat janā mūlataḥ tasyākāṅkṣāpūraṇayantratvena na varttante bauddhadarśanamateśiśuḥ indriyavṛttimān jīvaviśeṣaḥ  vikhyātāgnyūpadeśe ucyate yat jīvanasya sādhāraṇīṣu daśāsu eva ā janmano mṛtyu yāvat sarvāṇi vastūni tṛṣṇāgnau ca durdamaprayojanāgnau ca vartante pratyeka vyaktiḥ ghṛṇāgninā mohāgninā ca saha vasatitathā ca tasmin vartante janmajarāmṛtyuḥduḥkhaśokaḥkaṣṭakṣobhaḥbhagnāśā ca bauddha nikaṣā jīvana dahanatvena lakṣyate sabhyatāyā yasmin kasminnapi paryāye ubhayabalatāyāmavaśyakaraṇīyatāyā bhagnasakalpatāyā ca mūlagatā gācit bhītistiṣṭhati  sā bhītiḥ mānavajīvanasya hṛdaye satī vyākhyā karoti kathamādita eva mānavakriyāsu śaktiviruddhakāryakaraṇāya tathā śakterapavyavahārāya prāvaṇya  vartate  manuṣyaḥ tasya sarveṣāmudyamānā pādanyāsaḥ śithila iti sandigdhe evañca sotiśayoktyā pratyeka sakaṭa prakāśayati sa kevala tathye na viśvasitiapi tu adhikatarābhirucyā sa viśvasiti sa prayojanīyagurutvāpekṣayā adhikatarotsāhena praśnam samādadhāti pratyeka vyāpāre atikriyastiṣṭhati sa ātmāna tasya karmaṇe krīḍāyai ca sābhiniveśa samarpayati  ta dāsīkṛtya yasya parisamāptiḥ jāyate sa cintayati yat sa kevala saphalatvenātmāna prakāśayatikintu vastutaḥ ta kārāstha kṛtvaiva tasya sṛṣṭhirjayati manuṣyaścintayati yat sa kevala cintayatiparantu vastutaḥ tasya cintā jīvananiyamādhīnā jāyante yathā ca ālaphreḍakorajivskiḥ tarkayatitaccintanaviṣayā piñjaratvena vrajanti  yadāviṣkṛta manuṣyeṇa ta paritaḥ yāḥ śaktayastiṣṭhanti tāsā paripālāya saraleṣu jaṭileṣu vāādimeṣu vaijñānikeṣu vā cintāyā āviṣkāreṣu evāntimaḥ śabdo vartate api ca keciccaturā upāyāḥ santi ye manuṣya śvāsarodhakaradaśāyā mukta karttumarhanti avaśeṣe sarve rabhasāt samatvena pariṇatā bhavanti atra ko hetuḥ atrāya hetuḥ  manuṣya ātmānametādṛśena vīryeṇābhiniveśena caiṣu praśneṣu niyojayatitathā casa jīvanametādṛśyā vismayakaryāmū aṭṭālikāyā vāsayogya kartu ceṣṭate ivayena sa svīyasṛṣṭitaḥ mukti labdhu nārhati prāyaśūnyatāpīyadivase himībhūtahimavisarpaṇapādukāyā gatiriva tasya janasya gatirjāyate yā svaya ajñasya śiśoḥ jihvāyā dravati  yaḥ śiśuḥ prathama himasya upari calatipratisamaya manuṣyaḥ tadīyasṛṣṭiśīlaśaktiniḥsṛṣṭe nūtane pariprekṣite tathā mukhe svapitisa svapnaḥ tasya prabhurbhavativiśeṣeṇa yadi sa ta svapna vāstavāyita karttu śaknoti eva sampūrṇataḥ prakṛtistho janaḥ yastadīyaśaktīḥ prakāśayan vasatipraśnasamādhānāya sṛṣṭiśīlatayātmāna vivṛṇotisa tadīyasṛṣṭibhiḥ kārāruddho bhavaticintā vā bhāvanā vādhāraṇā vā sasthā vāutpanna vastu ādarśo vā  yadeva bhavatu vā na bhavatu vāsaḥ asaralaḥ preṣito jīva iti saralo hetuḥ sa yat karoti tasminnaya balapūrvo guṇo vartate sa na kṣamo bhavati  na jñānāyana ca āviṣkārāyasa khalu preṣitaḥ eva vidho jīvaḥ san tadīyavicitranaipuṇya prāyeṇa vyavaharati pratyakṣīkaraṇād viratyartha yat ayameva mārgo yatra sosti tasya vyavahāraḥ khalu balāt sidhyati iti āviṣkārāya tasyāsti gabhīrācetanānīhā tathā bādhā kasyacidviṣayasya śikṣaṇāya janānā bādho viśiṣṭeṣu kṣetreṣu vicitraḥ ayamasmābhiḥ nirdhāraṇātmakomanoyoga iti kathyate  gacchatā kālena punaḥ yat kiñcid ghaṭiṣyate tat kenāpi ākāṅkṣaṇīyaparivartanamiti vyākhyāta bhaviṣyati kintu janasyopari na kiñcit samāpatitamiveti  janaḥ karma karoti  sa kadāpi aniyata tarkayitumarhati yat sa kṣudhāvaśāt ca indriyavṛttivaśāt ca sāmājike sasthāne aśagrahaṇa karoti kintu kṣudhādayaḥ na sapramāṇa tasya gabhīratamāmantardṛṣṭi tathā sṛṣṭiśīlatāmupasthāpayantitathāpi te eva tasya samīpe prāptavyasya sāmājikavinimayasya kevalā ākārāḥ te tamātmavināśisandhānād rakṣantiyat sāmājikasūtramantareṇa bhaviṣyatiyatra viṣaye tasya sapramāṇatā lakṣyate ata eva sāskṛtika sasthāna sāmājika cādarśa prati tasya pravṛttiḥ na kadāpi sukhagamyā bhavati sa sāmājikaniyantraṇa necchati tathāpi tatraiva sa jīvikānirvāhārtha tat niyantraṇamatyāvaśyakamiti paśyati buddho manuṣyasyoddhāra cakāreti pradhāno viṣayaḥ sa uddhārobhavat unmattasamājāt asusthāyāḥ saskṛteḥ doṣayuktajanajīvanāt ca yat jīvana dalabaddhamatha ca sarvatrajaṭila vikṛta vā vyaktitva prakāśayatiyatra śaktivyavahāraḥ pravṛttyā tāḍitastathāniyantritaḥ  buddha etādṛśājjanajīvanāntara muñcati ye pāścātya deśīyāḥ śikṣārthinonubhavanti yat sāmājikajīvanasya adarśabhūteṣu rūpeṣu yanmūlya tasya  guṇadoṣavivecanesamartha āsīt buddhakṛtā sāmājikarūpāṇā viruddhe ākṣepā atīva caramā āsan adhunā vaya saskṛteḥ vyakteśca madhye sambandhasya prakṛtau yaccintayāmastadapekṣayādhikatara yāvanna jānīmaḥtāvadaya siddhāntaḥ pāścātyopajātīyasaskārāpekṣayā nagaṇya iti draṣṭavyam preṣitajīvanasya pariprekṣitenyabhāvaviṣaye buddhaḥ kimacintayat api vikalpo varaṇīyaḥ tajjāḍya vyākhyāti katha saskṛtayaḥ parivartanasya pakṣe dhīra calanti katha vā druta parivartana mānava nīticyuta karoti kutra vā kāṭhinya jāyate yat samagra sāmājika rūpa parivartanāya atīva anivārya karoti  yadā vaya bauddhapunarjanmavāda smarāmaḥ tadedameva smartavyam  kimartha buddhaḥ purātanasāmājikasṛṣṭibhyaḥ mānavavyaktitva rakṣitu prārthayate  sma  yataḥ yadā vaya punarjanma smarāmaḥ tadā vaya smarāmo yat itihāsasya asmin yuge ādarśa pradarśayata āvegapravaṇena preṣitasya jīvasya śaktiḥ samarūpapreṣitasahasrajīvānā sañcitaśaktibhiḥ  bhuktā bhavati  atītaphalopeto vyaktugaṇaḥ prākśaktireva āgacchati asmin bauddhe pariprekṣite idameva vismayakara bhittimulayadi prabhāvagatā gabhīrāviśvāsaḥ anyaiḥ janaiḥ ākāra prāpnotitarhi asmāka jīvana vyāpaka vibhakteṣu janeṣu gabhīramatha ca vistṛtamupādāna na bhavitumarhativastūnā samakṣa ida spaṣṭamiva pratibhāti yatyadi anye jīvāḥ yathā vaya tathā acetanapreṣaṇayā vyavacchidyatetathā ca eṣā janānā svābhāvikī sāmājikī sṛṣṭiḥ akalyāṇamayī bhavati yathā asmāka kadāpi vā sandehasūcaka kāraṇamastitarhi anyajīvanagataprabhāvasūcakabauddhasaśayaḥ susthe tathā yuktigrāhye bhittimūle sthāpitaḥ sāmājikāmarṣasya asyā pravaṇatāyā suṣṭhu adhika gurutva deyam yādṛśa gurutva bauddhaśāstreṣu dīyate tadapekṣayāpi yataḥ aya vyāpāraḥ sambhavataḥ sāmājitavyavahārasya sandhānasamyogasūtram kevalamasmāka paricitteṣu samājeṣu ata eva ayameva sampūrṇaḥ svābhāviko vyāpāro yat sāmājikānā pratiṣṭhānānā tathā teṣā prabhāvānā kṛteyān prabhāvān narāḥ parasparakṣetreṣu vyavaharantibauddheṣu baddhamūlamaviśvāsa vaya śasemahi svādhīnajātitvena ādhunikaśrīlakāyā utthānamadhikṛtya rigins yāmālocanā cakāra tatra cyate yat aya deśaḥ katiṣu viṣayeṣu sacetana āsīt tathā hi  vyvasthitaḥ lābhaḥuccākāṅkṣāmanuṣyāṇāmupari manuṣyāṇā kartṛtvakaraṇamūlakohakāraḥ ete viṣayāḥ khalu mānavasaghānā durmocanīyāḥ sahacarāḥ ayamaviśvāsaḥ kasyacit saketasya upari sagaurava varṇyateyaḥ saketaḥ reguṇe viśvaśāntibauddhamandirasya pārśve avasthite prekṣāgṛhe vaktuḥ vedikāyāḥ paścāt vartate katīnā janānā sahayogitāmāyāyā kiñcidapūrva bhojya svargādupahṛta bhavati etādṛśamapūrva bhojya nāsti buddhena ucyate yata sarve janāḥ adhyavasāyāt sveṣā muktimavaśyameva sādhayeyuḥ paścātyamatānusārataḥ ayamaviśvāsocintanīyaḥ aya rājadroha eva yathā eriṣṭaṭalaḥ paśyati manuṣyaḥ prakṛtyā rājanītiko jīvaḥ sa sāmājikādānapradānayormadhye sāmājika yoga paśyati yatra tasya vāsaḥ sāmājiko vyavahāraḥ manuṣyasya sārabhūto vyāpāraḥ ekākitā nirjanatā ca sāmājikavyarthatā sūcayataḥ manuṣyasya pakṣe samājabaddhatva ca nirjanatva ca ityanayormadhye kataradadhikatara svābhāvikamiti viṣayosmābhiḥ samyak na jñāyate eśīyo mānavaḥ nirjanatāpoṣakatvena bauddhadharma gṛhṇāti sa dharmaḥ susthataro vikalpa upayukta āśrayaśca yatra manuṣyasya sthitirvivicyate pāścātyo naraḥ nareṇa saha parasparakarmavinimaye tathā sambandhasthāpane sarvavidhām āśā poṣayati prakṛtyā saha tādṛśa sambandhamapi sa paśyati bauddhadharmaḥ manuṣyasyābhyantara karṣati bauddha dharmaḥ tādṛśī mānavīyāmabhijñatā nirdiśati yatra pratyeka nara ekākitva bhavatiyatra priyatamāya mitrāyāpi na kimapi sthānamasti atraia ekākijīvanasya avibhājya sayogarahita rahasyam bauddhadharme idameva nūtanatvam nara ekākī jīvaḥekaḥ svatantraḥ astitvapravāhaḥna kopi sagaḥ tasya ekākitva dūrikartumarhati theravādo bauddhadharmaḥ sarvadā asmin viṣaye viśeṣeṇa spaṣṭa mata poṣayati manuṣya ekākī jāyateekākī vasatiekākī mriyatesa eva ekākī nivvānasya abhimukha gacchati bauddhamatānusāraḥ yo jana idamāvaśyakamekākitvamāśrayatvena na gṛhṇātisarvadā sāmājika gambhīra sagam anusaratisacetane manasi ekākitva na sthāpayatisa tathākareṇa jīvanasya molikatattvāt dūrevatiṣṭhate eko janaḥ tasya ekākitve ki karotīti bauddhasya pakṣe gurutvāpūrṇo viṣayaḥ dharmalakṣaṇakathanāya pṛṣṭaḥ san hoāiṭāheḍamahodaya ida nirdiśati ādhyātmikī unnatiḥ siddhānta karoti yatna kopi janaḥ aparasmai janāya ādhyātmikatāyā vyavasthā karotipratyeka pṛthaktayā ādhyātmikatā sādhayati aparo janaḥ asmin vyāpāre ki karoti vā na karoti vā ityanena koapi sambandho nāsti duḥkhasya ca mṛtyośca viṣaye kīdṛśosmāka viśvāsaḥ aya na īdṛśaḥ āryasatyātuṣṭayeaṣṭāgikamārge pratibandhakapañcake kīdṛśo bauddhānā viśvāsaḥ aya na īdṛśaḥ asau draṣṭu śaknoti asmāka devālayaḥ yat upadiśati tat na idam tarhi ādhyātmike unnayane ko dṛṣṭānta upadeśo vā hitakaratvena dṛśyate bauddhā yadā vadanti nara ekaḥ sāmājiko jīvaḥ  tadā tasya korthaḥ tasyārthaḥ pratyeka janaḥ aparebhyaḥ pṛthak sonekeṣu jīvaneṣu saghacālakaḥ tasya paścāt avicchinnā kāryakāraṇaparamparāsti  yatra tasya svakīya jīvana antima padamadhikaroti asyā vyākhyāyā pāścātyaḥ notsāhitaḥ ata eva asmāka sambandhastena janena saha yaḥ sañcita tathādamya karmaphalamanusṛtya sagrāma kariṣyatiyat karmaphala pūrvajīvanebhyaḥ avataratimanastattvasammatā bhitti racayati bauddhanṛtattvavidyānusārataḥasya jīvanasya aniścitatā tathā ubhayabalatā ida sākṣya vahati yat na ādhunikaiuropasya astittvavādinaḥkintu gotamo buddhaḥ pañcaviśatiśakebhyaḥ prāk nūtana pariprekṣitamunmcayati smaḥādhunikaiḥ janaiḥ yat udvega ityuyate ayameva buddhaḥna sorenakīrkegārḍaḥyo yuktyapekṣayā śaktimattaraśaktibhiścālitāyā abhijñatāyā upari prathama niviḍa pariprekṣita mānavasampradāyāya pradadau nigṛhīte satikoṇasthāpite satiniṣpeṣite sati yā abhijñatā jāyate iyameva sābhijñatāyatra śāntiḥsatyatānirudvignatā ca durlabhā eva āgalaśabdaḥ ejāyiṭi anxietyegāsṭiyā angustiaeiti lyāṭinaśabdāt jāyate tasyārthaḥ sakīrṇatā iti asyā pṛthivyā janmagrahaṇāt para vayamanayā sakīrṇatayā niṣpeṣitā bhavāmaḥ manuṣyaḥ sakīrṇā praṇālī iva  yasyā madhyataḥ atītayugajīvanasya jhaṭikā garjatipārivārika jīvana na svīkaroti udvignatāyā vihvalatāsti  sā aniścitabhūmau sthāpitā adhunā pracalitasya ejāyiṭi iti pāścātyapadasya vyavahāramadhikṛtya kati janā vivāda kartum icchanti kintu āvegatāḍitajīvasya bauddhaviśleṣaṇena ida padamatīva upayuktam ida pada tadeva ādimatama rūpa sūcayati yat anubhūtiśaktisambhāvanāpravāheṇa racite mānavavyaktitve gṛhyate pūrvavartti jīvanameva tasya yoniḥ asmābhiryanna jñāyate tena ācchannatāyāḥ bodha nirdiśati ida padam sāmājikapariprekṣitasya parisare asmāka madhye yā parasparadurbodhyatā tāmapi sūcayatīda padam kāryasādhane kā bhūmikāsmābhiḥ grahītavyākīdaśī nītiḥ atyantamupayuktākīdṛśa vā caritramasmāka gabhīra prayojana sādhayati ityādīn viṣayān na jñātvā vaya kāryasādhanāya pravṛttā bhavāmaḥ aya vādhyatābodhopi anena padena sūcyate ṭāriseliḥ yathā jalavāyuviṣayaka bhāramāviścakāratathā buddhaḥāntarajīvanasya udvegajanaka pīḍanam āviścakāra sa ādhunikānāmastitvavādinā prāk atīva gurutvapūrṇa parijñānamudghāṭayati smayena sannikṛṣṭāsahanīyabhārabodho jāyate pratyeka mānavaḥ tena bhāreṇa sandhi karoti vyaktigatadaśāyāḥ prāṇakendre jīvanasya atīva kaṣṭakaraprahelikā vartate tayā saha sagrāmāya bauddhadharmaḥ sarvasyaiva pārśve sammārjanāyaastitvavādena saha tiṣṭhati saskṛteḥ bauddha viśleṣaṇa siddhāntamāyāti yatra sampūrṇasvatantrakāraṇaiḥ phrayeḍaḥ vadati yat saskṛteḥ sādhāraṇa ādarśaḥ pratyeka vyaktisūcake manuṣye yo bādhyatāmūlakaḥ pravṛttimūlakaḥ  acetanaḥ vyavasāyaḥ tasmin mūlabaddhaḥ  kathameṣā bādhyatām  ūlakaprasaktiḥ atra bauddhamuttara prayeḍasyottarāt pṛthak yataḥ phrayeṣasya mateyena mūlabhūtena tattvena pratyeka janaḥ sagharṣa karoti tasmin tattve yaunapravṛttiḥ tiṣṭhati bauddhaḥ phrayeḍasya ida mata na svīkaroti bauddhamate maula tattva na yaunapravṛttiḥkintu rūpagatānirvacanīyākalpanīyaśaktipravāhaḥ yo pūrvavarttijanmanaḥ ānīyate vyaktigatābhijñatāyā yat maula tattva tat pūrvajanmāgata sampurṇa gupta nidhānam ida vyaktiniyantraṇātītam tathā saskṛtiniyantraṇātītamapi pratyuta ida vyaktigatavyavahārasya sāmājikavyahārasya ca mukhya nirdhārakam kevala gabhīratamadhyānena ida pariśodhita bhavitumarhati  sāmājikavyavahārasya paricchannapārivārikādarśena saha tulanāyā kṛtāyā sacetanaśaktipravāhāpekṣayā ida gabhīratara tattva katha tathā  avaśa gatamiti pratibhātam  ata eva asmai tatvāya udvegaḥ iti ādhunika nāma vyavaharāmaḥ vayamatra paśyāmo yat  katha manuṣyaḥ tasya saskṛtisajjite ādarśe jīvane bādhyatāmūlaka dṛḍhagraha pālayatikatha druta sāmājika parivartana nītigarhitamācaratikatha saskṛteḥ pratiṣṭhite ādarśe sāmājikaḥ vidrohaḥ bhavati ete ādarśāḥ tamarthahīnatvāt rakṣatīti pratibhātam tadīyābhijñatotkarṣasamṛddhaye mārgānusandhānāya ta pālayanti janānā kṛte karmakaraṇāya yā saskṛtigatādarśasāmājikabhūmikāyā ca bhāṣā upadiśyate taddvyajñānamantareṇa janā na jānanti ke te āsanniti aniścita udvegaḥ sarvadā vyaktigabhīratāyā kārya karoti sa udvegaḥ spaṣṭaḥ viśeṣīkṛterthe sandeha nikṣipati pratyeka sāmājika lakṣya mīmāsāhīna karoti tataḥ pariṇāme tallakṣyamasantoṣajanaka bhavatiekataḥteṣā samājasya nigrahaḥ anyataśca rūpa prati karmaśakteḥantarnihitaḥ bhāra  etaddvayasya madhyevasthitāḥ santaḥ janāḥ pracaṇḍodvegavanyāplāvitā dvīpā iva pratibhānti te yadyapi vādhyatāmūlakatayātathāpi svabhāvataḥ eva sāmājikādarśamukhinaḥ bhavantitatra nyūnatamataḥasthāyibhāvena tathā āśikabhāvena te mukterāsvāda prāpnuvanti bauddhānā mate idameva maulika tathā aparivartanīya tathyam saskṛtiḥ durbodhyapaśuprārthanāyāḥ uttaram ida ta vadati  kaḥ sa itiyaḥ kasmiścit sāmājike nāṭake bhūmikādānāt para vartateyadā sa mriyate kevala tadaiva nāṭakasya samāptiḥ bhaviṣyatisaskṛtiḥ mānavapaśūnā dhūrttāviṣkāramūlakopāyaviśeṣaḥ  yena te ātmaparicayamarjayanti yāvat kopi janaḥ sāmājikādarśena saha saśliṣṭaḥ tiṣṭhatiyatra tasya janma bhavatitāvat tasya manasi sandeho na jāyate  iti pratibhātam mānavapragateḥ varttamāne paryāye parivarttanasya viruddhe pratirakṣaṇaśīlatā yathā himālayaparvatamālāyāḥ kṣetre tathaivātra svābhāvikī  anena vaya boddhu samarthā bhaviṣyāmaḥ  katha saskṛtayaḥ bahūnā vaśānā sampatti sādhayitumudyatāḥ tiṣṭhanti tathā vartamānajīvanaśailyā  dāruṇa parivartana yathā na bhavati tathā bahukoṭisakhyakajanajīvanānā niyantraṇa kurvanti  īdṛśasāmājikabādhyabādhakatāyāḥ atisāmpratikanāṭakavadupanyastamatha ca vipajjanaka citra hindumusalimasagrāme viśvāya upahṛtam hindusaskṛtiḥ ca musalimasaskṛtiśca bahuśatābdīḥ vyāpya pārśvāpārśvi avatiṣṭhetekintu dvayoḥ madhye pratirakṣaṇaśīlatāyāḥ tathā śatrutāyāḥ parasparabhāvo vidyate  tame khṛṣṭābde ema e jinnāmahāśayakartṛkapākistānadeśanirmāṇākāṅkṣā saskṛtidvayasya kathoratā sūcayati asmāka hinduṣu kācidapi sahānubhūtirnāsti punaḥ punaḥ vadāmyetat vaya gā khādāmaḥhindustā pūjayati asmābhiḥ na kimapi dharmīyamasāmya svīkriyate sa jātyā vasati sosmābhiḥ saha na bhuṅkte vayamekatra na vasāmaḥ  aha tvā vadāmimusalimāḥ ekasyā jātyāmantargatāḥ eśīyopamahādeśe varṣāṇā sahasrāṇi vyāpya samākīrṇasaskṛtidvaya paraspara bādhā sṛjati smasvīyasadasyān nirāpaddūratve sthāpayati sma bhāṣā sāhityasāmājikī prathā dharmaḥ ca svātantryena viracitāḥ   manuṣyasya ca tasya saskṛteḥ madhye yatnakṛtasambandhaviṣayakaḥ bauddhaprekṣāpaṭaḥ pāścātye śāstre śaktiśālittvānusandhānāya avadāna racayati yatra adhunā mānasikavikṛtijātakāyikaviśṛkhalāyā ālocanā paryavekṣaṇasya paryāyevatiṣṭhate  asmābhistādṛśī sambhāvanā vivecanīyā yat gabhīrataramānasikarogakāraṇānā mūla tatraiva sthātumarhati yatra bauddhāḥ astāyini parivartanaśīle  jagati durdāntā tathā asusthāmāsakti paśyanti  mānavavyaktitasya gabhīrataramātrāyā sthāyitvāpekṣayā sāmājika parivartanamadhikatara svāsthyakara bhavitumarhati mānavo yadā yathārtha jīvati tadā sa sacetanaḥ komalaśca kintu maraṇakāle sa kaṭhoraḥ anamanīyaśca ata eva anamanīyatva hi mṛtyulakṣaṇamsacetanā ca jīvanasya lakṣaṇam cārlasmarismahāśayaḥ tarkayati yat mokṣasya rūpa vilopasya rūpam  adhikārasūcakatāyāḥ kasyacit rūpasya vilopaḥ jīvanasya sārabhūta vastu anamanīyeṣu viścaleṣu rūpeṣu na dṛśyatekintu pratiṣṭhitaniyamasya viphalīkaraṇeṣu sthāyistirasāmājikaniyamāya manuṣyasya ākāṅkṣā vartate atiśayena tadākāṅkṣā varṇanāyā sārvalaukika prāvaṇyamida tathya varṇayati yat tathā mārkasamahodaya āhamanuṣyaḥ tattvād vahiḥ avasthite jagati vasati eṣā sambhāvanā yāvanna gauraveṇa gṛhyate tāvat asmāka prativeśijīvānā samṛddhaye mūlyavān mānasikasvāsthyakāryakramaḥ tathā parahitaiṣivyāpāraḥ pariṇāme kevalamanyat yantra bhavitumarhati yat yantramatyāvaśyakasāmājikapraṇodanā dṛḍhīkaroti tatraiva sarvavidhānā mānasikānā tathā āvegaprasūtānā viśṛkhalānā mūla varttate abauddhodyameṣu ekam antima vaiśiṣṭyamullekhayogyamyena samājasthamanuṣyasambandhīyabodho jāyate eṣu bavavaḥ sāmājikāvasthāyāḥ eka vaiśiṣṭya nirdiśanti tathā hi ārthanītikaśaktayaḥpratiṣṭhitā dharmāḥādarśāḥ rājanītisamparkitā vyavasthāacividyāsakrāntā vyavasthā ca ete khalu vyavahārasya pradhānā nirdhārakāḥ vyaktitvasampariktasāskṛtapaścātpaṭādhyayana kadāpi vā sāmājikacaritrākāreṇa mukhyaprabhāvatvena śiśuśālā samīkṣyate bauddhamānasikatāyā eko guṇo hi eva yat eṣā mānasikatā ekasmin upādāne pradhāna nirdhāraka paśyatiyat samādheyasamasyāyām svaya na prayujyate idamucyate yat mānavavyavahāraḥ mūlataḥ kenacit sāmājikena upādānena  yathā ārthanītika jīvanam nirdhāryate uttarākāreṇa vartamānamapi praśnāśatveneda vyavahriyate iti pratibhātiyadi pāścātye sarvajanaḥ vaśānukrameṇa ida na karotiaya nirṇayaḥ sukhataro bhaviṣyati kathametāḥ sarvā mānasikatāḥ praśna prārthayante manuṣyaḥ pṛthivyāḥ vividhāsu saskṛtiṣu kārya karoti  sa kathamittham ācarati ityasya uttaratvena yadeva ekaikam upādāna gṛhyate tadeva svaya prahelikāvastu yasya samādhānam anveṣaṇaparameva bauddhapaścāt paṭa ima praśna na prārthayate tathāpi bauddhaviśleṣanasya pradhāno guṇo hi eva yat ida samāje manuṣya sambandhiprakṛtapraśnasabodhanāya samartham katha tasya abhyāsāḥ santi  aya na praśnaḥ kintu katha sa teṣā parivartanāya na svīkaroti iti praśnaḥyadyapi ida sarveṣu spaṣṭa yat vartamānajīvanaśailyām yā calamānatāsti sā tasya samagrā sabhyatāmucchetturmarhati asya praśnasya uttarabuddhaḥ tarkayatibādhyatāmūlake samparke vartate pratyeka mānavaḥ tatsamparka saskṛtau dhārayati yatra sa vasati caturthodhyāyaḥ bauddhadharme premakaruṇayoḥ prakṛtiḥ sarve sukhino bhavantu pā yaḥ  iti hṛdayānubhūtericchayā prakāśita sārabhūta vastu eva prema pada saśliṣṭopadeśāntareṇāpi viśeṣaṇa pada saśliṣṭopadeśāntareṇāpi viśeṣaṇapremipadasamparkitopadeśā  api savādeṣu vartante  prativiṣaya pṛthag gurutvamasti iti kārāṇāt pratyeka viṣayavastu aparasmādeva yatheṣṭa pṛthak ekasya viṣayamadhikṛtya yā uktayaḥ santi tāḥ sādhāraṇataḥ anyasya kṣetre na prayojyāḥ aṅgulichoṭikāviṣayakakṣudratarasavāde gotamaḥ sannyāsino vadati yatyo janoaṅgulichoṭikākālamapi karuṇāmaya citta poṣayati sa jano bhikṣuriti ucyate aṅguttaranikāya buddhaḥ punarapi vadapi  yo janoṅgulichoṭikākāla karuṇāmaya citta karṣati bhāveti athavā tat citta prati manoyoga karotisopi yathārtha bhikṣuḥ gotamo vyākhyāti yat īdṛśasya bhikṣoḥ dhyānamagnatā vṛthā na gacchati yataḥ sa upadeśānanusṛtya karma karoti tathā ca yathāyatha rājya bhuṅkte bhuñjati attaranikāya  kṣudratarachoṭikā sthānasya ṭīkā vyākhyāti yat aya savādaḥ agnijvālayā saha tulanāmadhikṛtya yaḥ savādaḥ tasya antimāśaḥ agnijvālāsavāde gotamaḥ sannyāsina upadiśati yat agnijvālāsahanam api varaki vā paraduḥkhasahana varamtathāpi strīsaṅgo na kāmanīyaḥparadravyabhogaḥ na kartavyaḥ vā parasraparidhāna vā na kartavyam paribhujñjeyyaaguttaranikāya   agninā dagdhaḥ san bhikṣuḥ kañcit kāla kaṣṭa prāpsyatiathavā kaṣṭatamāvasthāyā mariṣyati kintu sa yadi strīsage tiṣṭhati athavā strīkhādya gṛhṇātistrīvastrādīnā paridhāna karotitarhi punareva narake janma grahīṣyatitatra ca sa cira duḥkha prāpsyati evañca anyavidhaspaṣṭadṛṣṭantaiḥ gotamaḥ siddhānta jñāpayati  kena prakāreṇa bhikṣavonuśīlana kuryuḥarthāt yadi te buddhasya upadeśamanusaranti tarhi teṣā bhikṣāyāstathā paridheyasya vastunaḥ prayogo yathāyatha bhaviṣyati sa āha  bho bhikṣavaḥyuṣmābhiḥ nimnavidhopāyenābhyāsaḥ kartavyaḥ vaya pīḍitāḥ santaḥ bhikṣābhojya vastramāśrayamauṣadha ca bhuñjmahe tāni dravyāṇi ye dātāro dadati te mahat phala tathā hita labhante asmāka tyāgadharmaḥ puraskāra prāpsyati aya saphalo bhaviṣyatiaya vṛthā na yāsyati bhikṣavaḥ yuṣmābhiḥ uparyuktenopāyenābhyāsaḥ karttavyaḥ bhikṣavaḥ yūya yadi hita paśyathatarhi yūya yatnena ceṣṭadhvam yūya yadi parahita paśyathatarhi yūya yatnena ceṣṭadhvam yadi yūyamubhayahita paśyathatarhi yatnena yūya ceṣṭadhvam aguttaranikāya asminnanucchede ida spaṣṭa yat bhikṣoḥ prayojanīyadravyāṇā bhogamadhikṛtya prāgvartinī uktiḥ anucitopāya nirdiśati aya na bhogonucitatvāt indriyatṛptyartha yo bhogaḥtasmāt bhikṣuḥ narake janma labhate varam tena dātṛhitakāraka karma karaṇīyamdharmīyajīvanopayogihitasādhaka karma sampādanīyam agnijvālāsavādaḥ etāvān prabhāvavānāsīt yat yasya prabhāvāt ṣaṣṭiḥ bhikṣavaḥ raktavamana kṛtavantaḥṣaṣṭiḥ bhikṣavaḥ sannyāsa tyaktavantaḥapare ṣaṣtiḥ bhikṣavaḥ sampūrṇa muktā abhavan aguttaranikāya kṣudratarachoṭikāviṣayikī ṭīkā varṇayati yat agnijvālānuśāsanāt para buddhaḥ pakṣakāla nibhṛtavāsa cakāra yadā sa vahirāgataḥ tadā sa svalpasasthakān janānapaśyat aguttaranikāyaṭīkā manorathapūraṇī  tadīyonujaḥ sahacaraśca ānandaḥ āha yat bahubhiḥ bhikṣubhiḥ sannyāsastyaktaḥ yatastenubhavanti yat te dharmīyajīvanayāpanesamarthāḥtenubhavanti yatyadi tenucitamācaranti tarhi viśvastaiḥ dātṛbhiḥ pradattānā dravyānā bhogaḥ anucito bhaviṣyati buddho vismitaḥ sannāha tasya nibhṛtavāsakāle na kenāpi bhikṣūṇā samīpe sukhaśvāsakāraṇam assāsakāraṇavyākhyātam tadabhyāsena bhikṣavo niścayena jñāsyanti yat te dattadravyāṇā vyavahāra yathāyatha kurvanti kṣudratarachoṭikākāṭīkāyā buddha ānandamavadat yat samudragāmino yathā bahavo mārgāḥ tiṣṭhantitathā tadīye upadeśe sukhaśvāsakāraṇāni vahūnyeva santi aguttaranikāya ṭīkāmanorathapūraṇī  sa sannyāsināmāhvānāya ānandamādideśa tataḥ eka mukhabandha dadau  bho bhikṣavaḥpremṇaḥ prāthamikaḥ paryāya eva eka sukhaśvāsakāraṇam mettaya sabbapubbabhaga atra kevala jīvahitasādhanāya jīvaiḥ saha sambandhastiṣṭhati eṣā na yathārthataḥ karuṇā aguttaranikāyaṭīkā punaśca ṭīkāyāmuyate yat ālocanābinduvyākhyānāya buddhaḥ agulichoṭikāviṣayakakṣudratarākhyānasya avatāraṇā cakāra aguttaranikāyaṭīkā    eva agnijvālāyāḥ upasahāratvena kṣudratarachoṭikāsavādaḥ ta mārga nirdiśati yatra karuṇāyāḥ prāthamikaḥ paryāyaḥ hi sukhaśvāsakāraṇamiti  vyākhyātam  idamullekhya yat  yathā ṭīkāyā dṛśyate  buddhaḥ karuṇāmayacittasya paryāyatraya pratiṣṭhāpayati tathā hi   prāthamikaḥ paryāyaḥ  yatra kevala jīvahitecchā tiṣṭhati  karuṇāpraveśamukhamyatraikāgratā janma labhate tataśca  ekāgratāsthāpanā  yatra samādhiḥ sthāna labhate sādhāraṇataḥ yaugikaḥ karuṇāmayacittaśabdaḥ uktārthatrayāṇāmanyatamārtha prakāśayati kṣudratarachoṭikāsavāde prāthamikorthaḥ prakāśitaḥ  kṣudratarachoṭikākhyāne gotame vyākhyāti yadi koapi bhikṣuḥ agulichoṭikākālamapi karuṇāmaya citta poṣati tarhi sa yathārthato bhikṣuriti  ucyate  karuṇāmaya citta sacetanajīvaiḥ saha samparka sthāpayati  yatra maṅgalecchā vartate aguttaranikāya ṭīkā asya sārvalaukikaḥ paridhirasti sarve jīvāḥ sukhino bhavantu  īdṛśī icchāsmin citte jāyate kena prakāreṇa bhikṣuḥ īdṛśa citta poṣati tasya viśleṣaṇa ṭīkāyāmasti tathā hi  poṣati sa katha poṣati yadā sa cintayati tadā sa ida poṣati yadā jānātitadā sa ida poṣati yadā sa paśyatitadā ida citta sa pālayati sapratyaya siddhāntakāle sa ida pālayati śaktiprayogakāle sa ida dhārayati jñānenopalabdhau sa ida poṣayati yadā sa pratyakṣajñānena jñātaya viṣaya jānāti tadā sa karuṇāmaya citta dhārayati tyaktavyaviṣayatyāgakāle ida sa poṣayati cintanīyaviṣayacintanasamaye sa ida poṣayati tattvataḥ pratyakṣīkaraṇīyaviṣayapratyakṣīkaraṇakālepi sa ida poṣayati kiñca cittapoṣaṇavyāpāroya kevala kalyāṇakāmanayā sacetanajīvasamparkitānuraktibhāvena upalabdho bhavet ayameva premṇaḥ prāthamikaḥ paryāyaḥ eva bhikṣuḥ sarvadā dharmīyakarmaṇi karuṇāmaya manaḥ pālayatimarhati sa yadi kevalamaṅgalichoṭikākālamapi premṇastathā karuṇāyāḥ prāthamike paryāye citta pālayati tarhi sa bhikṣuriti parigaṇyate tathākaraṇena sa upadeśānusāreṇa karma karotidhyānābhyāsa karoti tathā rājyasya bhojya bhuṅkte yathāyatham aguttaranikāya sa sukhena śvāsa grahītumalam kṣudratarachoṭikāyāḥ ṭīkā ta pāṭhamupanayati yatredamivocyate yat neda bhuñjati kintu paribhuñjati aguttaranikāyaṭīkā agnijvālāyā paribhuñjati ityeka pradhāna padam kṣudrachoṭikātaḥ asya padasya sayojanena dvayoḥ savādayoḥ madhye samparke gurutvamāropitam ṭīkāyāmucyate yat agulichoṭikākālamapi karuṇāmaya citta pālayan bhikṣuḥ kena prakāreṇa rājyasya khādyadravyamapacayaśūnya bhuṅkte paribhuñjatisa paribhuñjati paribhogaḥ caturvidhāḥ steyaparibhogaḥṛṇaparibhogaḥrikthaparibhogaḥprabhutvena paribhogaśceti asmin viṣayeduṣṭācaraṇayukto bhikṣuryadā dāna bhuṅktetadā steyaparibhoga ucyate yadā sadācārayukto bhikṣuḥ niścinta ṛṇakṛta dāna bhuṅktetadā ṛṇaparibhoga ucyate yadā śikṣārthinā sapta saghāḥ dāna bhuñjatetadā rikthaparibhogo bhavati yadi bhikṣuḥ hānikara prabhāva vinaśya dāna bhuṅktetadā prabhutvena paribhoga ucyate asmin viṣayebhikṣuḥ kṣudratarachoṭikāyā varṇitaḥapacayaśūnya rājyasya bhojya bhuṅkte tatra kāraṇadvayamastiprathamataḥyo bhikṣuḥ kevala agulichoṭikākāla karuṇā poṣayatisa prabhutvenaṛṇamuktatvenarikthabhāgitvena rājyasya bhojya bhuṅkte idameva kāraṇa yat sopacaya vinā rājyasya khādya bhuṅkte dvitīyataḥagulichoṭikākālamapi kāruṇikāya bhikṣave dānasya mahatī śaktirasti īdṛśāya bhikṣave yo dātā upahāra yacchati sa tasmādupahārāt mahat phalammahat hitammahat gaurava ca labhate idameva dvitīya kāraṇa yasmāt bhikṣuḥ apacaya na kṛtvā rājyasya bhojya bhuṅkte aguttaranikāya ṭīkā tulanā  visuddhimaggayo bhikṣuḥ kṣaṇamapi prāthamikaparyāyabhuktapremakaruṇāyukta hṛdaya pālayati sa ta dharmamarjayati yo dharmastādṛśena bhikṣuṇā arjyate sayaḥ dānaprakṛti cintayatiyaḥ saptaśikṣārthināmanyatamaḥ bhavatiyena vā hānikarāḥ sarve prabhāvā vinaṣṭāḥ sa eva ekorhaḥ saptavargīyāḥ śikṣārthinaḥ panthāna pratyakṣīkurvantiathavā srotaḥpraveśinaḥsakṛdāgāminaḥanāgāminaḥarhataśca phalamabhijānanti  premamayacittānuśīlanakāribhikṣusasparśa yaḥ poṣaka āyāti sa tadbhikṣoḥ yānācārādibhiḥ anuprāṇito bhavati ida hitāvahamanupreraṇa bhaviṣyati ānandadāyakāya puraskārāya mūlam pṛṣṭha  ṭīkā ida poṣakeṇa paravartidharmasyācaraṇāya bījatvena sevitumapi alam kāruṇikacittapālakaḥ abhyāsakārī dharmīyajīvanasyotkṛṣṭaḥ dṛṣṭāntaḥ sa eva yathārtha nirapacaya bhikṣā bhuṅkte nimagnatāparyāyabhuktapremayuktacittameva viśeṣeṇa kāruṇikacittapadena gamyate tathā hi  kramikavacaneṣubuddhaḥ phalaprasūdharmācaraṇakāriṣu pradhāna gṛhasthamanāthapiṇḍakamupadiśati  aguttaranikāya bahubhyo janebhyo bhikṣāyā dānamsamagdṛṣṭimato janasya poṣāṇam srotaḥpraveśīaguttaranikāya ṭīkā  api ca tat poṣaṇa bhaviṣyati sakṛdāgāmibhikṣaveanāgāmibhikṣavearhadbhikṣavejñānonmukhāya buddhāyasamyag jñāninebuddhapradhānāya bhikṣusaghāyabauddhāśramanirmāṇambuddhe dharme saghe ca āśrayagrahaṇamācāryapañcakaparyavekṣaṇamkṣaṇakāla kāruṇikacittakarṣaṇamanityatāpratyakṣīkaraṇam pradhānakāryāvalī kāruṇikacittacarcāyā āpekṣikatva gurutva pradarśayati kintu eṣā carcā muktyunmukhāntardṛṣṭicarcāyā nimne eva vartate kāruṇikacittamiti samastapadasya vyākhyāyā ṭīkāha  hitasādhaneccasametasacetajīvasamparkita cittameva kāruṇika cittam punaśca ida yathārthataḥ samādhiyogena antarbhukto bhavati  aguttaranikāya ṭīkā  evamatra kāruṇikacittam samādhiparyāyabhukta sarvathāpi premakaruṇānvita tiṣṭhati krakacadṛṣṭāntasavāde gotamaḥ bhikṣu moliyaphaggunamupadiśati yat sa kupitacittapoṣaṇa na kṛtvā kāruṇika citta pālayet majjhimanikāya moliyaphaggunaḥ sannyāsinībhiḥ saha atyanta sasaktaḥ savṛttaḥ tasmāt kopi yadi sannyāsinīnā doṣamullikhatitarhi sotīva kruddho jātaḥ evañca sannyāsinīnā pratikiyāsītyadi kopi tasyācaraṇe doṣa paśyati tacchrutvā buddhaḥ moliyamāhvayati sma sa tamāha yat sannyāsinīṣu atyāsaktiḥ sannyāsinā pakṣe anucittā ata eva yadi kopi janaḥ sannyāsinīnā vyavahāreṣu doṣa paśyatitadā sa īdṛśa manobhāva poṣayet  mama citta viṣayagāmi na bhavatu aha kuvākya na vadiṣyāmi aha sarvebhyo hitāya sahānubhūti poṣayiṣyāmi mama citta kāruṇika sat sarvadā kopamukta bhaviṣyati iti majjhimanikāya buddho moliyamupadiśati yat sa samamanobhāva poṣayet yadi kopi tadīya doṣa paśyatiathavā kopi ta vā sannyāsinīḥ vā āhanti gotamo bhikṣūnupadiśati  na kevala parakṛtaguṇadoṣavivecanamukheapi tu parasambandhiguṇadoṣavivecanakāle sarvadā kāruṇika citta lālayet savādeṣu buddho gotamo vyākhyāti yat yadi kopi aparasya doṣa saśodhayitumicchatitarhi sa yathākālamida kuryāt tadā sa kāruṇikena hṛdayena satya vadetśānta vadetlābhajanakatayā kārya kuryāt dīghanikāya katha vā parasparam salapet iti upadiśya punaśca sa sayojayāmāsa yat sarve bhikṣavaḥ sarvadā sarvaiḥ saha śānta vyavahareyuḥ madhyamamānavacaneṣu gotama upadiśati yat kopi janaḥ jātivicāra na kṛtvā premamaya hṛdaya karṣet majjhimanikāya ayamabhyāso na kevala sarveṣā karttavyopi tu ādhyātmikamārgaparisamāptaye upayogitā vrajati kassapa prati sihagarjana  savāde gotamo varṇayati yo bhikṣuḥ kāruṇika citta pālayatisarvān kṣatikarān prabhāvān vinaśyati āsava sa yathāyogya parivrājakaḥ samaṇaucyate athavā brāhmaṇa ucyate dīghanikāya atra gotamo dharmīyamādarśa varṇayatitenādarśena vyaktipakṣe prayojanamasti yadi vyaktiḥ parivrājako vā brāhmaṇo vā bhavitumicchati majjhimanikāyaṭīkāpapañcasudanī vaktṛtāmālāyā kṣātikarāṇā viṣayāṇā sūcī āsava asti tatra kṣatikarā viṣayā nāma ākāṅkṣāpunarjanmaavidyādṛṣṭābhimatam ca te viṣayāḥ ṭīkāsu eva vyākhyātāḥ tathā hi  indriyatṛṣṇāpunarjanmākāṅkṣāajñatābhrāntamata ca visuddhimagga te viṣayāḥ kevalam arhadbhiḥ sampūrṇa parityaktāḥ pārthivapariveśasya prakṛtiḥ anityā sā prakṛtiḥ arhatā tṛpti na vidadhāti te sūkṣmabhāvena prakṛti yathākrama paśyanti tathā ca te nirvāṇasya svādamanubhavanti phalataḥ te na punaḥ pārthivendriyasukhenākṛṣṭā bhavanti evamanityasukha vā punarjanmano duḥkha vā tān prabhāvitān karttu na śaknoti īdṛśaiḥ janaiḥ sarvavidha mānasika tamastathā bhrānta mata dūrīkṛtam tataḥ arhatpadasya samaparyāyaśabdaḥ khalu khinasavaḥ arthāt yena kṣatikaraprabhāvo vinaṣṭa iti punaśca yadi īdṛśo janaḥ premamaya hṛdaya karṣatitarhi sa yathārthataḥ parivrājakaḥ brāhmaṇo vā bhavitumarhati kramikavacaneṣu buddha āha bhikṣūn prati sukarmasādhanāt bhītiḥ na karaṇīyāyataḥ sukarmapada prakṛtyā sukhaparyāyam aguttaranikāya sa svakīya jñānamullikhati yat tena cira yat sukarma kṛta tat ānandāya sampadyate tasyaphala caivam  sa prāktane janmani saptaparṣaiḥ kāruṇika citta pālayāmāsa tasmāt sa ānandamayasukhasamūha bhuṅkte sārvalaukike prakāśe ca vikāśe ca sapta yugāni vyāpya sosyā pṛthivyā na punarjātaḥ sārvalaukikaprakāśakāle sa divye jagati janmagrahaṇa cakāra ābhassara punaśca vikāśakāle sa divyabrāhmaprāsāde punarjanmagrahaṇamakarot yatra sa mahābrahmarūpeṇa rājatva cakāra sa āsīt sakkaḥākāṅkṣājagataḥ prabhuḥṣaṭtriśatkṛttvaḥsa bahuvāra sārvalaukikaḥ samrāṭ san yathādharma śāsana cakāra tadā sa kāruṇika citta karṣati smayena sa suphala prāpnoti sma tasya premamaya citta samādhimārgasthaprāthamikaparyāyabhuktamāsīt anyasmin savāde bodhisattvasya kāruṇika tathā premamaya cittamullekhārhatā vrajati bhayātañkaviṣayake savāde āraṇyajīvanesṛṣṭa sakaṭamadhikṛtya vipraḥ jāṇussoṇiḥ gotama pṛcchatimajjhimanikāya   buddhaḥ jāṇussoṇi nivedayati yat vanavāsinā teṣā parivrājakānā brāhmaṇānā citta krodhānvita mālinyayukta cāsīt tasmātte bhayenātakena ca ākrāntā bhavanti majjhimanikāya sa jāṇussoṇi vyākhyāti yat ekadā sa svaya bodhisattva āsīt tadā buddhatvaśikṣaṇakāle soraṇyevasatkintu tasya hṛdaye krodhaḥ nāsīttat hṛdaya premamayamāsīt kāruṇika citta pratyakṣīkṛtya bodhisattvaḥ kadāpi dvidhāgrastaḥ na babhūvana vā bhītaḥ na vā ātaṅkitaḥ ṭīkāyāḥ sayojanamevam  mama citta krodhapūrṇa nāsīt asyāyamāśayahḥ mamaika karuṇāmaya hṛdayamāsīt tasmin hṛdaye hitecchā āsīt  bodhisattvaḥ tādṛśaḥ āsīt majjhimanikāyaṭīkāpapañcasudanī tataḥ para gotamosmin savāde tasya samyag jñāna varṇayatiidamanumāna yukta bhavet yat araṇye bodhisattvasya jīanamadhikṛttya eṣālocanā gotamakartṛkabodhilābhāt pūrvameva yaḥ kālasta nirdiśati katipayeṣu savādeṣu śiṣyāḥ premamayakāyikavācikamānasikakarmaṇāmanuśīlana kurvantīti dṛśyate athavā te tathā karttumapadiśyante iti dṛśyate kaścit śiṣya eteṣāmunnataye anuprāṇitobhavat yataḥ tasyāsti kāruṇika cittam dīghanikāyaṭīkā  yathā pūrva pradarśitamtat citta prāthamikaparyāyabhuktapremayuktamathavā samādhiparyāyabhuktapremayukta bhavitumarhati ṭīkāyā mate ubhayavidha citta premamayakarmasampādanāya samartha tiṣṭhati etā ālocanāḥ sahānubhavānupreratakāryāṇāmupari ālokasampāta kurvantiyatra sahānubhave prāthamikaparyāyagatapremakaruṇālakṣaṇa parisphuṭam bhavacakrāt mahāparimuktimadhikṛtya savāde dṛśyate yat guroḥ gotamād vicchedamāsannam dṛṣṭvā ānandaḥ roditumārebhe dīghanikāya tadā gotama ānanda smārayati yat tasyaiva upadeśa evam  sarvāṇi sukhakarāṇi vastūni parivartante tirobhavanti ca buddhaḥ ānanda sāntvayati tadīyapremamayasevā praśasya  ānandatayā cireṇa sadaikyavataḥ sevā kriyate  premayakāyikakarmabhiḥpremamayavācikakarmabhiḥpremamayamānasikakarmabhiśca tāni karmāṇi hitakarāṇisukhāvahāniadvaitāniparimāṇaśūnyāni ca dīghanikāya  ṭīkayā viśleṣaṇamevam  premamayakāyikakarmabhiḥ ityatra  kāyikakarmāṇiyathāupahāradānamukhaprakṣālanādīniyāni premamayahṛdayānupreritāni hitakarāṇi  ityatra tāni karmāṇi ucyante yāni magalavardhanāya kriyante sukhāvahāni  ityatrāśayaḥ  karmāṇi sukhena ca harṣeṇa ca kriyantena duḥkhena vā kaṣṭena vā advaitāni  aya bhāvaḥ  kati janāḥ kevalamapareṣā samakṣana teṣā parokṣampremamayakāyikakarmādīni sampādayanti anye ca kevalamanyeṣā parokṣana teṣā samakṣakāryāṇi sampādayanti kintu sa ānanda eva na vibhajya premamayakarmāṇi sampādayati sma evañca tat kṛtāni premamayakāyikakāryāṇi advaitāni savṛttāni parimāṇaśūnyāni  asyārthaḥ  parimāṇa vinā sa vivakṣati  tava premamayakāyikakāryāṇi parimāṇena atyanta pracurāṇi kintu ida jagat atīva sakīrṇamsattāyāḥ cūḍāpi atihrasvā kṣudre sāttvike jagati pracurāṇā karmaṇā sthānābhāvatvāt karmāṇi parimāṇaśūnyāni iti kathyate premamayavācikakarmāṇi  atra vācikakarmāṇi ityatra mukhaprakṣālanasamayaghoṣaṇādikarmāṇi sūcyante tāni ca kāruṇikacittānupreṣitāni bhavanti kiñca yadi kopi upadeśavāṇī śrutvā vadatimahāśayasādhūkta tvayā iti pramemayavāicikakarmaṇa udāharaṇam  premamayamānasikakarmāṇi ityatrāśayaḥ  yathāsamaya śarīrasya yatna kṛtvā sa nibhṛte sthāne upaviśya eva prakāreṇa cintayati  mamācāryaḥ  rogāt kleśācca mukto bhavatu sa sukhī bhavatu iti dīghanikāyaṭīkāsumaṅgalavilāsinī savādeṣu idamapi likhita yat bhikṣavaḥ teṣā sveṣā madhye premamayakāyikavācikamānasikakarmaṇāmanuśīlana cakruḥ gosigaviṣayakakṣudratarasavāde gotamaḥ anuruddhanandiya kimbila ca sannyāsinaḥdraṣṭu yayau te bhikṣavaḥ gosigasthe udyāne tasthuḥ majjhimanikāya  buddhaḥ sannyāsinaḥ pṛcchati  paryāpta bhikṣābhojya prāpya dugdhajalamiśraṇavadekatra sukhena sthitvā ki te kuśalina iti na vā te uttara dadati yat te nāma kuśalinaḥ teṣāñca paryāpta bhikṣābhojyamasti anuruddhasya netṛtve te pṛthak pṛthak buddha vadanti yat te dugdhajalamiśravaṇavat sukhena vasanti teṣā mate īdṛśaiḥ satīrthaiḥ bhikṣubhiḥ saha vāsaḥ mahān lābha eva te parasparahitārtha premamayakāyikavācikamānasikakarmāṇi kurvanti teṣā samakṣa ca parokṣam ca anuruddhaḥ anyān janān prati tadīyā bhakti varṇayati  aha nimnarūpa cintayāmi  mayā kimīdṛśānām mitrāṇā  sevārtha mama svīya cittamutsṛṣṭam  kiñca ki me jīvana teṣā sevārthamiti mahāśayaḥ asmāka śarīrāṇi khalu pṛthak pṛthak tiṣṭhantitathāpi asmāka cittāni niścayena ekatvāpannāni  majjhimanikāya  anuruddhasya premamayakāyikavācikamānasikakarmaṇā varṇana vistareṇa kathayati ṭīkā  premamayakāyikakarmāṇi  ityatra kāyikakarmāṇi kāruṇikacittatvāt apareṣā jñāne vā ajñāne vāpratyakṣa vā parokṣa vā asmin prasamgeapareṣā samakṣa kāyikavācikakarmāṇi tadaiva sambhavanti yadā kopi janaḥ aparaiḥ saha vasati vaiparītya sambhavati yadi janāḥ pṛthak pṛthak vasanti sarvāsu avasthāsu mānasikakarma sambhavati tathā hi  anuruddhaḥ paśyati  dau bhikṣū tena saha vasataḥ tayoḥ anyataraḥ vahiḥ viśṛkhala parityajyāyāti sa cintanena virakti na prakāśayati  keneda vyavahṛtam  iti varam sa tāni vastūni samuddhṛtya yathāsthāna sthāpayatiyathā svaya sa tyajati samuddharati ca athavā viṣāyasya upari yatna gṛhṇāti etānyeva pareṣā samakṣa premamayakāyikakarmāṇi ucyante tathā hi  kopi bhikṣuḥ vahirgacchatitasya śayyāviṣṭara prayojanīya dravya ca vahiḥ tyajati yathānuruddhena purva vyavasthāpitamtathaiva yadi sa karoti tarhi tasya premamayakāyikakāryāvalī pareṣā parokṣa bhavet yadānuruddhaḥ aparagurujanadvayena saha vasatitaddvayena saha madhura sukhakara ca ālapatitadā tat karma pareṣā samakṣa premamayavācikakarmeti ucyate sa yadi taddvaya mitratāsulabhāya saujanyamūlakāya vā ālāpāya niyojayatitarhi api premamaya vācika karma bhavet kiñca sa taddvaya praśna pṛcchatiathavā tayoḥ uttara dadāti  evavidha karmāpi vācika karmetyucyate kiñca yadā dvau gurujanau anyatra gacchataḥ tayoḥ anupasthitau sa tayoh guṇān praśasati  mama priyau bāndhavauvayovṛddhau nandiyaḥ kimbilaśca eva eva prakāreṇa sadācāraiḥ yuktau tau eva evamabhyāsa kurutaḥ iti eva vidha karma pareṣā parokṣa premamayavācikakarmeti ucyate premamayamānasikakarma tadaiva sambhavati yadā pareṣāmupasthitau vānupasthitau vā sa cintayati mama priyau bāndhavau vayuvṛddhau nandiyaḥ kimbilacca śatrutāyā jaṭilatāyāśca muktau bhavatām tau sukhinau bhavatām iti mahāśaya asmāka śarīrāṇi khalu pārthakya bhajanti yataḥ śarīrāṇi godhūmacūrṇavad vā mṛttikāvadvā cūrṇībhavanti tāni kadāpi ekata na bhajanti tathāpi asmāka cittāni niścayena ekatva bhajanti ayamāśayaḥ  yadā vayamekatra sānnidhya bhajāmaḥkadāpi pṛthak pṛthak na tiṣṭhāmaḥkadāpi vivāda na kurmaḥsarvadā aikamatya poṣayāmaḥ tadā asmāka cittāni ekatva bhajanti arthāt cittaikya jāyate katha te ātmanā cittāni tyaktvā pareṣā sevāyai niyojayanti tathā hi  kasyacit doṣayukta pātramasti kasyacidasti malina vastram kasyāpi cāsti saskaraṇīya karma asyāmavasthāyā doṣayuktapātravān kathayati bandhavaḥmama pātra doṣayukta ida pakva karaṇīyam iti kintu anye na vadanti mama prakṣālanayogya vastramasti iti athavā asti me teṣā vastrāṇi prakṣālayantipareṣā saskārakarma ca kurvanti anyeṣu ekatamenāpi prathamaghoṣaṇāyā sadṛśī sahayogitā sambhavativāndhavamama vastrāṇi malinānitāni prakṣālanīyāni iti athavā mamoṭaja bhagnadaśā vrajati tasya saskāraḥ karttavya iti majjhimanikāyaṭīkāpapañcasudanī siṅgāla prati upadeśe gotamaḥ gṛhastha siṅgālamupadiśati  premamayaśārīrikavācikamānasikakarmabhiḥ parivrājakān brāhmaṇān ca sevasvateṣā kṛte dvāramunmukta kurujīvanadhāraṇāya ca dravya dehīti parivrājakā api sahānubhavānuprāṇitāḥ santaḥ pratyupakāra sādhayiṣyanti  ṭīkāyāmucyate vistareṇa  premamayakāyikakarmabhiḥ  ityatra kāyikakarmasu kṛteṣu vyaktiḥ yadi premamaya hṛdaya sṛjati tarhi tāni karmāṇi  premamayānīti  yadā kopi sasārī eva cintayan bauddhamandira gacchatiaham bhikṣubhiḥ saha ālapāmīti tatra ca gatā jalapātra nītvā jala siñcatibhikṣūṇā pada vā pṛṣṭa vā savāhayati  ityādīni karmāṇi premamayakāyikakarmāṇītyucyate yadā kopi sasārī paśyati  bhikṣavo bhikṣārtha grāma praviśantītisa ca vadati śraddhayā tebhyaḥ anna vā dugdha vā bhojya vā dehītitadā eva vidhāni karmāṇi premamayavācikakarmāṇītyucyate kiñca yadā sa śraddhayāntarikatayā ca dharma śṛṇotivadati ca sādhūkta tvayā tadā evavidhāni karmāṇi premamayavācikakarmāṇiti kathyate yadā kaścit gṛhasthaḥ cintayatiasmāka sasāram āśritya ye gurujanāstiṣṭhanti te śatrutvāt tathā utpātāt muktā bhavantu tadā evavidha vacana kāruṇikahṛdayaprasūtakarma ucyate dīghanikāyaṭīkā bhavacakrān mahāparinirvāṇasavāde gotamaḥ bhikṣumupadiśati  ṣaṭ avasthāḥ santi  yābhiḥ lābho jāyate dīghanikāya tathā hi  pareṣā samakṣā vā parokṣa vā satīrthebhyaḥ bhikṣubhyaḥ prītiyukktakāyikavācikamānasikakarmasampādanamsatīrtheṣu bhikṣuṣu bhikṣālabdha dravya vibhajya grahaṇamsadācāraiḥ vyavahāraḥekāntataḥ duḥkhavināśāya matapoṣaṇam buddha āha  yāvatte uktadaśāṣṭaka pālayantitāvanniścita te unnataye kalpante ṭīkāyā vyākhyāyate  prītisnigdhakāyikakarmāṇi tānyeva yāni kāruṇikena hṛdayena kriyante evameva karuṇābhayamanaḥsādhya vācika karma premamayamiti kathyate karuṇāmaya manaḥsādhya mānasika karma premamayamityucyate asmin pāṭhe īdṛśī karmasamaṣṭiḥ sannyāsinā kṛte nirdiśyate tathāpi gṛhasthopi tādṛśa karma kartumarhati karuṇāmayahṛdayenānupreritāḥ santaḥ sannyāsinaḥ yadā sadācāra sādhayanti tadā tat karma prītisnigdhakāyikakarmetyucyate yadā gṛhasthā janāḥ śraddhāpradarśanārtha avaśiṣṭādhāra gacchantiathavā bodhivṛkṣa gacchantidharmasampradāya nimantrayitu yāntibhikṣārtha grāmamāgacchanta bhikṣumālokya ta draṣṭu gacchantiteṣā bhikṣāpātra gṛṇhantiupaveśanārtha tān anurundhantitaiḥ saha gacchantitadā evavidhāni karmāṇi prītisnigdhakāyikakarmāṇītyucyate yadā sannyāsinaḥ kāruṇikacittānupreritāḥ santaḥ sada cāramupadiśantidhyānaviṣaya vyākhyayā vadantidharmamupadiśantitadā etāni karmaṇi prītisnigdhavācikakarmāṇi ityucyate kiñca bauddhadharmaśāstra tripiṭaka nāma tatra buddhasya śabdāḥ santi praśnottararūpāḥ ida śāstra premamayavācika karma gṛsthānā prītisnigdhāvācikakarmāṇi tadaiva bhavanti yadā vadantivaya śraddhāpradarśanārthamaviśiṣṭādhāra gacchāmaḥ  vaya pūjārtha bodhivṛkṣa gacchamaḥ vaya śravaṇīyadharma śrotumavasara racayāmaḥ dīpaiḥ mālyaiḥ puṣpaiśca pūjā karavāma  vaya sadabhyāsatraya nirvāhayāmaḥ  sadācāraḥ samādhiḥ jñātam vaya yathocitakhādyādi vitarāmaḥ  varṣartau nibhṛtavāsarātāya bhikṣave upāyana yacchāmaḥ  adya ādhyātmikasampradāyavyavahṛta dravyacatuṣṭaya paridhānabhikṣāpātra śayyāauṣadha ca yacchāmaḥ  ādhyātmikasampradāya nimantrayāmaḥ teṣā kṛte ca kaṭhina bhojya sādhayāmaḥ  upaveśanārtha tān āsana darśaya  tebhyaḥ jala dehi gacchabhikṣūn paśyataiḥ saha anugaccha  upayukte viṣṭare upaveśanāya tān sāhāyya kuru  yathotsāha yathāśakti ca tān sevasva  evamanyatrāpi budhyate yadā bhikṣavaḥ pratyūṣe utthāya dehasādhanānte avaśiṣṭādhārasamīpa prakṣānārtha yāntiprathāgatakṛtyāni samyādayantiviviktasthāne upaviśya cintayanti  bauddhamandirasya sannyāsinaḥ sukhinaḥ bhavantu te śatrutāyāstathā jaṭilatāyāśca muktā bhavantu  ityevavidha teṣā karuṇāmayamānasikakarma yadā gṛhasthāścintayantimahānto janāḥ sukhino bhavantu te vairāt upadravācca muktā bhavantu tadā ityeva teṣā karuṇātmakamānasikakarma yadā bhikṣavaḥ paridheyavasanādinirmāṇāya navadīkṣitān sāhāyya kartu gacchantitadā tat karma pareṣāmupasthitau prītisnigdhaśārīrikakarmeti ucyate api ca gurujanapādaprakṣālana śraddhayā abhyarthanājñāpanamityādīni karmāṇi pareṣā samakṣa prītisnigdhadaihikakarmāṇi ityucyate yadā dīkṣiteṣu navīnā vā prācīnā vā dārumayadravyādīni vahiḥ viśṛkhala parityajya anyatra gacchantitadā kaścidbhikṣuḥ tāni dravyāṇi suśṛkhala sthāpayati viraktiprakāśa na kṛtvaiva sa manyate yat ukta karma tasya svasyeva karma evavidha karma apareṣāmanupasthitau premamayakāyikakarmetyucyate  agraja devaagraja tissa ete śraddhāsūcakāḥ śabdāḥ pareṣā samakṣa premamayavācikakarmaṇā dyotakāḥ bauddhamandire agrajadevasya agrajatissasyānupasthitau kopi bhikṣuryadi eva vadati  asmākamagrajaḥ devaḥ kutra gataḥkutra gataḥ vā agrajaḥ tissaḥ kadā tau pratyāgamiṣyataḥ  tadā eṣā uktiḥ pareṣā parokṣa kāruṇikavācikakarmeti ucyate vaya yadā prītisnigdhaiḥ locanaiḥ aparān drakṣyāmaḥtadā tat karma pareṣāmupasthitau premamayamānasikakarma yadi cintyate agrajaḥ devaḥ agrajaḥ tissaḥ ca pīḍāyāḥ ca asvāsthyāt ca muktau bhavatām  tarhi etādṛśa cintana pareṣāmupasthitau premamayakarmeti ucyate dīghanikāyaṭīkā iya ṭīkā varṇayati  kāruṇikacittānupreritāḥ santaḥ bhikṣavaḥ yadā yathāyathamācaranti tadā tat karma premamayakāyikakarmetyucyate iti kāruṇyasaujanyayoḥ miśraṇamullekhārham theravādīvyākhyānādidamāyāti yat maṅgalamaye manasi vicitraviṣayāṇāmadbhuta miśraṇa jāyate hitasādhaka kāruṇika manaḥ katibhiḥ mānasikaiḥ guṇaiḥ anvita tiṣṭhati tathā hi  pratyayaḥmanasvitāvivekaḥlajjānirlobhatāsamatāśāntacittatālaghutānamanīyatādakṣatāabhijñatāsaralonmukhitā ca  yathāyathamācaraṇāyānupreraṇāśaktitvena vivecanā lajjā ca hitasādhakacitteṣu vartete ityucyate vivecanā ca lajjā ca snāyavika doṣa na sūcayataḥ kintu upayuktavyavahārapravarttakaguṇān sūcayataḥ tatra yathākrama vyavahartuḥ svīyaruciḥ athavā pareṣā ruciḥ kārya karoti visuddhimagga snāyavikadoṣakaraṇādvātmavidveṣādvādūre vartamānaḥ śuddhasaujanyabodhaḥ tayoranupasthiteḥ upari nirbhara karoti yadā kaścijjana ātmavidveṣa poṣayati athavā pāpavyākulatāmanubhavatitadā sa vivekena lajjayā vā śūnyaḥ jāyate visuddhimagga  yataḥ asmin samaye sa svapakṣe parapakṣe vā yathāyatha hitakara kārya na karoti yataḥ upayuktanītisammatavyavahāraḥ ātmavidveṣādidoṣebhyo muktena saujanyabodhena pravartito bhavatitataḥ nītisammata jñāna tathācaraṇa prakṣobhajakleśamantareṇa sambhavati  mānasika sāmya namanīyatva laghutvamātmavidveṣādiduṣṭabhāvapariharaṇameteṣā prasage āgativinayamavalambya kaścijjanaḥ viśuddhavyavahāra  kartu śikṣate  vyavahāre kasyacinnarasya bhrame lakṣite bhramasvīkaraṇena ca viśuddhīkaraṇecchayā ca pratikāro vidhīyatena snāyavikapīḍanena asmin prasagevivekaśca lajjā ca aparahitasādhakamānasikaguṇaiḥ saha virodha na bhajataḥ teṣu guṇeṣu karuṇāpi vartate karuṇayā saha sarve ete guṇāḥ viśuddhavyavahāreṇa saha virājante kintu tatra bindumātraḥ kopopi na tiṣṭhatina pāpamna vā amanamanīyatā karuṇā vivecanālajjā ca mānasikasukhabodhāya samamanobhāvāya vā sampadyante visuddhimagga evañca sadācāraḥ karuṇayā ānandena ca saha virājate savādeṣu karuṇāmayakāryāvalī samaṣṭigatabhāvena kevala dharmācaraṇakāriṇā kṛte ālocyate tatra buddhaḥ ānandaḥ anuruddhaḥ kimbilaḥ nandiyaḥ ityādīnā parasparasavādosti tatra karuṇāsamṛddhakarmasampādanāya sannyāsinaḥ prati buddhasyopadeśo vartate yataḥ etādṛśa karma teṣāmunnataye bhavati kāruṇikakarmabhiḥ parivrājakānā ca viprāṇā ca sevārtha sigala prati tasyopadeśosti atra hetuḥ  parivrājakāśca viprāśca sahānubhūtiśīlāḥ santaḥ tameva upakariṣyanti savādeṣu ālocitānā karuṇāsiktakarmaṇā pradhānāḥ kartāraḥ hi bhikṣavaḥ tathāpi idamapi avaśyameva gamyate yat sādhāraṇā janā api bhikṣūṇā viśuddha vyavahāra tathā upadeśa gṛhītvā upakṛtā bhaviṣyantibhikṣūn prati kāruṇikakarmopadeśānā kaściddoṣaḥ api dṛśyate tathā hi  te sādhāraṇajanebhyaḥ kāruṇikakarmalābhāya pralubdhā bhavitumarhanti atra buddhasya kaṭhora vidhānamasti yat bhikṣavaḥ yathāyatha bhikṣālabdha dravya bhuñjīran ye kāruṇikakarmāṇi labhantete avaśyameva sukha prāpnuvanti ata ea hitakarakāruṇikacittena anuprāṇitāḥ santaḥ janāḥ pramamayakāyikavācikamānasikakarmāṇi kartu pravattante etāni karmāṇi sampādayantaḥ abyāsakāriṇaḥ tasmin kṣaṇe eva cittānuṣaṅga sukhamanubhavanti kramikānuśāsaneṣu praśasanīyaphalaṣaṭka varṇita buddhena yat sarvavidhasāpekṣavyāpāreṣu sannyāsisamīpe duḥkhabodhanivṛttaye bhavati aguttaranikāya tathā hi   nirvāṇopalabdhiḥ sarvavidhasāpekṣavyāpāreṣu sthāpitā bhaviṣyati  manaḥ sarvadeśād vimukha bhaviṣyati  sannyāsī nirvāṇarūpā śānti drakṣyati  mālinya tathā punarjanma iti sahajātā pravaṇatā dūra gabhiṣyati  sannyāsinaḥ sarvakarmaṇā samāptiḥ bhavati  sannyāsī kāruṇikakarmaṇā guru sevitu śakṣyati śabdāntaramavalambyocyatesarvavidhasāpekṣavyāpāreṣu duḥkhabodhajāgaraṇāt sannyāsī yathā arhatpuruṣo bhaviturmahati tasya lābhāḥ jāyante karuṇāayakarma ityasya viśleṣaṇa karoti ṭīkā  karuṇāmayakarmabhiḥ karuṇānvitasevābhiḥyasmāt saptavidhā śikṣārthinaḥ karuṇāmayakarmabhiḥ sadaikyavanta sevante yena bhikṣuṇā hānikarāḥ prabhāvā vinaṣṭāḥ sa sampūrṇakāruṇikakarmabhiḥ ācārya sevate  aguttaranikāyaṭīkā śikṣārthinaḥ vā aparejanā vā mārgābhijñatā labhante tathā ca srotaḥpraveśinaḥ sakṛdagāminaḥ anāgāminaḥ anāgāminaḥ arjjanasya mārgasya viṣayamadhikṛtya jñānamarjayantitathāpi te sampūrṇa karuṇāmayakarmabhiḥ guru na sevante kintu sampūrṇo muktaḥ puruṣaḥ arhajjanasya sukhāsvāda prāpya guru karuṇāmayakarmabhi sevate sarvavidhasāpekṣavyāpāreṣu duḥkhātmakaprakṛtiḥ asti tadviṣayakasampūrṇabodhāt sa punaḥ punaḥ punarjanmane ākāṅkṣā dūrīkaroti sa sāpekṣavyāpārāṇāmanityatva cāsāratva ca upalabhate tasmāt sa punareva kutrāpi āsakti na darśayati athavā tatra ghṛṇāmapi na prakāśayati sa sarvavidhakṣyatikaraprabhāvānā vināśakaroti ete prabhāvāḥ etāvatkāla tasya citte āsan kintu teṣā nāśāt sa sampūrṇa nirvāṇasukhamanubhavati sa karuṇāmayakarmabhiḥ guru sevitumalapityucyate evamatra karuṇāmayakarma antardṛṣṭi nirdiśatiyā mānasikadūṣaṇāt nara cita mukta karoti  tathā ca kṣudratarachoṭikāviṣayikī ṭīkā vadati  yadā sannyāsī pratyakṣajñānagamya viṣaya pratyakṣa jānāti tadā sa premamaya manaḥ poṣayati  yadyapīda gabhirāntardṛṣṭidvārā  nirvāṇopalabdhidvārā prema sṛjati tathāpi sāmānyārthayuktā karuṇā asmin prasage na āyāti  dhammapālena  tadīyaṭīkāyā viśuddhimārga vyākhyāsu viśadārtha prakaṭitaḥ   premakaruṇādayaḥ ye mānasikaguṇā indriyavadbhiḥ prāṇibhiḥ saha sambandha sthāpayanti te viṣayatvena na āyānti yadā dhyāninaḥ manaḥ nirvāṇa  labhate   kramikānuśāsanebhyaḥ uddhṛtasya prāguktasyānucchedasya ālocanāyām sāntardṛṣṭikaruṇāyāḥ rūpakāśrita samīkaraṇa sūcayati yat sadṛśabhāvāpannaḥ  vyavahāraḥ kṣudratarachoṭikāṭīkāyāmasti  yā paravarttinī ṭīkā dhammapālasyābhimatena saha sagatisampannā karoti ṭīkā anusṛtya kathyate yat premamayī karuṇā paryāyatrayevatiṣṭhate tathā hi  prāthamikaparyāyepraveśaparyāyesamādhiparyāye ca tathāpi karuṇāyāḥ uparyukta rūpakāśrita vyavahāramantareṇa savādeṣūllikhitāḥ sarve karuṇāsamparkitadṛṣṭāntāḥ niḥsaśaya vā sasaśaya vā samādheḥ praveśaparyāyasya athavā sthāpanāūlakaparyāyasya ca  śaktyā saha virājante  ida karuṇātmakatāyāḥ ca karuṇāyāḥca prayoge pārthakya karoti dvitīyā mānasiīmavasthā sūcayati yā karuṇāśakti dhārayati  prāthamikaparyāyāt sthāpanāparyāya yāvat kramikānuśāsaneṣu gotamaḥ bhikṣūṇupadiśati yat karuṇayā vā mānasamuktyā vā saha tulanīya na karmāpi viṣaya sa paśyati karuṇāyāḥ krodhapratirodhasāmarthyamastikrodhadūrīkaraṇasāmarthyamapi asti aguttaranikāya gotamaḥ bhikṣūn āha  yadi te muktipradhānā karuṇā prati sayatna manoyoga dadatitarhi krodho na jāyate athavā jātaḥ krodhopi dūra gacchati ṭīkāyāmucyate prītiḥ katha manasaḥ muktiḥ bhavitumarhati manasaḥ muktirhi prītiḥ tathā karuṇā eṣā eva karuṇā maṅgalakāmanayā indriyavadbhiḥ jīvaiḥ sahaḥ sambandhatvāt kiñca yataḥ sakaruṇa manaḥ pratibandhakādiviruddhaguṇebhyaḥ mukta bhavatitataḥ aya vyāpāraḥ manasaḥ muktiriti kathyate nirdiśya kathyatekruddhajanasyāpi karuṇāyā sañjātāyā manasaḥ muktiḥ bhavati asmin prasagekiyatā parimāṇena iyameva karuṇā tasyāḥ prāthamika rūpamapi viṣayopayogi tathāpyatramanaso muktiḥ iti kathanena sa kevala karuṇāsthāpanāparyāya sūcayati aguttaranikāyaṭīkā yadi kaścijjanaḥ vipadopareṣāmuddhārāya karaṇatva vrajati tarhi sa teṣā muktiḥ ityucyate atra hetureva phalam evañca yadā karuṇā yathārīti dhyānamagnatāyai kṛṣyateiya niścayena nivāraṇebhyaḥ manaḥ mocayati yataḥ krodhānmanaso muktaye karuṇāyā viśiṣṭā paṭutāstitata iya phalanāma prāpnotimanaso muktiḥ prathamā nimagnatā nivāraṇebhyo muktā asyāḥ pañca mukhyāni upādānāni santi tathā hi  vastuni prāthamikamanaḥsayogaḥ vitakka vastuni manoyogasthāpanam vicāra prītiḥ pītisukham sukha samādhiḥ samādhi ca visuddhimaggaḥ gabhīraḥ samādhiḥ atyantamānandaḥ ceti anayoḥ miśraṇena mānasikī daśā asvābhāvikī iti dṛśyate svābhāvikīṣu avasthāsuyadā eko naro manaḥsayoga karotitadā etāvanniṣpeṣaṇa tiṣṭhati yat paramasukha na sambhavati  prāthamikanimagnatālābhāya vinayanavyāpāre sā śikṣā kriyate yatra praceṣṭāyāḥ śaktiḥ ca samādheḥ sthiratā ca ityanayoḥ madhye samatā sthāpyate phalataḥ tīvrasya atha ca udvegamuktasya manasaḥ samādhiḥ sambhavati asyāmavasthāyā paramasukhasya navīnābhijñatā jāyate yathāyathasamādhaye samatāsampannapraceṣṭayā prayojanamasti tatprakṛtiviśleṣaṇāya viśuddhimārge buddhaghoṣaḥ eka sundara dṛṣṭānta dadāti bhāratīyāḥ śalyavidaḥ jale bhāsamāneṣu padmapatreṣu śalyakriyākaraṇāya śikṣā dadati visuddhimagga atyutsāhī śikṣārthī tatpatra nimagna karoti athavā tatpatra sampūrṇa dvidhā kṛntati bhītipravaṇastu padmapatre balasya prayogāya samartho na bhūtvā tatpatrakarttanāya vyartho bhavati atra saphalasya śikṣārthinaḥ samatāsampannā śaktirasti sa padmapatra nimagna na kṛtvāpi tatpatra sampūrṇa karttitumarhati evañca samādhilābhapraceṣṭā samatāsampannā bhavet tatra atyudvegastathā atigurutā na sthāsyatipunaścana sthāsyati atilaghutā tathā svapnālutā samarūpasampannasamādhilābhāya vinayaśca yatnaśca karaṇīyau ata eva paramasukhena saha muktapremāsvādaḥ durlabhaḥ mānasikaviṣayadhyānakāle prāthamikamanaḥsayogaḥ vitakkasamabhāvenaiva dhyānagatavastuṣu manasaḥ ca ānuṣagikamānasikaviṣayāṇā ca sthāpana karoti samādheḥ asmin paryāye idameva eṣā mānasikānā viṣayāṇāmapūrva vaiśiṣṭyam pratyuta āsaktiḥ mānasavastūni ākarṣati visuddhimagga kiñca āsaktiḥ sarvadā vyākulatayā saha vartate yatra vihvalatāyāḥ prāvaṇya dṛśyate āsaktyā sthāyihatāśābodhaḥ saśliṣyateyata āsaktyāḥ sadāvarttamānā sahacarī vyākulatā sābhiprāyamilanasādhakalakṣyasya upalabdhaye pratibandhakatā sṛjati prāthamikamanaḥsayogasya vitakkasthāpanam appanaiti ākhyāpi tiṣṭhati yasmāt vastuṣu manaḥsthāpanaśaktirasya vartate majjhimanikāya  tathāpi manasaḥ ca mānasaviṣayāṇā a dhyānamagnatāśaktirasti tataḥmanasā saha te sarve viṣayāḥ sthāpanābhidhānena viśiṣyante evamuparyuktāyā ṭīkāyāmsthāpanā appanadhyānamagnatāparyāyagatakaruṇā sūcayati yatra sadṛśī śaktirasti manomuktisādhanāya karuṇāyai vā dhyāninā puruṣeṇa avalambanīyāḥ paryāyā visuddhimagge vistareṇālocitāḥ maḥ adhyāyaḥsamāsataḥ poṣa gatāyāḥ karuṇāyāḥ sāmānyīkaraṇārtha tathā niviḍatāpādanārtha paddhatistatra varṇitā navadīkṣita ātmāna gṛhītvaiva sādhanāmārgābhimukha gantumarabhate sa icchati aha sukhī bhavāniaha varānmukto bhavāni iti tataḥ sa yathā sukhī bhaviṣyatīti kāmayatetathā anyepi kāmayante iti avabudhya sa svabhāvataḥ apareṣā maṅgala kāmayate tataḥ sa priyadharmaguruṣu anyatamāya karuṇā poṣayitum ārabhate idamucyate yat abhyāsakārī tadīyagurudevasya utsāhavardhaka priya vākya smṛtvāpraśasanīyavyavahāram dṛstvāupayuktaśikṣaṇa prāpya ca anāyāsenaiva tasmai karuṇārpaṇāya samartho bhavati tataḥ abhyāsakārī paryāyakrameṇa priyamitrāya karuṇārpaṇāya ceṣṭate navadīkṣitānā kṣetre viparītaliṅgatā parityājyātathā ca ceṣṭate nirapekṣajanāya ca śatrumanobhāvāpannajanāya cāpi ayamāśayaḥ  sa sarveṣu janeṣu karuṇāyā vistārāya tadīyacitta sampūrṇa namanīya dakṣa ca sādhayati atreda sambhavati yat abhyāsakārī śatrubhāvāpanna janamanusmṛtya ātmani śatrutā poṣaiṣyatiasya pratirodhāyajātavairasya anyatra sthāpanāya tathā tat sambhāvanāhrāsāya buddhaghoṣaḥ katividhān vimarśān kathayati atra eṣu vimarśadayamālocyate prathamataḥnaraḥ tadīyakarmaphalamuttarādhikārāt prāpnoti visuddhimagga abhyāsakārī yadi vaira poṣayati tarhi sa paryavekṣate yat sa tatkṣaṇāt vidveṣamiśrita mānasika duḥkha prāpnoti visuddhimagga punaśca sa bhaviṣyati adhikataravairasṛṣṭaye hetūnāviskaroti tasmāt maraṇāt para duḥkhamayapunarjanma yathā bhavati tathā ca vyāhatā bhavati ādhyātmikasamṛddhiḥ atra sa yadi vaira tyajatitarhi sa svaya vidveṣamiśritaānasikakaṣṭāt mukto bhaviṣyati kiñca sa bhaviṣyati svalpavairasṛṣṭaye hetūn sṛjati tena tasya punarjanma sukhakara bhavatiādhyātmikī samṛddhirapi bhavati api ca yadyapi kaścid vairī uparyuktaiḥ sarvaiḥ upāyaiḥ abhyāsakāriṇamapakarttu yātitathāpi vairijana prati pratihisā na karttavyā yataḥ kaścit janaḥ aparasya yatparimāṇamapakāramicchati tadapekṣayādhikatara duḥkha sa prāpnotiprāpsyati ca pratītyasamutpādatatasya prabhāvāt dvitīyataḥnaitādṛśaḥ kopi janaḥ yaḥ kasmisicit samaye kasyāpi na mātā pitā bhaginī bhrātā vā bhavati visuddhimagga yasmāt punarjanma asmāka paścāt anirdiṣṭakāla vitatya tiṣṭhatitasmāt adya pṛthivyā na kopi janaḥ asti yosmāka niviḍa sambandha nāgataḥ asmāka mātṛrūpeṇa yā vyaktiḥ ekadā asmān tasyāḥ aṅke sthāpayitvāāpattiśūnyānasmān pariṣkṛtyasarvavidhamapacaya svīkṛtya asmān sayatna pālayāmāsaatha ca tā prati adhunā vaya śatrutā poṣayāmaḥ pitṛrūpeṇāya janaḥ asmāka pālanāya dīrdha kāla kaṭhora śrama cakāra asmāka bhaginīrūpeṇa vā bhrātṛrūpeṇa vāya jano vividhaiḥ upāyaiḥ asmāka sahāyatā jagāma evam etādṛśa jana prati vaira na karttavyamyataḥ atīte kāle sa janaḥ asmāka kṛte upakāra cakāra evavidhābhiścintābhiḥ manaḥsayogāt abhyāsakārī śatrujana prati karuṇāpoṣaṇakāle jātakrodhasyānyatra sthāpanāya paṭutaraḥ jāyate śatrutāyā vināśa kṛtvā tathā kāścit mānasikī samatā prāpya abhyāsakārī ta prati karuṇā pālayitum agrasaro bhavitumarhati yā karuṇā sa ātmane anubhavatigurudevāyanirapekṣajanāya cānubhavati sā karuṇaiva asmai janāya karttavyā abhyāsakāriṇā janena eva sobhyāsakārī eteṣā viṣayamadhikṛtya karuṇāsakrāntā tīvrāmabhijñatāmavaśyameva racayet tataśca sa śatrujana prati karuṇā nayati anena abhyāsena dhyānī puruṣasḥ svabhāvata eva sarvajīvahitecchayā karmāṇi ācaritu yatate yadi abhyāsakārī ātmanipriyamitrenirapekṣajaneśatrāvapi karuṇā pālayitu saphalo bhavatitarhi tena ātmaparabhedabādhaḥ bhagnaḥ jātaḥ iti ucyate visuddhimagga aya vyāpāraḥ praveśaparyāyagatakaruṇālābha sūcayati tataḥ abhyāsakārī karuṇāyāḥ sthāpanaparyāya yāti tena karuṇā gabhīrā ca ekaniṣṭhā ca bhavati tatra praveśakṣamā śaktirasti ityucyate tataḥ abhyāsakārī tathārīti karuṇāyāḥ parisaramāgatānā jīvānā sakhyā vardhayati tathā ca sa uttarottara sārvalaukika paryāya yāvat karuṇā netu yatate sagotrīyavacaneṣu ātmā manibhaddaḥ gotama prati śloka vadati  manasvī janaḥ sarvadā bhāgyavān manasvī janaḥ sukha paśyati manasvijanāya āgāmikalya sundarataram sa vairāt pramucyate sayuttanikāya gotamaḥ prativadati  manasvī janaḥ sarvadā bhāgyavān manasvī janaḥ sukha paśyati manasvijanāya āgāmikalya sundarataram sa vairānna pramucyate sa hānihīnatāyā nandati samagra divasa samagrā rajanī ca sa sarveṣu jīveṣu snihyati tasya kasyopari vaira nāsti sayuttanikāya gotamasya ślokā nirdiśanti yat yo jano manasvitāyāḥ anuśīlana karoti sa vairāt na mukto bhavati kintu yo janaḥ hānihīnatāyā nandati sarvadāsarveṣu jīveṣu ca snihyati sa vairānmukto jāyate kasyacijjanasya cintā tiṣṭhati aha manasvīti kiyatā parimāṇena iti na viṣayaḥ sa vairāt na mukto bhaviṣyati iti ṭīkā svīkaroti sayuttanikāyaṭīkā ṭīkā viśliṣyati yat buddhenoccārite dvitīye padye uddiṣṭo janaḥ arhatpuruṣaḥ sa prema ca karuṇā ca manasi pālayati sa eva vairāt mukto bhavati asyāḥ ṭīkāyāḥ kortha viśuddhimārgamanusṛtya kathyate yat manasvitā sāvadhānatā vā hitakaro mānasikaḥ viṣayaḥ visuddhimagga ṭīkāsu aya niścayo savitarkamucyate kasmiścidupaṭīkāyāmyat hitakaramānasikaviṣayāḥ ahitakaramānasikaviṣayaiḥ saha sthātu na śaknuvanti  yadā manasvitā vā sāvadhānatā vā ityākhyaḥ hitakaro mānasiko viṣayaḥ asthāyibhāvena upasthitastiṣṭhati tadā kopi ahitakaro mānasiko viṣayo  na tatra sthātum arhati  eva yadi abhyāsakārī purvatanakrodhamuhūrtta cintayatitarhi tasya manaḥ varttamāne muhūrtte svabhāvata eva krodhānmukta bhavati sa hitakaramanoyuktaḥ yadā bhavati tadā sa trayodaśamānasikaguṇaiḥ anvitastiṣṭhati te sarvadā hitakaramanasā saha varttante tathā hi  pratyayaḥsāvadhānatāvivekaḥlajjāghṛṇāśūnyatānirlobhatāsamaprāṇatāśāntacittatālaghutānamanīyatādakṣatāviśeṣajñatā ṛjutā visuddhimagga saḥ anubhavadvayasya ekatarasyābhijñatā labhate tathā hi mānasika sukha samavṛttitā ca etau anubhavau hitakaramanasā anvitau tiṣṭhataḥ visuddhimagga yobhyāsakārī manasvitā sāvadhānatā vā poṣayatisa bhaviṣyati kāle sadṛśī hitakarī pravaṇatā sṛjatiīdṛśasya janasya kṛte āgāmikalya sundarataram iti tathāpi gotamasya matemanasvitayā śatrutāyāḥ anyatra sthapana na paryāptammanasvī sāvadhānī vā janaḥ śatrutāyā muktaḥ na bhavati anyeṣu prasageṣu karuṇā mānasamuktiriti kathyate atra hetuḥ  dhyānamagnatāparyāye mānasamuktau satyā sā muktiḥ alpakāla manaḥ krodhamukta karoti aguttaranikāya ṭīkā  maḥ yobhyāsakārī dhyānamagnatāparyāya vyāpya dakṣatayā karuṇā poṣayatisa svaya krodhamukto jāyate tathā ca dhyānamagnatayā saha paramasukha bhuñkte  api ṭīkākārāḥ gotamoktaślokasya nimnarūpā vyākhyā kurvanti tathā hi  vairibhāvāt yathāyatha mānasamuktisādhanāya karuṇā dhyānamagnatayā  poṣayitavyā  eṣā sambhāvanā parityaktu śakyate yataḥ manasvitā anyatra sthāpanena manaḥ kevala svalpakāla vairāt mukta karoti eṣā manasvitā na vairāt santoṣāvahā muktiḥ evameva karuṇā avadamanena svalpakāma mānasamukti sādhayati eṣāpi vairāt santoṣāvahā muktiḥ bhavitu nārhati ṭīkā tu pṛthagbhāvamavalambate  ṭīkā vyākhyāti yat prathame śloke uddiṣṭaḥ janaḥ adhunāpi aha manasvī vā sāvadhānī vā iti cintayā manasvitānuśīlana karoti sayuttanikāya tena na ātmanosārā prakṛtiḥ upalabdhā sa nopalabdhi karoti yatmanasvitānuśīlanesāpekṣaviṣayaḥ aparasāpekṣaviṣaya paśyati visuddhimagga sa nopalabdhi karoti yat kevalamanityā mānasikāḥ śārīrikāśca padārthā vartante tatra kasmiścidapi padārthe na cirasthāyī ātmā dṛśyate īdṛśo janaḥ bhrānta matapadacetanāmākāṅkṣā ca na nirākartu śaknoti visuddhimagga sa āśābhagnaḥ sañjātavairāt na mukto bhavitumarhati dvitīye śloke uddiṣṭo janaḥ abhyāsakārīsampūrṇamuktārhatpuruṣa iti vyākhyāyate sa sarvavidhasāpekṣavastūnāmanityatva pratyakṣīkaroti sonubhavati yat paramārthataḥ nityaḥ sārabhūtaḥ ca aham nāstiyoha daihikabhūteṣu manasi vā sarvatra dṛśyate saḥ ahamasmi ahamasmi mamansvī  evavidhayā cintayā na punaḥ baddhaḥ tiṣṭhati sayuttanikāya arhatpuruṣaḥ vaireṇa saha sarvavidhamānasikadūṣaṇebhyaḥ ātmāna cita moktumarhati visuddhimagga  sa sarvadā prema ca karuṇā ca pālayitumalam vairāt tasya muktiḥ paripūrṇā krakacadṛṣṭāntasavāde gotamaḥ vividhāsu avasthāsu kāruṇikacittalālanena prayojanamupadiśati majjhimanikāya buddhaḥ bhikṣūnāha yat teṣā sambodhana pañcadhā bhaviṣyati tathā hi  upayuktasamaye athavā anupayuktasamayesatyamanusṛtya athavā asatyamanusṛtyakārkaśyena athavā mādhuryeṇalābhajanakatayā athavā alābhajanakatayākāruṇikacittavadbhiḥ athavā krodhayuktaiḥ gotamaḥ bhikṣūn jñāpayati yat yenopāyenaiva teṣā sambodhana bhavatu vā na vāte karuṇāmaya citta pālayeyuḥ sa teṣā vinayana viśliṣyati  asmāka cittāni unmārgagāmīni na bhavantu vaya kuvākya na vadiṣyāmaḥ vaya parebhyaḥ hitāya sahānubhava poṣayiṣyāmaḥ asmāka cittāni prītisnigdhāni bhaviṣyantikrodhamuktāni bhaviṣyanti cittagatakaruṇayā vayam āhvāyakena janena saha sambandhasya cheda na kariṣyāmaḥ samagra jagadasmāka kāruṇikacittānā gantavya sthalam tena jagatā saha asmāka sambandhaḥ dṛḍhaḥ bhavatu cittāni bhavantu praśāntānivairāt muktāniviśālānivistṛtāniparimāṇaśūnyāni ca majjhimanikāya yādṛśī karuṇā bhikṣūṇā tiṣṭhatu tāmeva bhiksavaḥ janāya poṣayet tataśca karuṇāyāḥ sāmānyīkaraṇa karttavyam ṭīkā yathāśabda vyākhyāti  samagram sarvasacetanajīvasametamjagat sacetanānā jīvānā sthānamviśālam yasya viṣayatvena sacetanajīvagaṇastiṣṭhativistṛtam astitvarakṣāyai vistṛtā bhūmirastiparimāṇaśūnyam yataḥ idamutkṛṣṭamvairānmuktam krodha vinānirudvignam duḥkhaśūnyam majjhimanikāyaṭīkā atra varṇita citta vistṛtamyasmāt astitvasūcakasamagrabhūmirevāsyādhikāre vartaterūpamaya tathā rūpahīna jagat viśuddhimagga  yadā citta dhyānamagnatāparyāya yāvat kṛṣṭa bhavatitadā tat citta jagatparivartana karotīti kathyate ida rūpamaya sūkṣmajagat praviśati yadi dhyānamagnātāyāḥ prathamaparyāya  catuṣṭaya vyāpya kṛṣyate athavā ida rūpahīna sūkṣmatara jagat praviśati yadi ādhikyena kṛṣyate anena jagatā saha anvitasya manasaḥ avasthā vistṛtāḥ yataḥ svalpakālamapi dūṣaṇaparihārāya mahat sāmarthyamasti api catatpakṣ mahadupāyanamapi asti ṭīkā  yasmāt karuṇā dhyānamagnatāyāḥ ādyaparyāyatraye sthātumarhati visuddhimagga tasmāt atra vistṛtapadena trayāṇāmekatama budhyate atra prabandhekaruṇāmaya citta parimāṇaśūnyamiti api varṇyate sāmānyataḥyaḥ samādhiḥ sādhu kṛṣyate tathā dhyānamagnatāyāḥ prathame paryāye tiṣṭhatianyeṣu paryāyeṣu apisa samādhiḥ parimāṇaśūnyaḥ iti kathyate visuddhimagga prathamaparyāyamantareṇāpi uccataraparyāye samādhiḥ etāmākhyā prāpnotiyataḥ asmin samaye samādhiḥ indriyatṛṣṇādimayajagataḥ sarvavidhasīmāvaddhatābhyaḥ muktaḥ bhavati ṭīkā  yā iyam ākhyā dhyānamagnatāparyāyagatasamādhi nirdiśati sā tatraiva paryāye karuṇānvitacitta sūcayati evamasmin savāde gotamo bhikṣūnupadiśati yat te dhyānamagnatāparyāya yāvat karuṇā poṣayeyuḥ yadi te dhyānena kiyatā parimāṇena  karuṇākarṣaṇe saphalāḥ bhavanti tarhi teṣā cittāni karuṇayā yujyantesakaruṇaiḥ aparaiḥ guṇaiḥ api visuddhimagga dhyānaparavarttisamaye te hitakaracittena saha bhārasāmya sthāpayanti tathā ca mānasika sukha vā samavṛttitva vā anubhavanti teṣāmuparodho duḥsādhyaḥ krakacadṛṣṭānte gotamaḥ kāruṇikacittasya balasya ca sthāyitvasya ca dṛṣṭānta kathayati sa bhikṣūn pṛcchati  ko janaḥ yuṣmāsu khananena vā mūtratyāgena vā pṛthivyā vināśa kartu samarthaḥ bhaviṣyatīti neti teṣā prativacanamāsīt yasmāt pṛthivī gabhīrā aparimeyā ca appameyya tataḥ gotamaḥ pṛthivyāḥ abhedyatā kāruṇikacittasya śaktiḥ ityanayoḥ madhye tulanā pradarśayati sa bhikṣūnāha  api kopi bhikṣuḥ pañcasu upāyeṣu anyatamamavalambya apareṇa saha ālapet api sa premamaya citta pālayet athavā api te karuṇārdrahṛdayena aparajanena saha sambandha sthāpayet  bhikṣubhiḥ nimnoktopāyena vinayana kartavya  sarvaiḥ jīvaiḥ saha yat jagat tat sarvameva kāruṇikacittasya lakṣyasthala vidhāya vaya cittena  samagreṇa jagatā saha sambandha sthāpayitumalam  jagadiveda cittamakṣobha vairānmukta viśāla vistṛta parimāṇaśūnya ca majjhimanikāya yathā kopi janaḥ khanitreṇa ca pātreṇa ca viśālapṛthivīvināśāya na samarthaḥ bhavatitathā pañcavidhāni vacanāni pratikūlatayā karuṇārdracittavanta jana abhibhavitu na śaknuvanti majjhimanikāya pṛthivī yathā ākramaṇa nirākaroti gabhīratvāt aparimeyatvāt catathaiva karuṇārdracittam tadvat gotamaḥ bhikṣūnapadiśati yat te karuṇā pālayiṣyanti tathākaraṇena teṣā cittamakhaṇḍadeśavat avarṇanīya bhaviṣyatigaṅgāvat bhaviṣyati adahanīyam ūrṇāmayakhaṇḍena gharṣaṇāt susyūtaḥ viḍalacarmapuṭaḥ karkaśaḥ na bhavati bhiksavo yadi imamupadeśamanusarantitarhi teṣā citta sahasā pralubdhapradīpta karkaśa ca na bhaviṣyati sagotrīyavacaneṣu gotama upadiśati yat yasmin gṛhe bahavaḥ strīlokāḥ kintu atyalpāḥ puruṣāstiṣṭhantitat gṛhamanāyāsena ākrānta bhavati tadvat yo bhikṣuḥ karuṇārūpamanomukti na sādhayati sa niścitamamānuṣībhiḥ śaktibhiḥ upadrutaḥ bhavati sayuttanikāya anyataśca yasmin gṛhe bahavo narāḥ kintu atyalpā nāryyaḥ tiṣṭhantitadgṛha sahasā dasyubhiḥ ākrānta na bhavatitathā yo bhikṣuḥ karuṇārupamanomukti sādhayati saḥ amānuṣībhiḥ śaktibhiḥ abhibhūtaḥ na bhavati tataḥ sa bhikṣūn karuṇānuśīlanāya upadiśati savādānā pañcamasagrahe karuṇāsavāde gotamaḥ bhikṣūnupadiśati katha dhyātavyamitiyena dhyānena duṣṭagrahabhaya na tiṣṭhatibhikṣavaḥ taiśca upadrutāḥ na bhavanti khuddakapāṭha  lābhajanakeṣu abhyāseṣu dakṣaḥ janaḥ ki kuryāt yadā sa śāntipūrṇā daśā jānāti sa samarthaḥsajjanaḥsaralothaca dṛḍhaḥgrahaṇakṣamaḥnamanīyaḥ vinītaḥsantuṣṭaḥsukhena puṣṭaḥ bhavetsvalpakarmabhiḥ svalpavastubhiḥsamarthaiḥ indriyaiḥjñānī karmaṇi vivicya sasāriṇaścānukṛtya sa kadāpi na nīcācaraṇamācaret tadācarana jñānijanakartṛkaguṇadoṣavivecana janayati sa etāḥ kāmanāḥ pālayetsarve jīvāḥ sukha nirbhaya ca vasantu te sarve hṛdayena sukhinaḥ bhavantu ya eva prāṇavān jīvaḥsthiro vā asthiro vā vyatikramamantareṇadīrghothavā viśālaḥ madhyamo hrasvaḥ sūkṣmosūkṣmo vā dṛśyo vā adṛśyo vādūravarttī vā nikaṭavartī vā jīvo yo vā janiṣyate te sarve hṛdayena sukhino bhavanti kopi janaḥ apara jana na pratārayet kopi janaḥ kasyāpi samīpe kutrāpi ca sammānāt garvito na bhavet kenāpi anyajanahānicintā na karaṇīyā krodhād vā vidveṣād vā sarvān jīvān prati asīma citta pālayet yathā mātā svīyajīvanavyayenāpi ekamātra putra rakṣati asīma premamaya citta poṣayet bādha krodha virodha vāntareṇa samagra jagat prati upariadhaḥpārśvāt pārśvāntaram ca daṇḍāyamānāvasthāyāvacaraṇeupaveśane śayane vā sa manasvitāmavalambya dṛḍhasakalpo bhavet atrāyamevodātto bhāvaḥ prakīrtitaḥ mithyāmata parihāya satyamācaraṇa tathā satyadṛṣṭimavalambya kāmyavastuṣu āsakti dūrikṛtya sa nūna na navagarbha gamiṣyati khuddakapāṭha  ṭīkāyā mate yadā bhikṣāvaḥ uktasavādagataviṣayamavagatya tasya upadeśān anusaranti tathā karuṇā poṣayanti tadā vighnakāriṇaḥ devāḥ kamapi  vighna na sṛṣṭvā santuṣṭāḥ sukhinaḥ sahayoginaḥ sahāyakāśca bhavanti  khuddakapāṭha eva daivaśaktīnāmabhibhavāya karuṇāyāḥ sāmarthyamasti viśākhānāmadheyasya bhikṣoḥ upākhyānenāsya matasya samarthana kriyateyasya karuṇāśīlanāt amānuṣyaḥ śaktayaḥ tasya sannidhau paraspara śāntipūrṇabhāvena vasanti visuddhimagga tāḥ śaktayo yadi karuṇānuśīlanakāribhiḥ bhikṣubhiḥ saha sahayogitā na kurvantitathāpi tā bhikṣūnapakarttu na śakṣyanti sagotrīyavacaneṣu gotamo vadati  yadi amānuṣyaḥ śaktayaḥ karuṇārūpamanomuktisādhanakāriṇā bhikṣūṇām upadrava kurvantitadā vā eva pariśrāntā bhaviṣyanti sayuttanikāya tathāpi abhyāsakārī bhayādvā dāsyād vā amānuṣībhiḥ śaktibhiḥ sṛṣṭādupadravādrakṣaṇa na kāmayate vara bhayāsaktigarvādīn doṣān parityajya manomuktirūpakaruṇā karṣati  udāttabhāvam aguttaranikāyaṭīkā visuddhimagga tataḥ tasya citta sthira sāmyāpanna tathā paramasukhamaya bhavati viśuddhimagga tathā ca tat citta sarvavidhamānasikavipattipratirodhakāri bhavati idamucyate yat abhyāsakārī kāyikopadravādapi rakṣyate visuddhimagga  tathā hi  sāmānyā nārī sapavatī gotamasya pradhānā śiṣyā āsīt karuṇānuśīlana kurvatī sā karuṇayā svīyahānipratirodhāya samarthā āsīt aguttaranikāya tasyā ānugatye aviśvāsī san tasyāḥ svāmī vāṇena tā antumudyatobhavat kintu sasakhī samavatī premṇā karuṇayā ca svāmina mugdhamakarot ataḥ sa īpsita vadha samāptu na śaśāka viśuddhimagga tathāpi samavatī svaya vyatikramatva bhajati sā karuṇānuśīlane nipuṇā satyapi avaśeṣe tatkṛtahānikarakāryaphalāt agnidāhena amriyata abhyāsakāriṇaḥ karuṇā aparajanamanobhāva kalyāṇābhimukha kartu samarthā iti spaṣṭo dṛṣṭāntaḥ savādeṣu yadyapi nāstitathāpi karuṇāyā īdṛśī śaktirasti iti viśuddhimārge kathyate samādhaye catvāriśadvastuṣu anyatamasya upari yathāyatha dhyātumārabhate abhyāsakārī athavā antardṛṣṭisamunnataye yatate tasmāt prak sa nimnoktopāyena karuṇā pālayedityupadiśyate dhyānaviṣaya gṛhītā bhikṣuḥ prathamataḥ upāsanālayasaśliṣṭānā bhikṣūṇā sampradāyasya sīmā nirdeśet tataḥ sa teṣā kṛte evavidhayā cintayā karuṇā pālayet  te sukhino bhavantumuktāśca bhavantūpadravāt iti tataḥ sa grāmasthānā devatānā kṛte karuṇā pālayet tataḥ sa netṛsthānīyānā janānāmupuri karuṇā poṣayet ye janāḥ tasmai khādyādi dadati tataśca sarveṣā manuṣyāṇā tathā jīvānā kṛte karuṇānuśīlana kuryāt upāsanālayasaśliṣṭabhikṣūṇā kṛte pālitayā karuṇayā sa tasya sahacareṣu komalahṛdayatā janayati te ca ekatra tena saha sukhena vasanti upāsanālayasaśliṣṭānā devatānā kṛte pālitayā karuṇayā tā devatāḥ komalahṛdayāḥ satyaḥ yathāyatha rakṣaṇena ta sampūrṇa rakṣanti netṛsthānīyānā grāmavāsinā kṛte pālitayā karuṇayā te komalahṛdayāḥ santaḥ yathāyatha sayatna tasmai āvaśyakadravyadānena sevante mānavatā kṛte pālitayā karuṇayā te mānavāḥ svacchahṛdayā bhavanti tataḥ sa yadā parivrajati tadā te na avajñā pradarśayiṣyanti sarveṣu jīveṣu karuṇāyā pālitāyā bhikṣuḥ sarvatra nirbādha gantu samartho bhavatite na pratibandhakatā sṛjanti visuddhimagga uparyuktānuśīlane bhayamastiāsaktiḥ asti taddvayena hitakaramanuśīlana doṣayukta bhavitumarhati tathāpi bhārasāmyavivekaviśvāsaiḥ anuśīlana karttayam dhyānaviṣayatvena aparaviṣayasya grahaṇāt prāk anayā rītyā abhyāsakārī karuṇā khalu pālayiṣyati sādhāraṇakarmāṅgatena saḥ avaśyamevaivamācaret visuddhimagga anuśīlanagatayathāyathaprasagasthāpanāya premakaruṇānirbhara dhyāna bhūmirvā mṛttikā vā yatra samādhikarṣaṇa vā antardṛṣṭikarṣaṇa vā kriyate samyag jñānalābhāt paramapi evavidha karṣaṇam avyāhata tiṣṭhati aguttaranikāya  viśuddhimārgāt uparyuktyanucchedaḥ savādeṣu vā ṭīkāsu vā kevala dṛṣṭāntaḥ yatra spaṣṭam ucyate yat karuṇāyāḥ dhyānātmakamanuśīlana sapadi  sukhena aparajanamanobhāva prabhāvita karoti  iya śikṣā dhyānamagnatāyā kṛṣṭā karuṇā prati asāmānyā mātrā prakāśayati abhyāsakāriṇopareṣā sāhāyya kartu śaknuvantina kevala śikṣayābhikṣāgrahaṇenadharmīyajīvanagatadṛṣṭāntasthāpanenaapi tu karuṇāsamparkitadhyānātmakonnatisādhanena sambhavataḥidameva sahānubhūtiśīlānandakarṣaṇamityucyate kramikavacaneṣu gotamo vyākhyāti yat kaścid bhikṣuḥ sarpeṇa dāruṇa daṣṭobhavatyataḥ sa karuṇārdracittena sarpāṇā kulacatuṣṭhayena saha sambandha na sthāpayāmāsa aguttaranikāya   gotama āha  bhikṣuṇā karuṇārdracittena sarpāṇā kulacatuṣṭayena saha samparke sthāpite sati sa na daṣṭobhaviṣyat  eva sarpadaśanāt ātmanā rakṣaṇāya abhyāsakāriṇaḥ sarpāṇā kulacatuṣṭayena saha karuṇāmayacittena samparka sthāpayet evameva cintayitvā   karuṇā mesti virupakkānā kṛte karuṇā me ca erāpatānā kṛte karuṇā mesti chavyaputtānā tathā kaṇhāgotamakānā kṛte  karuṇā mesti padaśūnyānā kṛte tathā ca padadvayayuktānā kṛte karuṇa mesti padacatuṣṭayayuktānā kṛte bahupadānā kṛtepi ca padaśūnyā na māmapakurvantuna ca padadvayayuktaḥ catuṣpadāḥ na māmapakurvantuna ca bahupadāḥ sarve sacetanā jīvāḥsare prāṇavantaḥ jīvāḥ sare ekatra pavitrāṇi dṛśyāni paśyantu kamapi na pāpamāgacchatu buddhaḥ aparimeyaḥdharmaḥ aparimeyaḥsaghaḥ aparimeyaḥ kintu sarpāvṛścikā jalaukasaūrṇanābhāḥ kṛkalāsā mūṣikāśca sarve parimeyā ea mayā rakṣaṇa vistṛtammayā rakṣaṇa sthāpitam sarve jīvāḥ palāyana kurvantu aha bhāgyabhavantamadvitīya staumi aha saptasamyagjñāninaḥ staumi aguttaranikāya yadā gotama āha buddhādayaḥ aparimeyāḥ ititadā tasyāśayaḥ  sa buddhasyadharmasyasaghasya ca guṇān nirdiśati aguttaranikāyaṭīkā sarpādīnā parimeyo guṇosti aguttaranikāyaṭīkā gotamo bhikṣūṇ pradarśayati yat karuṇāpālana dharmīyasatyavyākhyāna ceti hitakarakarmadvayena te ātmānaḥ rakṣitu śaknuvanti hānihīnatā ca parihṛtya hānikarajīvebhyo dūra gatvā tiṣṭhanti kiñca sagotrīyavacaneṣu gotamo bhikṣūn upadiśati yat te karuṇayātmanaḥ rakṣitu śaknuvanti atra mallavīrasya ca tasya śikṣārthinaḥ ca dṛṣṭāntosti ātmarakṣāviṣaye tau bhinnamata poṣayataḥ mallavīra āha aha tvā lakṣyayāmi tva ca mām evamanyonyalakṣaṇena paraspararakṣaṇa sambhavati āvayoḥ mallakrīḍāpi nirvighna samāpti gamiṣyatīti anyataśca śikṣārthī āha  ahamātmāna lakṣayāmi bhavānapi ātmāna lakṣayatu iti gotamo vyākhyāti yat kartā śikṣārthinaḥ paddhati saphalamanusaret tathā ca upasaharati yat sa kartā manasvitāsthāpanena sadṛśī rītimanukuryāt śabdāntaraiḥ ucyatebhikṣavaḥ sveṣā manasvitāyāḥ unnataye parasparasahayogitā kuryuḥ yāparyāyeṇa apareṣāmupakāra parokṣataḥ sādhayiṣyati bhikṣavaḥ teṣā praśāntaiḥ manoyogaiḥ ca vyahavāraiḥ dharmīyajīvanasamparkitapuraskārāṇāmudāharaṇāni pradarśayiṣyanti tathā ca anyebhyaḥ anupreraṇā dāsyanti buddha āha  bhikṣavaḥya ātmāna rakṣati sa parānapi rakṣati yo vā parān rakṣati sa ātmānamapi rakṣati bhikṣavaḥ kathamātmarakṣākārī aparān rakṣati punaḥ punaḥ dhyānadhāraṇenadhānakarṣaṇenadhyānābhyāsena ca bhīkṣavaḥ evamātmarakṣākārī aparān rakṣatibhikṣavaḥ pararakṣākārī kathamātmāna rakṣati dhīratayā hānihīnagayākaruṇāvasthayāsnehamayayatnāvasthayā ca bhikṣavaḥ eva pararakṣākārī ātmāna rakṣati yadi abhyāsakārī ātmānamadhikṛtya athavā parānadhikṛtya svīyacittasya yatna gṛṇhātitarhi ātmānastathā pareṣāmapi upakāro bhavati ṭīkā spaṣṭa vadati  pālayitvādhyānavastu cintayitvābhikṣavaḥ evamātmarakṣākārī parān rakṣati yo bhikṣuḥ pārthivaviṣayagatamānanda parihāya pradhānadhyānavastu aharniśa pālayati karṣati ca sorhatpuruṣasya daśā labhate tataḥ aparo janasta dṛṣṭvā cintayatiayamuttamo bhikṣuḥ tena yathāriti abhyāsaḥ kṛta iti  bhikṣusamparkīyametanmata poṣayitvā sa svargamupāgamiṣyati eva ya ātmāna rakṣati sa parānapi rakṣatīti  dhairyeṇa ityasyārthaḥ dhīratayā sahiṣṇutayā ceti hānihīnatayā ityasyārthaḥ prāthamikaparyāyagatakaruṇayā saha anukampayā iti premāvasthayā ityasyārthaḥ prāthamikaparyāyagatapremṇā saha prītyeti sasnehayatnāvasthayā ityāsyārthaḥ prāthamikaparyāyagatasahānubhūtānandena saha snehānvitasevayā sahānubhūtasukhena ceti yaḥ parān rakṣati sa ātmānamapi rakṣati asmin prasagebhikṣuḥ karuṇāpremasahānubhūtānandaḥ iti udāttabhāvatrayamadhikṛtya aharniśam ādyaparyāyatrayagatadhyānamagnatāmācarati tathā karaṇena sāpekṣavastuvaiśiṣṭya jñātvā arhatpurusasyāvasthā labhate eva yaḥ parān rakṣati sa ātmānamapi rakṣatīti sayuttanikāyaṭīkā arhatpuruṣasḥ pareṣu dharmīyajīvanāt prāpyānā purasārāṇāmādarśabhūtaḥ kaścijjanaḥ arhatpuruṣamālokya prītaśca dṛḍhapratyayaśca bhavati tathā ca tadīyavyavahāreṇānuprāṇito bhavati tasmin samaye hitakarahṛdayavān janaḥ bhaviṣyati kāle arhatpuruṣatvārjanāya kāraṇāni sṛjati asya viśvastasya hitakarasya ca cittasya kārānāt sa janaḥ kartṛrūpaḥ maraṇāt para nyūnatamataḥ svarge janiṣyate eva yobhyāsakārī svīyānuśīlanena ātmāna rakṣati sorhatpuruṣaḥ san parānapi rakṣati yadyapi premakaruṇāsahānubhūtānandaḥ ca  iti udāttabhāvatrayānuśīlanena abhyāsakārī aparān hitāvaha ca pratyakṣa ca prabhāvitān karotitathāpi savādeṣu anyaviṣayasya ullekho nāsti vara yo jana etān bhāvān karṣatisa tasya citta yathākrama krodhātniṣṭhuratvāt paradoṣādoṣāt ca rakṣati iti viṣayeṣu savādā gurutvamāropayanti prāgukte savāde gotamaḥ varṇayati yat abhyāsakārī aparān prati tasya manobhāvamadhikṛtya dhīratayahānihīnatayākaruṇāvasthayāsasnehayatnāvasthayā ca tadīyacitta rakṣati karuṇā prema sahānubhūtānandaḥ iti udāttabhāvatrayabodhāya antimabhāvatraya vyākhyāyate ayamāśayaḥ  dhyānamagnatāparyāye sārvalaukikapremāditvena te bhāvā gamyante aguttaramāśayaḥ  dhyānamagnatāparyāye sārvalaukikapremāditvena te bhāvā gamyante aguttaranikāya visuddhimagga ete udāttā bhāvāḥ krodhādyanaitikavācakabhāvāt abhyāsakāriṇa rakṣanti uktabhāvatraya khalu antardṛṣṭermūlatvena vyavahriyateyathā antardṛṣṭyā abhyāsakārī sarvavidhamānasikadūṣaṇa cira parityaktumagrasaro bhavati sa tathākaraṇena sarvavidhānuṣaṅgikaduḥkhaiḥ saha punarjanamana ātmāna muñcati tataśca arhatpuruṣaḥ bhavati eva parān prati svīyabhāvamavalambya sobhyāsakārī svīyacitta rakṣatitenātmanaḥ rakṣaṇa samāpti gacchati aya savādaḥ abhyāsakāriṇā dṛṣṭāntamūlakakarmasu tathā dharmīyasamṛddhisamparkitatātparyedhika gurutvamāropayati yadyapi atra sāmājikakarmopadeśānā spaṣṭa ullekho nāsti tathāpīda gamyate yat sahānubhūtisamparkitopadeśānā vistṛte pariprekṣite pareṣā kṛtebhyāsakāriṇā hṛdayānubhūta udvego mukhyataḥ śikṣayā  karmaniṣṭha prakāśitaḥ  sāmājikodvegasya ca tadānuṣaṅgikakarmaṇo madhyenivāryaḥ sambandhosti  iti vayamanubhavāmaḥ pūrvatanasya sarvavidhālocanāparatana yāvadavicchinna vahati kintu buddhenātra etāvadanivāryatva nānubhūtam sa sahānubhūtiḥ saralākaruṇākaruṇātmakakarmāṇietatrayasamparkitopadeśeṣuviśeṣeṇa sahānubhūtimūlakopadeśeṣu sāmājikodvegena saha sāmājikakarmaṇaḥ samparka paśyati sa vyaktigatakṣetre tathā sahāyakabhrātrīyakarmaṇi  yatra aparaiḥ saha abhyāsakāriṇo yogostitat saparkitaparyāyasyopari gurutvamāropayati sa premakaruṇāsamparkitadhyānātmakopadeśaiḥ saha paravartiparārthamūlakakarmaṇā sambandha sthāpayitu prayojana nānvabhavat yataḥ paravartiviṣayasyopadeśaḥ tenānyatra dattaḥ kintu atreda gamyate it īdṛśadhyānānusaraṇāya īdṛśaparārthaparakarmaṇā svābhāvikī pravaṇatā tiṣṭhati pālitapremakaruṇālocanākāle gotamaḥ apūrvāṇā guṇānāmupasthāpana karotiye guṇāḥ sahānubhūtiḥ saralākaruṇāḥ premamayakarmāṇi  iti eṣā viṣayāṇā prasage prāyeṇa nālocitaḥ etepūrvā guṇāḥ teṣā rakṣaṇātmakāḥ viṣayāḥvyaktigatāstathā manastatvasammatā lābhāḥparavartijīvanāya api lābhāḥ kramikavacaneṣu gotama upadiśati yat aṣṭau lābhāḥ santi kaścijjanaḥ karuṇarūpamanomuktitaḥ tān lābhān arjayitumalamyadā vā tīvrāaṅgīkṛtāvardhitāpratiśrutitvena pariṇatā bhavati aguttaranikāya naraḥ samyak svapiti sa samyak jāgartti sa suḥsvapnān na paśyati sa manuṣyāṇā priyo bhavati somanuṣyāṇā priyo bhavati devatāsta rakṣanti sogninā viṣeṇaastraiśca nābhibhūto bhavati tasyopalabdhiryadi mahattarā na bhavati tarhi sa brāhmajagat ārohati  aguttaranikāya ṭīkayā viśleṣaṇamevam  sa bhayaṅkarān svapnān na paśyati sa yadyapi paśyatitathāpi te svapnāḥ kevala śubhāḥ svapnā eva sa ātmāna paśyati yathā  sovaśiṣṭādhāre śraddhā nivedayatīva athavā buddhadharmasagha ca pūjayatīva yathā apare janāḥ svapnān paśyantitathā sa na paśyatiapare paśyanti  te dasyubhiḥ veṣṭitāḥsarpaiḥ tāḍitā athavā vivaramadhye patitā iva sa nāgninā viṣeṇāstraiśca abhibhūto bhavati asmin prasage kati gokathā kathayanti kaścit gauḥ daṇḍāyamānaḥ san vatsāya dugdha dadāti sma kaścit vyādhaḥ hastena kunta dhṛtvā acintayataha gāmimam prahariṣyāmi iti tena kunte nikṣipte sati sa kuntaḥ goḥ śarīram āhatya punareva tālapatramiva pratyāgataḥ atra praveśaparyāyagatā karuṇā na hetuḥna vā sthāpanaparyāyagatā karuṇā api tuvatsahitāya goḥ sutīvrā ākāṅkṣā eva karuṇāyāḥ mahatī śaktirasti aguttaranikāyaṭīkā karuṇārūpamanomuktisañjātalābhāḥ khalu upari uktāḥ kintu ete lābhāḥ svabhāvataḥ sarvāsu avasthāsu ghaṭante iti kadāpi na savādeṣu vā ṭīkāsu vā uktam gotamopi karuṇāyāḥ sahānubhūteśca mahatī śakti
