dhṛtvāpi śatruśūnyo nāsīt īrṣyāparāyaṇo bhrātā devadatta eva tasya pramāṇam vividhāsu daśāsu manaso śaktiḥ ca parārtha tacchakteḥ kāryakāritā cetyanayoḥ madhye samānupātaḥ lakṣaṇīyaḥ sahānubhūtiḥ manasaḥ kayācit śaktyā saha viśeṣeṇa nānvitā bhavati abhyāsakāriṇaḥ aparānupadiśantiaparebhyaḥ bhikṣā gṛhṇantiparārtha ca dharmīyajīvanasya dṛṣṭānta sthāpayanti eṣu sarveṣu kṣetreṣu sahānubhūtiḥ paricālikā śaktirityabhidhīyate karuṇārdrakarmāṇi karuṇāmayacittasya kāñcit śaktimavalambante tāni karmāṇi parahitasahāyakāniyadyapi karuṇārūpā manomuktiḥ parebhyaḥ kīdṛśa hita sādhayati sa viṣayo nālocitaḥtathāpi ida niḥsaśaya gamyate yat karuṇākarṣaṇa kasyāpi sahānubhūti niviḍā karoti evañca paravartipararthaparakarmasu prabhāva prakāśayati kasyacinmanobhāvasya śaktiḥtajjātalābhāḥtaddoṣapratikārā yadā ekatra niḥsaśaya prakāśyante tadā teṣu madhye pratyakṣayogo dṛśyate sahānubhavaḥ prakṛtyā eva grahaṇīyo manobhāvaḥ tatra preṣaṇāśaktirastitāṛśaḥ sahānubhavaḥ vartamānena vā bhāvinā puraskārena na kadāpi samarthyate prāthamikaparyāyagata kāruṇika citta bhikṣujanasya bhikṣābhogadhyānābhyāsa bhikṣunāmadhāraṇa ca samarthayitumarhati api ca kāruṇikacittapreṣitaparasparasāpekṣakaruṇātmakakarmāṇi saghasya samṛddhaye bhavanti tathāpi karuṇārūpamanomuktisañjālalābhāstathā taddoṣapratikārā atīva vicitrāḥ pracurāḥ cayata uccaparyāyagatamanaḥsañjātāsāmānyalābhāya eva ātyantiko manoyogo dīyate ida niḥsaśayamucyate yat etādṛśa manobalamapi svalpasamāhitabhāvasañjātalābhān janayati  uparyukte savāde karuṇājātalābhān ālocya gotamaḥ karuṇāvikāśa praśasyāha aparimeyakaruṇākarṣaṇaśīlasya manasvino purusya nigaḍāḥ kṣaya gacchanti sa sasāracakrasya bhittimūla nāśa yātīti paśyati yo janaḥ kevala prāṇiviśeṣāya karuṇā poṣayati sa tathākanraṇena hitasampādako jāyate yo mahān puruṣaḥ sarveṣā prāṇinā kṛte sahānubhūtiśīlo bhavati sa pracura puṇya sagṛhṇāti ṛṣitulyā nṛpāḥ sacetanajīvapūrṇā dharaṇī jayati tataśca te katipayayāgakaraṇāya vratī bhavati tathā hi  assamedhaḥpurisamedhaḥsammāpasaḥvājapeyaḥ niraggalaḥ iti  kaścijjanaḥ karuṇāmayacittasya samyakpoṣaṇena yat puṇyamarjayati tasya puṇye yaḥ ṣoḍaśo bhāgastasyāpi ekaṣoḍaśabhāga puṇya te na saccinvanti te candramaṇḍale nakṣatrāṇi iva śobhante yo na hanti na vā ghātayati aparaiḥyo na dasyutā karotina vāparaiḥ dasyutā kārayatisarveṣā bhūtānā kṛte yasyāsti karuṇā sa kamapi jana prati vaira na poṣati aguttaranikāya nigaḍā kṣaya gacchanti sa sasāracakrasya bhittimūla nāśa yātīti pasyati ayamāśayaḥ  yo janorhatpuruṣasyāvasthā gataḥ sa daśa nigaḍān parityajati atra sasāracakrabhittimūlanāśontarbhūtaḥ iya daśā yathākrama labhyate antardṛṣṭyā asyā asti karuṇā yā ayavahitahetutva vajati athavā nigaḍā nāśa yānti asyārthaḥ  vidveṣaḥ tathā a vidveṣasamparkitanigaḍā vināśa yānti sa sasāracakramiti mūlanāśa paśyatiyataḥ sa karuṇayānvitaḥ san dūṣāṇasvarūpasasāracakrabhittimūlasya tathākathita nāśapaśyati aguttaranikāya ṭīkā savādeṣu daśavidhā niaḍā sayojana ucyante te nigaḍāḥ sasāracakreṇa saha jana badhnanti tathā hi  vyaktitvasya mithyā dṛṣṭiḥsaśayaḥyāgādiśāstrānuṣṭhāneṣu āsaktiḥindriyākāṅkṣākrodhaḥrūpajagate ākāṅkṣārūpahīnajagate ākāṅkṣāpadasthitisacetanatāmohaḥ avidyā ca yataḥ arhatpuruṣeṇa ete nigaḍāḥ apasriyantetataḥ tena sasāracakrīyasamagrabhittimūlanāśaḥ upadhā kriyate anena paunaḥpunikaduḥkhādiyuktapunarnavīkṛtajanmanaḥ kāraṇa nāvaśiṣyate vividhāsu ṭīkāsu ālocitānā dūṣaṇānā parityāgāya spaṣṭopāyadvayamullikhati ṭīkā tathā hi  antardṛṣṭidvārā dūṣaṇānām unmūlanena sthāyiparityāgasyopāyaḥ samucchedappahāna samādhidvārā dūṣaṇānāmavadamanena asthāyiparityāgasyopāyaśca vikkhammanappahāna prathama bhāṣyamarhatpuruṣa nirdiśati avyavahitakāraṇatvena aparimeyakaruṇayā saha antardṛṣṭi pālayati sakṣepeṇasa karuṇāyā upari dhyānena dhyānamagnatāparyāya yāvat samādhi pālayitvā sthāsyati  tataśca dhyānamagnadaśyāyā utthāya sa cittasya ca śarīrasya ca viśiṣṭān tathā sāmānyān guṇān praveṣṭu guṇān praveṣṭu tadīya sutīkṣṇa citta  niyojayati   pariṇāme cittasya ca śarīrasya ca pratyeka viṣayamasthāyina parivartanaśīla tathā anirbharayogya paryavekṣya tasya citta svabhāvataḥ tasya  nirvāṇasyānusandhāna karoti yat sarvavidha pārthiva parivarttana tathā asthāyitvamatikramya vartate   parivartanaśīla jagat tathā parivartanahīna nirvāṇamadhikṛtya gabhīrāyāmantardṛṣṭau sañjātāyāmindriyākāṅkṣādimānasikanigaḍaiḥ bandhanasya  prāvaṇya dūrībhavati  yāḥ sarvāḥ pratikriyāḥ cira parityaktavyāḥ tāsā na samarthana karotyaya navāviṣkṛtaḥ bodhaḥ dvitīyā vyākhyā savāde ullikhita kamapi jana viśliṣyati yasya kevalamaparimeya premāsti īdṛśo janaḥ sampūrṇa kintu alpakāla vidveṣamūlakasarvaviṣayebhyo muktastiṣṭhati atra vidveṣambandhinigaḍāḥ vidveṣasambandhyāhitakaramānasikadoṣān nirdhiśanti tathā hi  asūyāsañjayaḥ udvegaśca visuddhimagga  yadā buddha āhasa sasāracakrīyadūṣaṇarūpabhittimūlasya tathākathita vināśa paśyati tadā sa samāhitapremṇā dūṣaṇānāmasthāyi avadamana nirdiśati abhyāsakāriṇo dūṣaṇāni dhyānamagnadaśāyāḥ paramapi dṛṣṭigocaratā gantumarhanti tathāpi premadhyānakāle dhyānamagnapuruṣaḥ tadīyadūṣaṇānā samīkṛtāvadamanena saha tṛptikara parama sukhamanubhavati  aparimeyapremapoṣaṇāt sontardṛṣṭimaktaye bhittimūlatvena īdṛśamānasikāvasthādvārā athavā īdṛśamānasikāvasthāsañjātaparamasukhabhogadvārā upakṛto  bhavati  kramikavacaneṣu ekādaśalābhaviṣayakedhyāye gotamaḥ ekādaśasakhyakānā lābhānāmekā sūcī dadāti yo janaḥ premarūpamanomukti sādhayati sa janaḥ tān lābhānarjayati prāguktāṣṭalābhaiḥ saha sayojanametat  sa śīghra tasya citta samāhita karoti tasya varṇa ujjvalo bhavati sa nirudvegena mriyate aguttaranikāya  niḥsandehena etat sarvalābhakāraṇāt gotamaḥ punarapi upadiśati yat cāndrāyaṇavrateṣu uposathamahatāmācāryāṇā śiṣyāḥ sareṣā bhūtānā kṛte premakaruṇānvitāparimeyahṛdayavikāśāya abhyastā āsan aguttaranikāya brahmā karuṇāpremasahānubhūtānandasamavṛttitvabhāvān karṣati ca pālayati ca majjhimanikāya aguttaranikāyaṭīkā tasmāt jīvaddaśāyā prāguktabhāvānā karṣaṇameva brahmasāyujyārjaāya rītiviśeṣaḥ gotama imā rīti varṇayati  vāseṭṭhakaścit bhikṣuḥ karuṇāsahānubhūtānandasamavṛttitānvitacittena satatamekasyā diśi sattāvadbhiḥ bhūtaiḥ saha sambandhitaḥ tiṣṭhati tathā ca dvitīyasyā tṛtīyasyā caturthyā ca diśiupariadhaḥ pārśvāpārśvi ca tādṛśamācarati sa sarvatra viśvabhūtaiḥ saha sambandha sthāpayati samabhāvena  premamayacetasāyatra cetaḥ tiṣṭhati nirākulavairānmuktaviśāla vistṛta tathā aparimeyam vāseṭṭha ekaḥ śaktiśāliśaṅkhavādakaḥ svalpaceṣṭayā catasṛṣu dikṣu pratidhvani sraṣṭu śaknoti sma tatra parimeya karma na parimeya tiṣṭhati karuṇāsahānubhūtānandasamavṛttitānvitamanomuktisādhanena tādṛśī avasthā jāyate vāseṭṭha ayameva brahmasāyujyamārgaḥ dīghanikāya punaśca eko bhikṣuḥ ekasyā diśi yathā uttarasyāmsattāvadbhiḥ bhūtaiḥ saha satata samparka sthāpayati premamayacetasā tadvat dvitīyasyā tṛtīyasyā caturthyā ca diśiupariadhaḥpārśvāpārśvi ca samparka sthāpayati sa samabhāena sarvatraviśvabhūtaiḥ saha sambandhitastiṣṭhati  premamayacetasā  yatra cetaḥ nirākulavarānmuktaviśālavistṛta tathā aparimeyam vāseṭṭha ekaḥ śaktiśālī śaṅkhavādakaḥ kevala svalpaceṣṭayā catasṛṣu dikṣu pratidhvani sraṣṭu śaknoti sma tatra parimeya karma na parimeya tiṣṭhati premamayamanomuktisādhanena sadṛśī avasthā jāyate vāseṭṭha ayameva brahmasāyujyamārgaḥ yadā prāguktopadeśānusārataḥ premādayaḥ kṛṣyante tadā te eva udāttā bhāvā ucyante aguttaranikāya savādeṣu ādyasakalanacatuṣṭāye karuṇāpremasahānubhūtānandasamavṛttitānā lakṣaṇāni na kṛtāni tathāpi ṭīkābhiḥ viśuddhimārgeṇa ca teṣā viṣayāṇā lakṣaṇāni tathā vyākhyānāni kṛtāni pratyekodāttabhāvasya spaṣṭavaiśiṣṭyāstīti kāraṇāt ekasmin bhāve upasthite apareṣā bhāvānāmanupasthitirgamyate paradūhkadūrīkaraṇāya karuṇāyā bhaktirūpa vyaiśiṣṭyamasti paraduḥkhakātaratā eva karuṇāyāḥ karma visuddhimagga karuṇāyāḥ dhyānātmaka karṣaṇa hisāpratirodhāya viśeṣeṇa phalapradam visuddhimagga sahānubhūtānandasya prītiprada lakṣaṇam asti visuddhimagga anasūyā eva tasya karma visuddhimagga  sahānubhūtānandasya dhyānātmaka karṣaṇa hi asantoṣapratirodhāya viśeṣataḥ phalapradam visuddhimagga samavṛttitāyāḥ samamanobhāvāpanna lakṣaṇamasti visuddhimagga  yo manobhāvaḥ sacetanajīveṣu tiṣṭhati samabhāvena sarvajīvadarśanameva samavṛttitāyāḥ karma visuddhimagga samavṛttitāyāḥ dhyānātmaka karṣaṇa nāma rāgapratirodhāya viśeṣataḥ phalapradam samavṛttitārūpa udātto bhāvaḥ samavṛttitānubhavāt pṛthak pūrvatra sacetanajīvaviṣayikī nirapekṣatā varttate kintu paratra na sukhasyana vā duḥkhasyānubhūtiṣṭhiṣṭhatiyā sacetanamanasaḥ vividhāsu daśāsu sahacaro jāyate visuddhimagga  eteṣā caturṇā bhāvānā karma khalu janapreṣaṇamūlakam  parama jyotiḥ sāra dadāti  sarve jīvā etebhyo duḥkhādibhyo muktā bhavantu evavidhayā cintayā paraduḥkhakaṣṭadūrīkaraṇāya ākāṅkṣādaśā  hi karuṇā  sarve jīvāḥ sukhino bhavantu evavidhayā cintayā sukhahitasādhanāya ākāṅkṣādaśā hi prema yūyamānandamanubhavatha ida sādhu yat yūyamānandamanubhavatha idamatīva sādhu  iti cintayā satata parasukhahitasādhanecchādaśā eva sahānubhūtānandaḥ atītakarmaphalakāraṇādeva janasya sukhāni ca duḥkhāni ca bhavanti iti cintayā parasukhaduḥkhaviṣayikī abhijñatā eva samavṛttitā caritracitraṇeṣu ca sārasagraheṣu ca virodhābhāso dṛśyate tathā hi  prema paramaṅgalasādhanāya bhaktitvena lakṣyate prema hi sukhasādhanecchādaśā atra karmapratiśrutirgramyate tathāpi sarve sukhino bhavantu itīcchāyā premṇaḥ sārarūpa vartate  yatra karmapratiśrutibhāvanayā prayojana nyūnameva dṛśyate sambhavatotra heturhi eva bhavitumarhati yathā  savādeṣu ullikhitāḥ premakaruṇāviṣayakopadeśāḥ kevala dhyānayogena eteṣā bhāvānāmanuśīlana nirdiśanti ata eva upadeśāḥ kevala sarve sukhino bhavantu sarve duḥkhānmuktā bhavantu evavidhecchānuśīlanamāvahati premakaruṇādhyāna ca pareṣā kṛte ānuṣaṅgika karma cāntarā kopi sambandhaḥ gotamena kadāpi noccāritaḥ tathāpi ida gamyate yat eteṣā bhāvānā karṣaṇena dhyānino janasya bhrātrīyakarmaṇā prakṛtau tathā paridhau parivarttana sūcyate yobhyāsakārī samāhitasārvalaukikapremakaruṇānuśīlana karotisovaśyameva janahitasādhanāya gabhīra vicalito bhaviṣyatītyatra na kopi vyaktikramaḥ premamayakarmaṇā ca saralāyāḥ karuṇāśca sahānubhūteścopari ye upadeśāḥ santiteṣu premakaruṇayoḥ karmamayī dik varṇitā eteṣāmupadeśānā bindumātra vastu apina dhyānamūlake prasaṅge sīmitam eṣu upadeśeṣu gotamaḥ sāmājikakarmapreṣaṇāmupadiśati iti gamyate tatra premakaruṇāsavādeṣu dharmīyajīvanasya adhikacintāmūlakabhāvasya gurutva na laghu āsīt tathāpi gautamena tannollikhitam  yadi duḥkha jāyate tarhi karuṇā mithyā bhavati visuddhimagga yadyapi kevala duḥkhaprakāśena karuṇātmakatā prakāśyatetathāpi karuṇāyā tādṛśī avasthā nāsti sarve duḥkhānmuktā bhavantu kevalamevavidhā icchā karuṇāyā tiṣṭhati paraduḥkhenābhibhūtāḥ santaḥ vaya parān sāhāyya na kurmmaḥ ekataḥ hṛdayahīnatā anyataśca paraduḥkhena vihvalatā anayormadhye duḥkhamantareṇa yatnasya vikalpo vartate karuṇākarṣaṇakāle jātaduḥkhadūrīkaraṇāya abhyāsakārī satata sacetanaḥ syāt sa prathamataḥ atiduḥkhārtajanamadhikṛtya icchati sa duḥkhamukto bhavatu iti tataḥ sa priyajanāyanirapekṣajanāya śatrusthānīyajanāya ca karuṇā karṣati visuddhimagga  yadi śatrujanaviṣayamadhikṛtya praśno jāyate tarhi prāyukta pratiṣedhaka prayujyate karuṇā yathā udāttabhāvarūpā bhavati tathā karaṇāya abhyāsakārī karuṇā samīkuryātdṛḍhīkuryāt sāmānyīkuryācca idamullekhārha tat pālisavādeṣu ṭīkāsu ca premaśabdo yamartha sūcayatiāgalabhāṣāyā premaśabasyārthaḥ tasmāt pṛthak savādeṣu prema na dāmpatyapremāthavā laiṅkikaprema kasmiścit gurutvapūrṇe savāde gotamaḥ yathāyatha dāmpatyasamparka vyākhyāti yat svāmī tadīyā striya sevetastrī api tataḥ para ta prati sahānubhūtiśīlā bhavet udāttabhāvarūpapremakarṣaṇāya viparīta liṅga prati premṇaḥ prakāśo na karttavya ityupadeśaḥ navadīkṣitebhyo dīyateyataḥ tathā kṛte prema sukhena tṛṣṇātvena pariṇata bhavati visuddhimagga  abhyāsakārī sarvadā āsaktiparihārāya avahitaḥ syāt anyathā premavikāśo yathāyatha na bhavati visuddhimagga yatna kṛte ida sambhavati dhyātā prathamataḥ ātmāna prati kramaśaḥ premakarṣaṇena premaparidhi vistṛta karotitataḥ śraddheyamācārya pratimitra pratinirapekṣajana prati pariśeṣe ca śatrujana prati tasya lakṣya bhavet samāhitasārvalaukikaprema tataḥ sovaśyameva ida samīkuryātdṛḍhīkuryāt tathā vistṛtīkuryāt tatra sārvalaukika prema ātmaparabheda na karoti visuddhimagga sahānubhūtānandasyārthaḥ pareṣā sāphalye prītimayatā yadātra parihāsaḥ mattatā vā vartate kopi vā yadā parasāphalyena ātmavismṛto bhavati tadā sahābubhūtānando bhithyā jāyate visuddhimagga yathāsambhava hitakaramanaḥpakṣe suṣamatayā prayojanamasti parasāphalyetisasattivaśataḥ suṣamatāyā hānirjāyate sā hāniḥ ahitāya bhavati eva viśuddhābhyāsāt vicyutirbhaviṣyati sahānubhūtānandakarṣaṇāya priyamitrasya gatamāgatamanāgata vā sāphalyamadhikṛtya ānandakarṣaṇamārabhate viśuddhimagga tataḥ sa yathākrama nirapekṣajanasya ca śatrujanasya ca sāphalyamadhikṛtya sahānubhūtānanda karṣati eva premakaruṇākṣetre yat kriyate tadapi ānuṣaṅgikaparyāyeṣu sa karoti samavṛttitā parasukhaduḥkhadarśanena sampūrṇasuṣamacittatā kevala dhyānamagnatāyāḥ caturthe paryāye samavṛttitāyāḥ karṣaṇa bhavati visuddhimagga dhyātāraḥ samavṛttitākarṣaṇāyānupreṣitā bhavantiyataḥ te ādyodāttabhāvatraye kiñcinmanda phala paśyanti teṣu udātteṣu bhāveṣu pratyekabhāvaḥ dhyānamagnatāyā ādyeṣu triṣu paryāyeṣu anyatame paryāye kṛṣyate visuddhimagga sarve janāḥ sukhino bhavantu evavidhecchāpoṣaṇena sacetanajīvakṛtāmodeṣu udvegastiṣṭhati ādyodāttabhāvatraya tādṛśena udvegena anvito bhavati viśuddhimagga kintu samavṛttitā tādṛśenodvegena muktā kiñca ādyodāttabhāvatraye anumodanasya vā vidveṣasya vā vyāpārastiṣṭhati visuddhimagga premṇaḥ rakṣāvaśyameva karaṇīyā anyathā prema āsaktyā vipariṇamyate karuṇāpi yathāyatha rakṣitavyā anyathā karuṇā pareṣāmavasthāsu vidveṣeṇa vā duḥkhabhāvena vā vipariṇamyate eva sahānubhūtānandaḥ mattatājanako bhavitumarhati samavṛttitayā saha tulanāyā kṛtāyā mandaphalatvena uktavipattayo dṛśantetathāpi samavṛttitāyāḥ evavidhena upāyena rakṣayā prayojana nāsti avaśeṣe ādyodāttabhāvatraya sukhānubhavena sahānvitamyataste bhāvā vairāthisāyāḥ asantoṣāt ca mukterupāyā eva te sarve punaśca duḥkhena api yuktāḥ visuddhimagga   dhyānamagnatāyāścaturthe paryāye samavṛttitārūpodāttabhāvena saha yaḥ samavṛttitānubhavastena saha tulanāyā kṛtāyā dhyānamagnatāyāḥ ādyaparyāyatrayasañjāta  parama sukha sthūlameva dṛśyate  samavṛttitā mithyā bhavati yadi tatra kevala jñānahīnatā vartete visuddhimagga samavṛttitāyā yathāyatha kṛṣṭāyā satyā iyamupalabdhirjāyate yat anye janāsteṣā karmaṇā kartāraḥ evañca teṣāmuttarakālīnā avasthā varttamānakarmaṇā nītigatā dṛṣṭibhaṅgī prativimbiyiṣyati visuddhimagga yadā dharmaḥ suphalāya kalpateḥ tathaiva adharmaḥ viparītaphalāya sampadyate visuddhimagga apare janāḥ pariṇāme sveṣā bhāgyāya bhāra niścitameva grahīṣyanti eva ca abhyāsakārī tasya bhāgyāya bhāra grahīṣyatietadviṣayamadhikṛtyāvahitaḥ san dhyātā puruṣaḥ amaṅgalajanakamano bhāvāt tathā paravyavahāragatavidveṣāt tadīya manaḥ mukta karoti tathā ca sa dhyānamagnatāyāḥ caturthe paryāye hitakāriṇī paksapātahīnatā poṣayati samavṛttitārūpodāttabhāvakarṣaṇāt prāgeva abhyāsakārī dhyānamagnatāyāḥ tṛtīya paryāya yāvat aparodāttabhāvānāmekatama poṣayet viśuddhimagga sa samāhitadaśāyā utthāya svābhāvikanirapekṣajana ca mitra ca śatru ca adhikṛtya samavṛttitā pālayati paravartiparyāyeṣu sa pūrvavadācarati yadā sonena bhāvena dhyānamagnatāyai sāgraha ceṣṭaye tadā avaśyameva caturtha paryāya gacchati ayameva kevala vyatikramaḥ iayamevodāttabhāvasya prakṛtiḥ tā prakṛtimavabudhya vaya śaṅkhavādakasya prāguktāmupamā pratigantu śaknumaḥ ṭīkā viśliṣyati  vāseṭṭhakaścit śaktiśāliśaṅkhavādaka āsīta evañca kaścit durbalaḥ śaṅkhavādakaḥ śaṅkhavādanakāle catasṛṣu dikṣu pratidhvani sraṣṭu samartho na bhavati sa sarvatra pratidhvanivistārāya nālam anyataśca śaktiśālī śaṅkhavādakaḥ sarvatra dhvani vitanitu śaknoti kṛṣṭamanomuktidvārā asmin prasage yā karuṇā yadā karuṇāprasaga āyātitadā praveśaparyāyagatā karuṇā athavā sthāpanāparyāyagatā karuṇā viṣayopayoginī bhavati tathāpi yadā manomuktiprasaga āyātitadā kevala sthāpanaparyāyagatā karuṇā viṣayopayoginī bhavati yat karma ākāṅkṣāviṣaye vartate tat parimita karmetyucyate yat karma rūpayuktaviṣayaka rūpahīnaviṣayaka ca bhavati tat karma aparimeya karmetyucyate  parimeyakarmātikramaṇatvāt ida karma aparimeya karmetyucyate viśeṣeṇa sāmānyena ca catasṛṣu dikṣu sambandhavitānatvāt ida karma aparimeya  karmetyucyate  tasmin viṣaye na tiṣṭhatitasmin viṣaye na pratisṭhita bhavati ākāṅkṣāviṣayakamadaḥ karma rūpamaye vā rūpahīne vā karmaṇi cira na tiṣṭhati ida tatra pratiṣṭhita na bhavati kosyārthaḥ ākāṅkṣāviṣayakakarma rūpamaye vā rūpahīne vā karmaṇi āśraya na paśyati ātmanaḥ pratiṣṭāyai suyoga na prāpnoti kevala rūpamaya vā rūpahīnameva vā karma ākāṅkṣāviṣayakakarma vyāpnoti cātiśete ca idamātmanaḥ pratiṣṭhāyai suyoga prānoti mahāsamudra ivāya vyāpāraḥ mahāsamudraḥ kṣudra jalāśaya parābhūya ātmanaḥ avasara prāpya pratiṣṭhito bhavati ida rūpamida vā rūpahīna karma ākāṅkṣāviṣayakakarmaphala pārśve pakṣipati idameva brahmasāyujyāya kalpate dīghanikāyaṭīkā ṭīkā varṇayati yat karuṇā praveśaparyāyagatāmathavāsthāpanaparyāyagatā karuṇā sūcayati karuṇā samādhiparyāye dhyānamagnatāyā nimne eva athavā dhyānamagnatāparyāye yadyapi iya karuṇā savādeṣu vivṛtāyāḥ karuṇāyāḥ prakṛtena prayogeṇa saha sagacchatetathāpi manomuktitvena sthāpanaparyāyagatā karuṇaiva gamyate tādṛśa viśeṣaṇameva premṇā ca sahānubhūtānandena ca saha prayojyam samavṛttitayā sahāpi prayojyam samavṛtitā sacetanajīvānadhikṛtya samānamānasikatārthe prayujyate  yathā kaścit śaktiśālī śaṅkhavādakaḥ svalpaceṣṭayā catasṛṣu dikṣu pratidhvani sraṣṭumarhati tathaiva kaścidabhyāsakārī manomuktikarṣaṇena catasṛṣu  dikṣu vartamānaiḥ jīvaiḥ saha sambandhenānvito bhavitumarhati  yadā śaktiśālī śaṅkhavādakaḥ catasṛṣu dikṣu pratidhvani bhavati śabdāntaraiḥ kathyatena kimapi sthānamasti yatra śabdaḥ na śrūyate karuṇādimanomuktikṣetreṣu api tādṛśī avasthā lakṣyate kintu asya vyāpārasya korthaḥ prathamataḥmānasikīmavasthāmadhikṛtya ida sagurutva smartavya yat ekṭibhiṭi iti pada pāliḥ kammalaāgalakarmacetanā inṭenaśan sūcayati visuddhimagga karma ityasya sthale cetanā ityasya sthāpanena ṭīkāyāḥ sthāna pariṣkṛta jāyate durbalena śaṅkhavādakena sṛṣṭa parimeya śabdaplāvanamiva ākāṅkṣāviṣayikī cetanā parimeyā bhavati yadā kaścinnaraḥ dhyānamagnatāmarjayatitadā manaḥ dhyānamagnatāyāḥ ādyaiḥ caturbhiḥ paryāyaiḥ yukte rūpamaye jagati tiṣṭhatiathavā samādhigatamahattārāvasthayā saha yukte sūkṣmatare rūpahīne jagati vartate yata udāttabhāvaiḥ saha yuktā mānasikī avasthā dhyānamagnatāyā ādyeṣu caturṣu paryāyeṣu tiṣṭhatitataḥ sāvasthā rūpamayajagat eva rūpamayaviṣayikī yā mānasikī avasthā tayā sahānvitā cetanā rāgādibhāvebhyaḥ sarvathā muktā bhavatiye rāgādibhāvā manaḥ badhnanti sṛjanti ca parieyatā sīmā vā  sā cetanā aparimeyetyucyate kiñca udāttabhāvakarṣaṇaratobhyāsakārī vṛddhiviśeṣeṇāthavā kramaśaḥ pratyeka diśi sattāvad bhūteṣu tān vitanotiathavā sāmānyena yugapat sarvatra tān vitanoti visuddhimagga eva caitanyāgataviṣayāṇā pariprekṣite abhyāsakāriṇaḥ cetanā aparimeyā jāyate yadā aparimeyā karuṇācetanā vartatetadā parimeyā ākāṅkṣāviṣayikī cetanā na tiṣṭhati  samudrasya ca puṣkariṇyāśca rūpakalpam ullikhya ṭīkā yadeva parimeya karma tat tatra prasage na tiṣṭhati iti vacanasya aparamartha nirdiśati yadi kaścit janaḥ tasya jīvanasya kasmiscit samaye udāttabhāvānāmanyatama karṣatitarhi tasya mṛtyau etadbhāvānvitacetanā sārthakatāmāyāti tathā brāhmaloke tadīyapunarjanmane kalpate tasmin samaye kimapi parimeyamākāṅkṣāviṣayagata karma sārthaka na bhavati eva brāhmaṇyaloke punarjanmane udāttabhāvānā prabhāvaḥ pratiṣṭhitaḥ  iya vyākhyā dhyānamagnatāyāḥ paryāye karuṇādimanomuktikarṣaṇaphalānāmantarbhāvāya śaktiśāliśaṅkhavādakasya upamāyā vāstavamavasara vitanoti savādasyopasahāre gotama āha yat yo naraḥ prāguktopāyena udāttabhāvacatuṣṭaya karṣatisa strīsasargavairopadravamānasikadūṣaṇebhyaḥ muktaḥ bhaviṣyati tathā ca sa manobalamarjayati brāhmaguṇasampannoya janaḥ maraṇāt para brahmaloka gacchati yadā premakaruṇāsahānubhūtānandaḥsamavṛttitā ca caturvidhānāmupadeśānā rītimanusṛtya kṛṣyante tadā te guṇā udāttā bhāvā iti kathyate brahmavihāraaguttaranikāya śabdataḥ udāttā bhāvā hi jīvanayātropāyāḥ vihārabrahmavat devatāḥbrahmā athavā te bhāvāḥ jīvanayātrāyā utkṛṣṭā upāyāḥ visuddhimagga pratyekodāttabhāvaḥ krodhahisādyahitakaradoṣaghnogadaḥ eva sarve catvāro bhāvā abhyāsakāriṇe hitāya bhavanti  yadyapi nirdiṣṭe samaye kaścit dhyātā eka bhāvamupakāraka matvā tatra gurutvamāropayitum arhati gotamaḥ karuṇābhūtakṛṣṭabhāvasya sārvikeṣu  lābheṣu gurutvamāropayati yataḥ karuṇāsamṛddhakarmāṇi tathā sahānubhūtimadhikṛtya tasya sarve upadeśāḥ karuṇayā saha samparkitāḥ karuṇāyā kācid vṛddhiḥ paravarttidvaya sajīvīkaroti arthāt samagradharmīyajīvanasya preṣaṇā ca prakāśanā ca samṛdhyā bhūṣayati catvāra udattā bhāvā vā brahmavihārā vā samavṛttitāyā manastattvasammatalābhān pratibimbayantiyeṣu ādyatraya tulyapadatva bhajatikintu samavṛttitāyāḥ pada mahattamam ekasyā ṭīkāyā teṣā vikāśasya kramaḥ pradarśitaḥ pitarau tayoḥ santānānā kṛte yān bhāvān anubhavataḥ taiḥ bhāvaiḥ saha udāttabhāvānā tulanā kriyate yadā śiśuḥ garbhasya madhye vartatetadā karuṇāmayacetasā pitarau kadā vā sarvāvayavānvita svāsthyavanta putra drakṣyāvaḥ ititataḥ yadāya komalaḥ śiśuḥ pṛṣṭhadeśe śeteyūkamakṣikādibhiḥ daśanāt athavā nidrāvyāghātakāraṇāt roditi vilapati vātadā tat śrutvā pitarau sādharaṇī karuṇāmanubhavataḥ  kiñca atīva ākāṅkṣaṇīyavarṣeṣu yadā krīḍākāle śiśuḥ dhāvati athavā viśrāma labhate tadā tadālokya pitroḥ manaḥ śata utkṛṣṭaviśuddhanavanītasiktatūlanirmitakomalakandukā  iva komala bhavati  pitroḥ citta paritṛpta cānandita ca bhavati tadā tayoḥ sahānubhūta ānando jāyate tataḥ yadā putraḥ tasya bhāryāyai bhūṣaṇāni dātu śaknoti tathā ca svakīye gṛhe vasatitadā pitarau samavṛttisampannau santau arthāt samacittatāmavalamba cintayataḥ adhunā āvayoḥ putraḥ svādhinaḥ san sthātumarhati iti eva tau tasmin samaye samavṛttitāmarjayataḥ aguttaranikāyaṭīkā eva vidhenopāyenayobhyāsakārī udāttān bhāvān karṣatisa prathamataḥ karuṇā poṣayati asmin samaye sa sacetanajīvebhyo hitamicchati visuddhimagga tataḥ yadā sa paśyatiśṛṇoticintayati yat te jīvā duḥkhādhīnāḥ visuddhiagga  tadā sa paraduḥkhaūrīkaraṇāya anurāgarūpa prema karṣati yataḥ ayamanurāgaḥ dhyānamagnadaśāyā kṛṣyateabhyāsakārī karmāpekṣayā bhāvavikāśāya samāhito bhavati  karuṇākarṣaṇena abhyāsakārī yebhyaḥ hitamaicchatteṣā duḥkha dūrībhavatu iti aicchat teṣā jīvānā samṛddhi yadābhyāsakārī paśyati disvā taā sa ānandito bhavati visuddhimagga atra paśyati ityasyārthaḥ  dhyātā vartamāne parasamṛdhi samīkṣate athavā atītasamṛddhi bhāvisamṛddhi vā cintayati visuddhimagga tasya cintā kevala vastugataviṣayeṇa sīmitā tiṣṭhati eva sahānubhūtānandakarṣaṇena abhyāsakārī pareṣā kṛte saśliṣṭānā bhāvānā nirmāṇa sapūrayati na kopi avaśiṣyate sa samavṛttitā kraṣṭumarhatisā samavṛttitā na samānamānasikatāsañjātabhaktiḥ sa nirapekṣadarśakaḥ san sarvān jīvān paryavekṣate visuddhimagga abhyāsakārī vyaktigatalābhāya tathā manastatvasammatalābhāya udāttabhāvānāmekatama pālayitumanu preṣito bhavati sa krodhādiviṣaghnāgadatvena prāguktabhāvacatuṣṭaya palayitu pravṛtto bhavati upadiṣṭavikāśakramaḥ maulikapratikriyācatuṣṭayādarśamanusarati  imamādarśa punaḥ punaḥ anusṛtya abhyāsakārī pareṣā kṛte ghaniṣṭha cintayitu pravartate tasya sāmarthyamapi samānamānasikatayā yukta jāyate ida niḥsaśayenocyate yat dhyānena udāttabhāvānā karṣaṇa hitakarapareṣā prakṛtāsu avasthāsu kṛtā pratikriyā prabhāvitā karoti tena prabhāveṇa pratikriyāyāḥ tīvratāupayuktatāsthāyitā ca parivartante gotamaḥ kadāpi na pratipādayati yat udāttabhāvaviṣayakāḥ caturvidhā upadeśā ekāntata tasyaiva yo janaḥ kevalam udāttabhāvānāmanuśīlana karoti sa sādhu na karoti  gotamaḥ spaṣṭataḥ muktaye aṣṭāṅgikamārgīyopadesaiḥ saha udāttabhāvānā kevalamanuśīlanasya vaiparītya pradarśayati   caturvidhopadeśānusāreṇa  karuṇādīnā kevalamanuśīlana parāṅmukhīkaraṇāya anāsaktayepraśāntyaivirāgāyapratyakṣajñānāyasamyagjñānāya nirvāṇāya ca hitakaratvamāvahatikintu kevala brahmaloke punarjanme kalpate  mamānuśīlana sampūrṇaviṣayavimukhatā sādhayati api ca tadanuśīlana viṣayāsaktityāge indriyabhogavirataupraśāntabhāvalābhe pratyakṣajñānārjanesamyag jñānārjanenirvāṇalābhe viśeṣataḥ asṭāṅgikamahāmārgāvalambane sahāyakatā vrajati  dīghanikāya udāttabhāvānā kevalamanuśīlana brahmaloke punarjanmane kalpate na tat cita dūṣaṇamukti vā punarjanmamukti kārayitumalam brahmādayaḥ api sakaṣṭajarāmṛtyupunarjanmanāmadhīnatā vrajanti aguttaranikāya  kevala buddhopadiṣṭamārgānusaraṇadvārā nirvāṇalābhāt kopi janaḥ pariṇāme nirvāṇaśāntau punarjanma parivartanaduḥkhādibhyo muktimarjayitumalam aguttaranikāya tathāpi sarve janāḥ kaṣṭanivāraṇāya gotamasya upadeśān grahītumasamarthāḥ santaḥ tebhyaḥ palāyante tatrāsamarthā janā anyathā upadiśyantetatra tu mahattama lakṣya na sādhyate ekadā brahmaloke punarjanmagrahaṇāya udāttabhāvānuśīlana kartavyamityupadeśaḥ sāriputtena dhānañjānināmakāya viprāya pradattaḥ majjhimanikāya tatkṣaṇādeva tathā kṛtvā maraṇāt para sa punaḥ brahmalokejāyata alokadṛṣṭyā gotama etatsarvamavagatya pratyāgata sāriputtamāha  sāriputtaapyekadā tvayā utthāya nikṛṣṭabrahmaloke pratiṣṭhito vipro dhānañjāniḥ parityaktaḥtasya tu adhikatarasādhanīyavastu āsīt  majjhimanikāya  sāriputto vyākhyāti yat tena sa brāhmaṇo brahmaloke pratiṣṭhāpito yato brahmaloko brāhmaṇebhya eva buddhasya praśno nirdiśati yat dharmācāryaḥ śiṣyasya kalyāṇārtha kadāpi paritṛpto bhavitu nārhati ācāryopi nirdiṣṭe samaye yathāsādhya śiṣya pramodayet yataḥ brahmaloke punarjanmagrahaṇamantardṛṣṭilābhānnikṛṣṭataramśiṣyo yadi paravartisamṛddhaye utsāhī bhavatitarhi saśliṣṭopadeśadānamācāryasya mukhya karttavyam gabhirāntardṛṣṭisampanno jano yadā udāttabhāvān karṣatitadā prāguktā doṣā na tiṣṭhantiyataḥ te tataḥ yathāyatha viṣaye kṛṣyante  gotamo varṇayati yat sādhāraṇajanakartṛkodāttabhāvakarṣaṇa ca mahata ācāryasya jñāninā śiṣyeṇodāttabhāvānā karṣaṇa cāntarā spaṣṭa pārthakyamasti aguttaranikāya yadā sādhāraṇo jana udāttabhāvān karṣatitadā sa maraṇāt para brahmaloke punareva jāyate kintu tatratyavāsānte sa punaḥ nārakajanatvenakṣudhārtapretatvena athavā paśutvena janma grahīṣyati aguttaranikāya  sarvavidhapunarjanmano muktamarhatpuruṣamantareṇa mahata ācāryasya udāttabhāvakarṣaṇarataḥ jñānī śiṣyaḥ maraṇāt para brahmaloke punaḥ  janiṣyate  kintu nirantarodāttabhāvānuśīlanāt sa tatra arhatpuruṣaḥ bhavati tasmin jīvane samāpti gate saḥ ataḥ para punaḥ na jāyatekintu amaranirvāṇasamudbhūtā nirāpattāmarjayati gautamasya karuṇā premasahānubhūtānandaḥsamavṛttitā ca samyagjñānalābhāt paramapi gautamaḥ caturvidhānāmupadeśānā paddhatimanusṛtyanirantara sarvavidhodāttabhāvacatuṣṭayasya karṣaṇa cakāra aguttaranikāya sarvabhāvacatuṣṭayakarṣaṇe buddha āsīt dakṣa iti sarveṣā nikaṭe spaṣṭamāsīt kasmiścit savāde gṛhastho jīvakakomārabhacca āha  bhadra  mayā śrutam brahmā karuṇayā vasatīti  brahmā eva bhāgyavān buddhaḥ aha spaṣṭataḥ paśyāmi yataḥ bhadra  bhāgyavān buddhaḥkaruṇayā vasati majjhimanikāya yata ida mata tiṣṭhati yat brahmaparyāyā devāḥ karuṇāpremasahānubhūtānanda samavṛttitā ca cakṛṣuḥjīvakaḥ gotama brahmā iti pratipādayatiyataḥ sa paśyati yat gotamaḥ karuṇayā vasati gotamaḥ prativadatijīvakalālasāghṛṇāmohadoṣaiḥ sa sadaikyavān kupito bhavati tadartha te doṣāḥ parityaktāḥmūlāt vicchinnāḥmūlavihīnāstālatarusamāḥ vinaṣṭāścate bhaviṣyati kāle udetu na samarthā bhaviṣyanti jīvaka etadviṣayamadhikṛtya yat tvayā ucyatetat mayā gṛhyate iti majjhimanikāya tataḥ jīvakaśca gotamaśca premasahānubhūtānanda samavṛttitā cādhikṛtya parasparāmālocanā cakratuḥ gotamo jīvaka jñāpayati yat lālasāghṛṇābhramadoṣaiḥ yadeva bhavatu vā na bhavatu hisāatṛptiḥ vidveṣapūrṇatā ca vihesāvantaarativantapaṭighavantanāśa gatāḥ eva buddhaḥ sagaurava jīvaka kathayati yat tasya karuṇādisamudayaḥ lālasāghṛṇābhramatyāgamapekṣya sañjātaḥ asmin savādegotamaḥ krodhahisāsantoṣavidveṣadoṣān premādīnā viparitā iti sthāpayati ṭīkāyā gotamasyoktiriya vyākhyātā  jīvakaeta viṣayamadhikṛtya yat tvayā ucyate tat yadi bhavati  jīvakamahān brahmāḥ avadamanātmakatyāgena krodhādīn tyajati sa tathā karunayā vasati aha nirākaraṇātmakatyāgena tān doṣān tyajāmi eta viṣayamadhikṛtya yat tvayā ucyate tat yadi bhavati tasyārthaḥ yadi ida prāguktiva bhavati tarhi aha te ukti gṛhṇāmi jīvakeneda mata gṛhītam tataḥ bhāgyavān buddhaḥ avaśiṣṭodāttabhāvānadhikṛtya tasmai prāguktā śikṣā vistareṇa dadau majjhimanikāṭīkā brahmā karuṇādīnāmantarāyān avadamanena parityajati samyagjñānalābhasamaye tu gotamena sarve mānasikā doṣā unmūlitāḥ eva karuṇādīnā karṣaṇasya samaye doṣāvadamanena prayojana nāsāditi kāraṇāt taddamanaceṣṭā tena na kṛtā antardṛṣṭikarṣaṇadvārā te sarve kārtsynyena nirākṛtāḥ antardriṣṭivikāśāya kaścit janaḥ prathamataḥ viśuddha vyavaharatisamādhi cāvalambate viśuddho vyavahāraḥ sarvadā prayojanīyamūlatva brajatiyena sosadācaraṇodbhūtānutāpāt mukto bhavitumarhati visuddhimagga viśuddho vyavahāraḥ vartamāne kāle hitakaramānasikatva poṣayatibhaviṣyati kālepi hitāramānasikatva sṛjati visuddhimagga  hitakaratvasamparkitasādhāraṇasasthānasya madhye eva avasthitaḥ san kopi janaḥ samāhitacittasya susaskṛtā avasthāḥ sthāpayitumāśānvito bhavitumarhati samādhiyogyeṣu catvāriśatsakhyakeṣu viṣayeṣu visuddhiagga  dhyānī jana ācāryopadeśamanusṛtya eka vā ekādhika vā icchati visuddhimagga tataḥ dhyānī puruṣaḥ manaḥdravyayoḥ sūkṣmaprakṛti praveṣṭhu yantratvena samādhiśāṇita manaḥ vyavaharati sontardaṣṭi karṣati antardṛṣṭimān abhyāsakārī yadi udāttabhāvānā samāhitāvasthāḥ karṣatitarhi saḥ abhyāsasya spaṣṭaviṣayatvena ubhayasmin viṣaye dakṣo bhavati tathāpi ubhaya viṣayamekatrīkṛtya sayuktābhyāsarūpeṇa sa kraṣṭu śaknoti atthakanagarīsavāde sasārī dasamaḥ ānanda pṛcchati buddhopadiṣṭaḥ ekamātraḥ abhyāsosti na veti yobhyāsaḥ manomukti sādhayatihānikara prabhāva vinaṣṭa karotibandhanāt ca anatikramaṇīyā mukti prasūte majjhimanikāya ānandaḥ ekādaśābhyāsān lakṣyasādhakān ullikhya uttara dadāti tatra ekatama hyevam   kaścit bhikṣuḥ satata premamayacittena ekasyā diśi avasthitaiḥ bhūtaiḥ saha samparka sthāpayatievañcadvittīyasyā diśi avasthitaiḥ bhūtaiḥ sahatṛtīyasyā diśi avasthitaiḥ bhūtaiḥ sahacaturthyā diśi avasthitaiḥ bhūtaiḥ saha evañca upariadhaḥpārśvāpārśvi avasthitaiḥ janaiḥ saha sa samparka sthāpayati sa samagraviśvasya bhūtaiḥ saha satata sarvatra samabhāvena samparka sthāpayati  karuṇāmayena cetasāyat cetaḥ sthiravairāt muktaviśālavistṛtamaparimeya ca tataḥ sa eva cintayati karuṇārūpamanomuktiriyamapi sañjāyate iṣyate ca yadeva sañjāyatethavā iṣyate tadeva asthāyitadeva virāmādhīnam  tasyaivamupalabdhirbhavati tatra pratiṣṭhitaḥ san sa hānikara prabhāvavināśa sādhayati yadi sa tatra karotitataḥ sa nimnaparyāyagatanigaḍapañcakanāśa karoti tataḥ svargaloke tasya svataḥ sañjāta punarjanma bhavati  prāguktā rītimanusṛtya antardṛṣṭi kraṣṭu dhyānī purusaḥ prathamataḥ svābhāvikenopāyena udāttabhāvānāmanyatama karṣati tataḥ sa etatsamāhitāvasthāyā uttiṣṭhatekintu dhyānamagnatāyā manasaḥ viśuddhatā prakṛtadhyānamagnadaśāyā para kañcit kāla tiṣṭhati visuddhimagga sa udāttabhāvapoṣaṇa tyajati tadā sa vastutattve tathā mānasatatte yādṛśī prakṛtirastitasyā anusandhānāya sapadi tīkṣṇa manaḥ niyojayati mānasaviṣayāṇā vividhāni kāryāṇi tiṣṭhanti tathā ca dehanirmāṇāya vastugatāni upādānāni santiteṣāmupāānānā kā prakṛtiḥ mānasakāryāṇā vā kā prakṛtiḥ anayoḥ madhye pārthyakyamanubhavati sobhyāsakārītathā hi  karuṇāyāḥ kopi bhāvaḥ bhūteṣu manaḥ sthāpanāya tathā manaḥpoṣaṇāya yuktastiṣṭhati tasmin bhāve siddhe ānandamaya utsāho jāyate antardṛṣṭimantareṇa sthāpana poṣaṇa tathā ānandamayotsāhabhāvaḥ  etāni trīṇi sahavartīni mānasikāni kāryāṇi manasaḥ avibhājyāḥ apṛgbhūtā daśā iva anubhūyante antardṛṣṭiyogāttāni kāryāṇi pṛthak pṛthak pratīyante visuddhimagga eva vidhamanusandhāna bahuṣu prasageṣu vividhamānasikakāryeṣu ca punaḥ punaḥ kṛtam visuddhimagga tadvat akhaṇḍavastunicayah vividhaiḥ upādānaiḥ nirmita iti abhijñatayā pratyakṣīkriyate tadā jīvaḥ vāhuḥśiraḥ ityādidhāraṇānā sthaleṣu kevala bhautikīmabhijñatā dhyānī janaḥ arjayati tatra sa kaṭhināśa komalāśa vāuṣṇāśa vā śītāśa vā pratyakṣīkaroti pūrvamakhaṇḍavastunicayatvena yat pratīta tadadhunā asavaddhabhautikābhijñatayā nirmitamiti dṛśyate vyaktisattā katibhiḥ vāstavaistathā mānasikaiḥ ghaṭakaiḥ dravyaiḥ nirmīyate teṣu dravyeṣu spaṣṭeṣu satsu teṣā sādhāraṇāni lakṣaṇāni prakāśante visuddhimagga tadā pṛthak pṛthak mānasika tathā vāstava ghaṭaka pratyakṣīkriyante kathamiva  parivartanaśīlamasthāyi asāra ca tatra kṣaṇāt kṣaṇāntara dravyagatā calamānatā nāsti eva tāni sarvāṇi asantoṣajanakāni dhyānī janaḥ pratyaha pratyakṣīkaraṇīyān viṣayān sākṣāt abhijñātu pravartate yataḥ abhijñāyamānā cetanāpi vināśaśīlātata ida spaṣṭa yat cetanāyāḥ kasmiścit kṣaṇe sampūrṇa vilīne sati aparacetanākṣaṇo jāyate visuddhimagga  vyaktisattāyā tathā pariveśe parivartanaśīleṣu asāreṣu dravyeṣu śaraṇasvarūpa sthāyinamātmāna nāvalokya dhyānī janaḥ sarvavidhagocaravastu  asthāyitvena duḥkhatvena pīḍātvenasphoṭakatvenabāṇatvenakṣobhatvenakleśatvenavijātīyatvenavilīyamānatvenaśūnyatvenasvārthahīnatvena paśyati aguttaranikāya eva vastutattvasya navabhāvena pratyakṣīkaraṇāt yogī svabhāvata eva mukti kāmayate sa imā mukti nirvāṇasya upalabdhau pratyakṣīkaroti tadā sa sarvavidhamasthāyitva ca parivartana cātikramya vartamānāyāḥ kasyāścidavasthāyāḥ sakṣiptaḥ jñāna labhate prathame antardṛṣṭigataprāthamikaparyāyeṣusamāhitacetasā anubhūtāyāḥ asamyaktāyāḥ sutīkṣṇapratyakṣīkaraṇena tasya susthitajagaddṛṣṭiḥ kiyatā parimāṇena viparyastā āsīt tataḥ nirvāṇasya upalabdhyā kā eva prakṛtā śāntiḥ iti viṣayamavagacchati paramā śaktimanubhūya sa tathaiva atilobhanīyapārthivākarṣaṇaiḥ na punaḥ pralubdhaḥ bhaviṣyati ekataḥ sarvastūnāmanirbharayogyatā tathā anityatā yathā spaṣṭāanyataḥtatahiva spaṣṭā nirvāṇasya nirāpattā dhyānī janaḥ satata samādhinā tasya cittamavaśyameva śāṇita kuryāt gabhīropalabdhisamṛddhaparyāyatrayamatikramya srotaḥpraveśī sannapi dhyānī satatameva antardṛṣṭi pālayet eva gocaravastūnāmasantoṣajanakaḥ svabhāvaḥ kramaśaḥ spaṣṭāt spaṣṭatara jāyate tadvat nirvāṇasya sāmagrikī viśuddhā prakṛtiḥ satatamadhikatamaspaṣṭatā vrajati arhatpuruṣasya phalalābhena antardṛṣṭiḥ sampūrṇā bhavati punarjanmanaḥ muktaḥ san maraṇāt para sa nirvāṇasya mṛtyuhīnāmavasthā labhate eva vidhenopāyenabhavacakrāt paramamuktaye bhittimūlatvena udāttabhāvasamūhaḥ vyavahriyate srotaḥpraveśinaḥ upalabdhyāpi abhyāsakārī yogī aparān janān antardṛṣṭimārgamupadeṣṭumarhati   pañcamodhyāyaḥ purāṇā prakṛtistathā prācīnatā ādhunike bhārate saskṛtavidyānuśīlanasyetihāse yadā vaya mudraṇayantrasya vartamāna  samunnata yuga praviśāmaḥ sma tadā bahuṣu ādyeṣu vastuṣu anyatama vastu prati vibudhānā tathā saskṛtapremiṇā manoyoga ākṛṣṭobhavat  saskṛtasāhityasya mahāgranthānā mudrākanena prayojane eva tat vastu nihita vartate saskṛtabhāṣayā viracita mahābhārata bhāratavarṣasya mahattamo granthaḥ samagre viśvepi asya mahattamattā prasiddhā tadgranthaprakāśanāviṣaye eva yugasya udyamasya ca garvaḥ sūcyate   tamakhṛṣṭābdāt  khṛṣṭābda yāvat samaye kalikātāsthaiśiyāṭiksosāiṭināmadheyasya pratiṣṭhānasya prasādāt paṇḍitaiḥ saskṛtamahābhārata  prakāśitam  asmāt prāk syārauiliyāma jonsmahodayena ātmanastathā pāścātyadeśasya kṛte saskṛtamāviṣkṛtam tena kālidāsakṛtasya ṛtusahārākhyasya kṣudrakāvyasya eka saskṛtamāviṣkṛtam tena kālidāsakṛtasya ṛtusahārākhyasya kṣudrakāvyasya eka saskaraṇa prakāśitam tadṛtusahāra varṇanāmūlaka gītikāvyam tatra prācīnabhāratīyaitihyānusāreṇa vastūnā varṇanā vartate  tame khṛṣṭābde vagīyākṣarayuktamṛtusahāra tena kalikātātaḥ prakāśitam kintu mahābhāratasya prathamasaskaraṇāt para bhārate tathā videśe vibudhamaṇḍalasyābhiniveśaḥ saskṛtavidyānuśīlane kendrībhūto babhūva mahābhāratasya prathama saskaraṇa vicāramūlaka nāsīt ida sāralyena kati pāṇḍulipīḥ anusṛtavatyāḥ sampādakaiḥ hastagatāḥ idameka sundara saskaraṇam ida bahubhirdarśakaiḥ asya abhiprāya pūrṇamakarot kintu anena yathārtha svanaḥ sūcitaḥ tataḥ asmābhiḥ jārmānasaskṛtapāṇḍityasūcaka viśāla tathā pradhāna sāhityakarma prāptam  yadā ilyāṇḍavāstavyo jārmānadeśīyaḥ paṇḍitaḥ myāksamūlāramahodayaḥ prathamameva ṣaḍbhiḥ khaṇḍaiḥ vibhakta sāyaṇabhāṣyasametamṛgveda sampādya  prakāśitavān  yo granthaḥ bhārate tathā indoiuropīyajagati prācīnatamaḥ   ida vicārasambalita prathama mudrita saskaraṇam  na kevala taddhastagatapāṇḍulipīnāmapitu anekajīvitapāṇḍulipīnāmarthād yaiḥbhāratīyapaṇḍitaiḥ akhilaḥ vedaḥ kaṇṭhasthīkṛtaḥ teṣā sāhāyyena  myāksmūlāramahābhāgaḥ vedasya viśuddha pāṭha pratiṣṭhāpayitu yatate sma  te paṇḍitāḥ pāṇḍulipīnā sāhāyyena pāṭhasya saśodhanāya myāksmūlāra sevante sma tataḥ paravastutaḥ bhārate tathā videśe paṇḍitaiḥ saskṛtaprakāśanasya gauravamaya itihāsa ārabdhaḥ kalikātāvāstavyo hemacandravidyāratnamahāśayaḥ vagīyapāṇḍulipimūlasya rāmāyaṇasyaika saskaraṇa prakaṭīkṛtavān  gasapāregoresionāmadheyaḥ iṭālīyapaṇḍitaḥ pyārīnagarītaḥ iṭālīyānuvādasametasya rāmāyaṇasyaika prathama vicārasambalita saskaraṇa vyaktīcakāra  ttamakhṛṣṭhābdāt  tamakhṛṣṭābda yāvat tasya kālaḥ bhārate tathā bhāratād vahiḥutkṛṣṭhapāṭhalābhāya paṇḍitaiḥ prabhūto yatnaḥ kṛtaḥ tadartha ca kati prakāśanālayā api pratiṣṭhitāḥ tadyathā kalikātāyā jīvānandavidyāsāgarapratiṣṭhitaprakāśanāsasthānamvārāṇasyā haridāsaguptakṛtā caukhambā saskṛtamālābombāinagaryā tukārāmajavajīcālitaḥ nirṇayasāgaramudraṇālayaḥpunāsthamānandāśramamudraṇagṛhamśrīragam ityasya vāṇīvilāsasamudraṇasasthānamtathā ca samagra bhārata vyāpya bahavo vikhyātāḥ prakāśanālayāḥ tataḥ eśiyāṭikasosāiṭiḥ anyāni pratiṣṭhānāni cāpi etādṛśa karma jagṛhuḥ tathā hi  eśiyāṭikasosāiṭidvārā vivliyothekāiṇḍikāsirijaḥ tena saha saskṛtaprakāśanātrivāndramasaskṛtasirijaḥmādrājasya eḍāra thiyojaphīkyāla sosāiṭiḥvāgaloraviśvavidyālayasya prakāśanāvibhāgaḥprāyeṇa bhārata vyāpya viśvavidyālayalagnāḥ sasthāḥ athavā anusandhānarupaśodhakārya viduṣā samājāḥ yatra kriyatetathā casaskṛtagranthaprakāśanālayāḥ etāni sasthānāni saskṛtasampadaḥ pracārāya sayuktāni saskṛtasāhityasya viśālatā vismaya sūcayati asya sāhityasya anyatama lakṣaṇīya vaiśiṣṭya nihitamasti purāṇeṣu upapurāṇeṣu ca mahābhāratād rāmāyaṇāt ca para teṣāmāgamanamabhavat   tame khṛṣṭābde punāsthā bhāṇḍārakaraprācyāvidyāgaveṣaṇāsasthā tatrabhavataḥ rāmakṛṣṇagopālabhāṇḍārakaramahāśayasya anupreraṇayā mahābhāratasya  vicārasameta saskaraṇa prakāśayitumudyoga lebhe  saskṛte ida karma mahadapūrva tathā ca bhārate prathameva vartamāna bhāratasya mukhyeṣu saskṛtapaṇḍiteṣu anyatamasya bhi esa sukṭhaṅkaramahodayasya haste asya karmaṇaḥ bhāraḥ samarpitaḥ sa purātanapāṭhasampādanārtha kati niyamān sasarja ye niyamāḥ sarvatra vibudhajagatā susthatvena śuddhatvena ca gṛhītāḥ  tasyodyoge upadeśe ca punāyāḥ bhāṇḍārakaraprācyavidyāgaveṣaṇakendrataḥ avaśeṣe mahābhāratasya apūrva viśleṣita saskaraṇa prakaṭībhūtam  ida bhāratīyavaidūṣyasyāpūrva nidarśanam  yatra ādhunikapaddhatyā sāhityavicāreṇa saha prācīnasaskṛtavidyāyāḥ ca pāṭhasampādanāyāḥ ca samanvayaḥ  sādhitaḥ  samagre bhārate ye hastalekhā āsanye ca bhāratād vahiḥ āsan  te sarve sagṛhītāḥ bhāratavahirbhūtaśyāmajābhādideśeṣu mahābhāratasya pāṭhāntaratvena ānuṣagika yat sāhitya prāpta tadapi prārthanādhīna kṛtam phalataḥ mahābhāratasya mahāsaskaraṇam mahādarśatvena gṛhītamabhavat aparaiḥ viśvavidyālayaiḥ sasthānaiḥ ca ayamādarśo gṛhītaḥ  rāmāyaṇasyānyāni saskaraṇāni antareṇāpi vālmīkīyarāmāyaṇasya vicārasambalita saskaraṇa mahābhāratapaktitaḥ barodāprācyavidyāgaveṣaṇāsasthānena  gṛhītam  āmedāvādastho gujarāṭaviśvavidyālayaḥ bhāgavatapurāasya kārya gṛhṇāti sma bhāratīyasaskṛtimukha khalu purāṇam bhārata jijñāsuḥ janaḥ purāṇebhyaḥ prayojanīya sāhāyya vāñchati prācīnakālādeva purāṇasammatā sabhyatā tathā saskṛtiḥpaurāṇiko dharmaḥpaurāṇika darśanampaurāṇiko viśvāsaśca bhūmaṇḍalasya sarvāsu dikṣu śraddhayā anumoditāni tathā svīkṛtāni ata eva purāṇānāmastitve yat calamānatva tat svaya siddhasatyatvena jātam ādhunikabhāratīyasamājopi purāṇānā bhittau ātmāna niyantu śaknoti vastutaḥ purāṇasamūhaḥ hi bhāratavarṣasya bauddhikapragateḥ nirantaro hetustathā protsāhako viṣayaḥ ādhunikamanveṣaṇa yadyapi darśayati yat atyalpasasthākāni vidyamānāni purāṇāni yuktyā prācīnakālīyānīti pratipādayantitathāpi purāṇasāhityasya mūla vaidikasahitāracanāyuge eva bhavitumarhati purāṇasya prācīnatama ullekhaḥ atharvavedasya mandradvaye lakṣyate yatraikatarasya ṛcāmiva samapavitramūlyatvam astīti ucyate sāmnā chandasā yajusāmiva purāṇānā samayo nitya samucyate anyatarakṣetre itihāsena sahāsyollekhaḥ kṛtaḥ vaidikasāhityasya bahuṣu grantheṣu itihāsena saha pṛthak vā ekatra vā purāṇasyollekhaḥ kriyate tathā hi  śatapathabrāhmaṇegopathabrāhmaṇejaiminīyopaniṣadijaiminīyabrāhmaṇetaittirīyāraṇyake bṛhadāraṇyakopaniṣadichāndogyopaniṣadisākhyāyanaśrautasūtreāśvālāyanagṛhyasūtre cetyādiṣu api ca anyeṣu prācīneṣu pavitreṣu ca grantheṣu api purāṇasya svīkṛtiḥ pratiṣṭhāpyate yathā  āpastambadharmasūtregautamadharmasūtrevyāsasahitāyām uśanāsahitāyāmmanusahitāyāmyāñavalvayasahitāyāmśavarabhāṣyeśāṅkarabhāṣyavātsāyayanabhāṣyetantravārttike cetyādiṣu yāskakṛtaniruktānusāreṇaṛgvedopi itihāsamiśramantramullikhati yaḥ punaḥ brahmaṇaḥ prakāratraye antarbhūtaḥ tasya mate purātana sat yat nūtana bhavati tadeva purāṇam prācīne yuge yadāsīt tadeva purāṇa purātana veti aṣṭādhyāyīti granthe pāṇininā uktam purāṇa yataḥ purātaneṣu divaseṣu jīvitamāsīt tataḥ tat purāṇamiti kathyate iti vāyupurāṇasya matam padmapurāṇa purāṇānāmanya vicitramartha paśyati te eva prācīnāḥ pāṭhā ye katicit parasparasavaddhākhyānāni vadanti prācīne kāle ida tathā abhavat tatasceda purāṇamityucyate  iti brahmāṇdapurāṇasya matam eva purāṇasya lakṣaṇeṣu viśleṣiteṣu eko viṣayaḥ spaṣṭo bhavati sarvatra purāṇāni prācīnanibandhairupetāni purāṇānā prācīnatve teṣu pavitreṣu pāṭheṣu na kopi sandeho vartate atra prasage itihāsa padena sahāsya sayogaḥ vicāryaḥ eva atharvavedasahitāyā tathā vibhinneṣu brāhmaṇeṣu itihāsaśabdasya paunaḥpunyena vyavahāro dṛśyate asyārthaḥ  dhruvamida savṛttam ittha vā ittha vedamāsīt eva pratibhātamida yat itihāsaḥ sambhavataḥ atītakālasya yathārtha savṛtta vṛttānta sūcayati ata eva purāṇamitihāsaśceti śabdadvaya na samārthajñāpakamiti anumīyate anyataśca teṣā vaiśiṣṭya tathā karmakṣetramapi sambhavataḥ pṛthak yāskasya mate devāpiśāntanukathāyām itihāsatvamasti vaiśvāmitrasudāsasya tathā paijavanapurohitasya kathāpi itihāsasya paryāya gacchati eva yadyapi itihāsaḥ purāṇa ca anyonyasambandhena ghaniṣṭha yujyatetathāpi purāṇeṣu kalpanābhāgo nātīva tātparyahīnaḥkintu itihāse asya paridhiḥ sīmitaḥ tathāpi dvayormadhye prācīna pārthakya na spaṣṭa na ca saralam tasmāt ekastathā sadṛśaḥ pāṭha ātmāna purāṇīyamiti svīkaroti anyatra ca punaḥ aya pāṭhaḥ itihāsatvena svīkriyate itihāsatvena vā itihāsottamatvena vā svīkṛta mahābhārata purāṇaśabdasagraharūpeṇa ātmanaḥ svīkṛti na tyajati aṣṭādaśamahāpurāṇeṣu anyatama khalu vāyupurāṇam ida gurutvapūrṇa purāṇamiti svīkriyate kintu tasmin vāyupurāṇe paktiviśeṣo dṛśyateyatrāsti  imamitihāsa paṭhan janaḥ mahat yaśaḥ lapsyatetasya jīvanamapi dharmayukta syāt iti etādṛśamapi brahmāṇḍapurāṇe śraddhayā udīritam ida yugapat purāṇa tathā itihāsaḥ ata eva vitarkabhayāt idamevocyate purāṇasyetihāsasya ca madhye bhedasya rekhā na sarvadā sukhabodhyā kauṭilyaḥ purāṇam itihāsāśa manyate tasya mate purātanī kathā ca varṇanā ca purāṇasya madhye tiṣṭhataḥ dharmaśāstramarthaśāstra cetihāse tiṣṭhataḥ atharvavede katipayeṣu purāṇeṣu cāpi purāṇasyetihāsasya madhye na kimapi pārthakya pratiṣṭhitam yathārīti pṛthivīarṇanāyāmatharvavedaḥ purāṇaśabda vyavaharati kintu tasmin vede vratānugamanaviṣaye itihāsaśabdasya prayogaḥ dṛśyate chāndogyopaniṣadaḥ ṭīkāyā śakarācārya ubhayoḥ madhye spaṣṭha pārthakya sūcayitu yatate sma tasya mate śatapathabrāhmaṇe ūrvaśī ca purūvāśceti dvayoḥ kathā vartate eṣā kathā viśuddhetihāsasyāntargatā kintu jagattatva prakṛtyā paurāṇikam  yatrocyate sṛṣṭeḥ prāk anastitvamabhūt tasmādanastitvāt ca krameṇa jagadāvirbhavati iti vastutaḥ śaṅkarācārya eva prathama dvayoḥ śabdayoḥ madhye spaṣṭa pārthakya darśayitu ceṣṭhate sma kintu tasya mata na sarvaiḥ gṛhītam mahān vaidikaḥ paṇḍitaḥ sāyaṇācāryaḥ asya prativāda cakāra tasya mate viparītamasya satyamiti śatapathabrāhmaṇe urvaśī purūravāḥ cetyanayoḥ yā kathā dṛśyate sā paurāṇikī prakṛti nirdiśati yataḥ tatra prācīnatama kiñcit vivṛtam sṛṣṭeḥ sūcanāyā kevala jalamāsītsarva jalamayamāsīt  etādṛśī uktiḥ niścitamasyāḥ sṛṣṭeḥ aitihāsikatva darśayati  eva dvayoḥ prasiddhayoḥ paṇḍitayoḥ madhye parasparavirodhimatapārthakye sati purāṇetihāsayoḥ madhye bhedarekhāyāḥ prāyeṇa viluptikaranameva  śreya ityasya kevala pramāṇam   sargapratisargavaśamanvantaravaśānucaritayuktasya pañcalakṣaṇasya purāṇasya sahata lakṣaṇa tathā purāṇasya nirdiṣṭa yugamapi purāṇānā  kṣetre na prayojyam yadyapi purāṇalakṣaṇa vividheṣu purāṇeṣu vivṛtamtathā caamarakoṣe tat dṛḍha samarthitam pañca lakṣaṇāni api antareṇa vicitrā viṣayāḥ prāyeṇa sarveṣu purāṇeṣu dṛśyante tathā hi  devatānetṛtvapavitrāṇi sthānānibahūni vratānivividhadānānā gurutvavistṛta bhaugolika vivaraṇādyam keṣāñcinmate dvayoḥ pārthakyamākhyānasya netṛṇā sakhyāyāḥ upari āśritya vartate yatra tetā eka eva tatra sa itihāsaḥ kintu yatra teṣā sakhyā ekādhikā tatra tat purāṇam tathāpi idamapi na samyak pratipādanīyam rājaśekhareṇa tasya kāvyamīmāsāyā dvividha itihāsaḥ iti kathitam ekaḥ parikriyeti paricīyate yatra kevalameka eva netāanyaśca purākalpanāmedhayā yatra bahavaḥ netāraḥ santieva tasya mate rāmāyaṇa parikriyāparyāya gacchatimahābhārata ca purākalpaparyāyam spaṣṭhataḥ rājaśekharasya mate itihāsasya paridhiḥ bindumātreṇāpi sīmitaḥ purāṇasya pañca lakṣaṇāni antareṇāpi purāṇasyānyaprakāra lakṣaṇa bhāgavatapurāṇe vāradvaya brahmavaivartapurāṇe sakṛt eva dṛśyate atra purāṇa daśalakṣaṇamiti smṛtam daśa lakṣaṇāni hi evam  sargaḥvisargaḥ vṛtiḥrakṣāantaramvaśaḥvaśānucaritamsasthāhetuḥ apāśrayaśca yata lakṣaṇāni purāṇānā kiñcit mahattva vaiśiṣṭya nirdiśatitata eteṣā vistṛtālocanā prayojanīyā prathama lakṣaṇa sarga iti paricīyate sargasyārthaḥ sṛṣṭiriti mūlaprakṛtau sattvarajastamasā kṣubdhadaśāyā satyā trividhāhasattā jāyate tataḥ pañcatanmātrāṇi pañcamukhyāni bhūtāni ca jāyante sṛṣṭeraya kramaḥ hi sargaḥ visargaḥ hi jīvajagataḥ sṛṣṭiḥ ekasmāt bījād yathā dvitīya jāyate tathā eko jīvonyasmān jāyate brahmā eva sṛṣṭeḥ kartā sa parameśvarasya prasādāt sṛṣṭisakrāntā sarvā śakti dhatte vṛttirhi gurutvapūrṇa vastu yena jīvaḥ prāṇasāram vibhartti nyūnatamataḥasya dṛṣṭigrāhyasya jagataḥ kati bhāgā vṛtyadhīnāḥ tiṣṭhanti naraḥ prāṇadhāraṇārthamannagodhūmadugdhaphalādīni vastūni gṛhṇāti punaśca katicit vastūni śāstraniyamapālanārtha tena gṛhyante rakṣā purāṇasya caturtha vaiśiṣṭyam sādhūnā paritrāṇāya tathā duṣkṛtā vināśāya īśvaraḥ vibhinneṣu yugeṣu sthāneṣu ca vahūni rūpāni dhatte sa āstikān rakṣatināstikānā ca vināśa karoti kintu idamīśvarasya prāyeṇa sāmānya karma mukhyobhiprāyo hi īśvarasya līlādharmi vacanam nara īśvarasya pavitrā līlāmanusaran tathā īśvara japan smaran mokṣa labdhu śaknoti mahāpurāṇasya pañcasu lakṣaṇesu yat manvantara kathyate tadeva antaram siddhāntaśiromaṇigranthasya gaṇanāyā anusāreṇa  varṣeḥ eka manvantara bhavati manvantarāṇi caturdaśa pratyeka manvantara manuviśeṣeṇa adhiṣṭhita vartate prāyeṇa sarvāṇi purāṇāni caturdaśamanūnā nāmaviṣaye tathā padaviṣaye aikamatya svīkurvanti te eva  svāyambhūvaḥsvārociṣaḥuttamaḥtāmasaḥraivataḥcakṣuṣaḥvaivasvataḥsāvarṇiḥdakṣasāvarṇiḥ brahmasāvarṇiḥdharmasāvarṇiḥ rudrasāvarṇiḥdevasāvarṇiḥindrasāvarṇiśca pañca manavaḥsaptavarṣayaḥdevaḥindraḥ mānavaśca eṣā manvantarāṇā pramāṇam purāṇānā paravartti vaiśiṣṭya vaśaḥ rājñaḥ sarve vaśā brahmaṇā sṛṣṭāḥ eṣā nṛpāṇā trikālīyavivaraṇamima paryāya gacchati bhāgavatapurāṇa vadati  rājñā brahmaprasūtānā vaśastraikālikonvayaḥ iti rājñā praśastita ida pratibhāti yat teṣāmatītakarmaṇāvarttamānakāryāṇā tathā bhāviviṣayāṇā gauravameva asya mukhyobhiprāyaḥ anyeṣā purāṇānā mate vaśaḥ na kevalaḥ rājavaśaḥanena ṛṣivaśopi budhyate ataḥ paramāyāti vaśānucaritam bhāgavatapurāṇa paryavekṣate yat vaśānucarita teṣā vṛtta vaśādharāśca ye kati pradhānā rājān ima paryāyamalakurvanti teṣā gauravamaya kārya vistareṇa atra varṇitam rājagauravagāthāyāmapi punaḥ anyāni purāṇāni prasiddhānā pradhānānā munīnāmantarbhuktimicchanti vastutaḥ puṇyaślokānā rājñā vivaraṇāni niḥsandehena ādarśavādasya utpattaye smaraṇīyāni kintu asmin prasage maharṣīṇā gututva na kadāpi laghumūlyatva vrajati yudhiṣṭhirahariścandrajanakādīnā caritrāṇi asaśaya divyāmanupreraṇā dadati kintu tasmin samaye vyāsavālmīkivaśiṣṭhādīnā svalpasakyākānāmavadānāni niḥsaśayena janānā bahūni kāryāṇi saskurvanti aṣṭama lakṣaṇa hi sasthāsajñakam iya pañcalakṣaṇasya purāṇasya pratisargeṇa saha sādṛśyamāvahati tathāpi viṣṇupurāṇe pratisargasya sthale samārthakaḥ pratisahāraḥ śabdaḥ gṛhītaḥ iya sasthā jagataḥ sampūrṇā vinaṣṭhi sūcayati pratikalpamanusṛtyeya vistareṇa varṇyate vartamānakalpasya nāma śvetavarāhakalpa iti aya  varṣairupetaḥ siddhāntaśiromaṇeḥ viśiṣṭagaṇanayā jñāyate yat akhilo viśvaḥ  varṣebhyaḥ para sampūrṇataḥ vināśa gamiṣyati ataḥ para hetureva eka lakṣaṇam aya hetuḥ sarvadā sṛṣṭihetūn jīvitān jīvān nirdiśati te jīvā ajñatayā bhrāntyā vā kati karyāṇi sādhayanti aya ca pariṇāme anyā sṛṣṭi nayati vastutaḥ viśvasya sṛṣṭeḥ vinaṣṭeśca mūlabhūto hetūḥ eṣā jīvānā bhāgyam ata eva te eva hetutvena tathā mūlakāraṇatvena svīkṛtāḥ antima vaiśiṣtyamapāśrayothavā āśraya iti paricīyate yat tattva samagratva vā vyakti sṛṣṭi vinaṣṭi vā nayati tadeva apāśrayabodhakam ayameva brahmā paramātmā vā ayamevaikaḥ kevala dhyātavyaḥ sarvāṇi nava vaiśiṣṭyāni daśamasya puṣṭaye kalpante bhāgavatapurāṇamanusṛtya daśamasya lakṣaṇasya saskārāya nava vaiśiṣṭyāni savistaramālocyante bhāgavatapurāṇamanyatra lakṣaṇadaśakasyānā sūcī racayati tatra daśa lakṣaṇāni hvevamsargaḥvisargaḥsthānampoṣaṇamūtiḥmanvantaram īśānukathānirodhaḥmuktiḥ āśrayaśca evamidamāyāti yat tṛtīyacaturthapañcama ca nāma nūtanam sthānampoṣaṇam ūtiḥ dvitīyasūcistha manvantara prathamasūcīsthasya antarasya samānam tathaiva vaśothavā vaśanucaritam īśānukathayā saha tulyārthakatva nayati apāśrayasya āśrayasya ca madhye kimapi pārthakya nāsti prathamasūcīsthā sasthā caturvidhā tathā hi  naimittikīprākṛtikīnityāātyantikī ca āsu catasuṣu ātyantikī sasthā dvitīyasūcīsthā mukti nirdaśatianyāḥ tisraśca nirodhasamānāḥ sthāna samagrasya viśvasya bhaugolika vivaraṇa dadāti janānā sakhyāabhyāsāḥ caritrāṇi cātra parighyante eva purāṇānuśīlane bhogoliko viṣayopi yugapat anena lakṣaṇena saha vartate poṣaṇa nāma īśvarāllabdhā karuṇā athavā tallabdhaḥ prasādaḥ jīvāḥ samagrasya viśvasya sṛṣṭaurakṣaṇeniyantraṇevināśe ca tasya īśvarasya asīmā śakti boddhu yatante te tā śakti boddhu śaknuvanti sa duḥkhamuktaye tebhyaḥ asīmā karuṇā dadāti ajāmīla āsīt madyapaḥpāpasaktaḥcaritrabhraṣṭaḥ ca kintu sopi īśvarasya cirantanānandād vañcito na babhūva ūtiḥ hi antima lakṣaṇam iya karmaprāvaṇya nirdiśati utkṛṣṭasya vā akṛṣṭasya vā kṛtakarmaṇaḥ phalādeṣā icchā jāyateevamūrtiḥ īśvarasya akṛtrimāyā karuṇāyā viruddhe pratyakṣameva daṇḍāyate ūtaye narāḥ īśvareṇa saha milanasyākāṅkṣā darśayitu vyarthā bhavanti ida pūrva darśita yat brahmāṇḍapurāṇamapi purāṇasya daśa lakṣaṇāni adhikṛtya ekā sūcī dadāti teṣu lakṣaṇeṣu santi  sargaḥvisargaḥsthitiḥkarmāvasāhaḥmanuvartaḥmanvantarampralayavarṇanammokṣanirūpaṇamvaśānucaritamharikīrttanamvedavṛttānta ca eṣu ādyāḥ aṣṭau bhāgavatoktalakṣaṇānā pratirūpamanusaranti āsana poṣaṇa ca harikīrttanena parigṛhyete vedavṛttānta na kiñcit īśakathāmantareṇa evamida pratīyate yat bhāgavatapurāṇa purāṇagataviṣayāṇā spaṣṭā dhāraṇā poṣayatiasya sūcī vartamānānā purāṇānā prāyeṇa sarvāṇi lakṣaṇāni parigṛhṇāti kintu arthaśāstrasya praṇetāraḥ purāṇasambandhini asmin viṣaye vistareṇa bhinnamata poṣayanti kauṭilīyārthaśāstrasya jayamaṅgalaṭīkāyā nimnoktaḥ śloko dṛśyate  sṛṣṭipravṛtisahāradharmamokṣaprayojanam brahmābhirvividhaiḥ prokta purāṇa pañcalakṣaṇam atra purāṇānā gurutvapūrṇalakṣaṇatvena dharmaḥ atīva tātparyya vahati niścayenātra yathārthamukhabandhāt para dharmīyā ālocanā gṛhītāḥ mantrataravarṇānāt para bhāgavatapurāṇa dharmāya yathāyatha manoyoga dadāti ida vadati manvantarāṇi saddharma itiyaḥ spaṣṭataḥ dharmasya upayogitā gurutva ca svīkaroti ata eva aya siddhāntaḥ na ucitaḥ yat pūrva dharmaḥ purāṇānā cintāyā nāntarbhūta āsīttathā ca asya dhāraṇā kevala paravarttiyuge āgatā eva bahuṣu prācīneṣu grantheṣu na kevala purāṇasya lakṣaṇa karttu praceṣṭā kṛtāapi tu purāṇavaiśiṣṭya vyākyātu prayatnaḥ kṛtaḥ purāṇeṣu pañcalakṣaṇāni tiṣṭhantuna vā tiṣṭhantu athavā daśavaiśiṣṭyāni tiṣṭhantu vā na tiṣṭhantu  iti na praśnaḥ pañcasu vā daśasu vā lakṣaṇeṣu vistṛtā varṇanā darśayati yat tāni lakṣaṇāni kāścit nirdiṣṭān pāthān nirdiśanti purāṇapada na kevala purātana kiñcinnirdiśatiapi tu ida kañcit purātana pāṭhamapi sūcayati  iti asvīkārenyāyo bhaviṣyati api ca purāṇasahitāyāḥ prayoga ima viṣaya draḍhayati yataḥ sahitā īdṛśa tātparya na vahati eṣā sarvadā kartānā pustakānā vā sagrahāṇā vā nirdiṣṭa prasaṅga racayati nedṛśī kāciddhāraṇā athavā nedṛśa kiñcillakṣaṇam itihāsasyopari prāpyate vibhinneṣu prācīneṣu śāstreṣu itastataḥ ida pada vyavahriyate kintu anayā rītyāsya lakṣaṇa na lakṣitamatha vā vaiśiṣṭyakathanena vivṛtampurāṇaiḥ sahāsyāvicchedyonuṣaṅgaḥ evātra kāraṇa bhavitum arhati tayoḥ atīva ghaniṣṭhaḥ sayogaḥ hi sambhāvyo hetuḥ athavā itihāsasya upari bhinnasya spaṣṭasya ca lakṣaṇasyābhāvaḥ vastutaḥ vedasya purāṇasya cadharmaśāstrasya purāṇasya cadarśanasya purāṇasya ca madhye sagatiḥ atīva ghaniṣṭhāntaragā ca kintu pratyeka pṛthak spaṣṭa ca paricaya vahati kintu purāṇetihāsayoḥ viṣaye etādṛśa sādṛśa na aṅkhyate kati paṇḍitā manyante yat purāṇamitihāsaḥ ca bhinnau viṣayau tulanīyamskandapurāṇam kumārikākhaṇḍaḥitihāsapurāṇāni bhidyante lokagauravāttasmin samaye kati vidvāsaḥ punaḥ tayorekatvamanubhavanti tulanīyam  vātsyāyanasya nyāyabhāṣyamlokavṛttamitihāsapurāṇasya viṣayaḥvitarka parihāya vaya kevala paśyāmaḥ yat purāṇeṣu kalpanāyāḥ nirdiṣṭovasarostikintu itihāse prakṛtasavṛttaghaṭanānā bāhulyamasti purāṇeṣu prācīnatāyāḥ prasaṅge asmāhiḥ itomadhye kati svīkṛtāḥ prācīnā granthāḥ ullikhitāḥ tatra purāṇa paricchannagranthatvena svīkṛtam eṣu prācīneṣu śāstreṣu atharvavedasahitā atīva gurutvapūrṇā atraiko mantrosti yasyāśayaḥ  ucchiṣṭājjāyate purāṇa ṛgvedenasāmavedenayajurvedena ca saha ucchiṣṭapada yajñāvaśeṣān sūcayati kintu sāyaṇasya vyākhyāna sayatna manoyogamākarṣati sa vadati sarveṣā bhūtabhautikānāmavasāne śiṣṭa urvaritaḥ paramātmā iti arthāt yadā sarva vināśa yāti tadā kevala paramātmā tiṣṭhati ucchiṣṭapada ta paramātmāna dyotayati eva purāṇānyapi vedā iva apauruṣeyāṇi etāni na kasyāpi mānavasya sṛṣṭikarmāṇi athavā sakalanāni anyatrārthavedo varṇayati  vartamānasya jagataḥ pariprekṣite satyadraṣṭāramantareṇa na kopi janaḥ pūrvatanakalpasyāstitva jñātu śaknotiyo janaḥ pūrvatanakalpasya nirdiṣṭa yathāyatha cākāra vistareṇa jānātisa eva paurāṇika hyabhidhīyate sa suṣṭhu purāṇānā prācīnāḥ kathāḥ ākhyāyikāḥ ca jānāti eva spaṣṭa pratibhāti yat atharvavedasya kāle purāṇāni tathā paurāṇikāḥ aparicayasya tamasi nātiṣṭhansamāje teṣā sabalaḥ pādanyāsa āsīt atharvavedasahitā punaśca varṇayati  vrātyastomasya prasage itihāsaḥ purāṇa gāthānārāśasī imamanusarantiyonena saha vistareṇa paricitaḥ sa eva itihāsasyapurāṇasyagāthāyāḥnārāśasinā priya dhāma bhavati asmin prasage ida smaraṇīya yat aya viśiṣṭo mantraḥ vātyastomotsavasya antarbhuktaḥ cirantanaḥ paramātmā vrātyapadena prakaṭīkṛtaḥ paippalādasahitā vadativrātya vedamagra āsīditi ida niścayena svīkriyate yat viśvasya sūcanāyā vrātyaḥ sarveṣāmagre āsīt aya vastutaḥ paramātmatatvena saha ekatva tulyatā ca vrajati rudrādhyāyeṣu api vaya paśyāmaḥ namo vrātyāya iti vrātyaśca rudraśca abhinnau iti api sūcyateeva yāthāyathyenocyate yat itihāsaḥ purāṇa ca ṛgvedaḥsāmavedaḥyajurvedaḥ iva saśraddha prācīnatva bhajataḥ sahitāmanu brāhmaṇam āyāti caturṣu sthaleṣu śatapathabrāhmaṇam itihāsapurāṇamathavā purāmullikhati ādyeṣu triṣu sthāneṣu itihāsaḥ purāṇa ca pṛthaktvena na prakāśete taddvayamabhinnam kintu avaśiṣṭe dṛṣṭānte ṛṣiḥ padayugalasya madhye pṛthaktva pratiṣṭhāpayitu yatate ayamullekhaḥ pariplavakathayā saha yuktaḥ asmādasmābhiḥ jñāyate yat pariplavānuṣṭhānasya aṣṭamyā rajanyāmitihāsasyāvṛttirbhavati navamyā ca purāṇānā pāṭhaḥ bhavati eva brāhmaṇānā yugepi itihāsaḥ purāṇa ceti padadvayasya sattā pṛthaktvena tathā yuktatvena yugapat tiṣṭhati sma prathamo dṛṣṭānto brahmayajñasya prasage lakṣyate vividhānā vedānā pāṭhaḥ vividha phala janayatiyadi anuśāsanavidyāvākovākyamitihāsaḥ purāṇa cagāthā ca nārāśasī ca paṭhyante kenacijjanena madhuyāgasya phala labhyate paravarttini dṛṣṭānte idamullikhyate yat kaścid vidvān pratyaha veda paṭhet anuśāsanenavidyayāvākovākyenaitihāsenapurāṇenagāthayānārāśasyā ca sākam  sa yadi pratidinamida karoti tarhi sa samagrāya samājāya tathā īśvarāya paripūrṇa santoṣa dadāti tasmin brāhmaṇe anyatrocyate yat ṛgvedaḥ yajurvedaḥsāmavedaḥatharvavedaḥitihāsaḥ purāṇavidyāupaniṣatślokaḥsūtravyākhyānamanuvyākhyāna ca sarvāṇi vedaiḥ saha anvitāni kopi janaḥ anena sārvabhaumatva paramaśaktimatva cārjayati caturthadṛṣṭāntasya gurutvamitomadhye darśitam evañca gopathabrāhmaṇe svīkriyete purāṇānā gurutva ca mahatva ca atrocyate  eva sarve ite vedāḥ kalparahasyabrāhmaṇopaniṣaditihāsapurāṇaiḥ saha viracitāḥ anyasmin mantre ida brāhmaṇa pañcavedaracanetihāsa vivṛṇoti  te pañca vedā hi sarpavedaḥpiśācavedaḥasuravedaḥitihāsavedaḥ purāṇavedaśca ida vadati pūvasyā diśi sarpavedo nirmitaḥdakṣiṇasyā piśācavedaḥpaścimāyāmasuravedaḥuttarasyāmitihāsavedaḥuparu ca adhaśca purāṇavedo nirmitaḥ asmin prasage bhūḥ bhuvaḥ svaḥ janaḥ mahaḥ iti pañca mahāvyāhṛtaya ullikhyante pañcavedebhyaḥ para vṛdhatkarat guhatmahattacceti pañca mahāvākyāni utthitāni evamatra purāṇebhyaḥ vedebhya iva sadṛśī maryādā tathā padasthitiḥ dīyate purāṇāni itihāsāśca prācīnatva pavitratva ca bhajangti iti vivicyate jaiminīyopaniṣadi ca tadbrāhmaṇe cāpi nyūnatamataḥ pañcasu sthaleṣu     purāṇebhyaḥ sākṣya sarvotkṛṣṭatvena svīkriyate brāhmaṇānāmantimośaḥ āraṇyakatvena itihāsatvena ca paricīyate taittirīyāraṇyake purāṇaśabdaḥ brahmayajñaprasagena punaḥ punaḥ vyavahṛtaḥ yadi vaya chāndogyopaniṣadi bṛhadāraṇyakopaniṣadi ca vyavahṛtasya purāṇapadasya purāṇapadasya prayoga tātparya ca vicārayāmaḥtadā paśyāmo yat purāṇāni vedāḥ iva namasyatā yānti purāṇānā vedānā ca sadṛśa mūlya tathā gurutva tiṣṭhati yataḥ ruddhaśvāsasya muktaye sādhātikyā praceṣṭayā prayojana nāstitataḥ prakṛtyaivocyate yat vedānā tathā purāṇānā yoniḥ svayakriyaḥ svataḥ sphūrtaśca bṛhadāraṇyakopaniṣadekena sundareṇa dṛṣṭāntena viṣayamima sarala karttu yatate tathā hi  sa yathā ārdrendhanāgneḥ avyāhitāt pṛthag dhūmā viniścarantieva vā aresya mahatto bhūtasya niḥśvasitam etad yad ṛgvedo yajurvedaḥ sāmavedotharvāṅgirasa itihāsapurāṇam iti ida vākya katibhiḥ uddhṛtibhiḥ chāndogyopaniṣadā samarthitam tadyathā  ṛgveda bhagavodhyemi yajurveda sāmavedamatharvāṇa caturthamitihāsapurāṇa pañcamamvedānā veda pitrya rāśimetat bhagavodhyemi  ṛgvedo yajurvedaḥ sāmaveda ātharvaṇaścaturtha itihāsapurāṇaḥ pañcamo vedānā vedaḥ vastutonyatrāpi asyāmupaniṣadi dṛśyate yat itihāsapurāṇa pañcamavedatvenānumoditamtasmai ca pavitratvasya parama pada pradīyate evamida parisphuṭa yat īdṛśasya purātanasya yugasya sṛṣṭikarmāṇi khalu purāṇāni etāni ca kati nītīḥ na kevala vyākurvantiapi tu etāni nirdiṣṭam ākāra parigṛhya janebhyaḥ punaḥ punaḥ praśasāmākarṣanti sma sūtrasāhityasya pṛṣṭāsu purāṇā gurutva tathā prācīnatva paunaḥpunyena sūcyate sākhyāyanaśrautasūtre pañcamavedatvena purāṇa svīkriyate tathā ca āraṇyakāya upaniṣade ca yad gurutva tadeva pradīyate purāṇāya āśvalāyanagṛhyasūtre purāṇasambandhinaḥ pracurāḥ prasagāḥ santi katiṣu kṣetreṣu vedādhyayanena saha itihāsasya purāṇasya ca adhyayana vihitamāsīt kutracit sthāne idamucyate yatyaiḥ paṇḍitaiḥ itihāsasya tathā purāṇānāmiva śāstrāṇā svādaḥ anubhūtaḥte devaiśca pitṛbhiśca saha amṛtasāgare magnā bhavanti tasmin sūtre anyatra vahniśikhāprajvalanasya prasage ida varṇyate yatyadaivāmarāṇā janānā pavitreṣu karmasu itihāsasya purāṇasya ca prayogaḥ syāt sa samayaḥ śubhalakṣaṇānvita iti  kintu idamavaśyameva svīkartavya yat śrautasūtreṣu purāṇaviṣayaka yadvivaraṇa prāpyate tanna kimapi purāṇa vā purāṇasya ślokasagraha  vā viśeṣeṇa ullikhati  asmin viṣaye āpastambadharmasūtram apūrva sthāna tathā padamadhikaroti tatkāle vartamānataḥ purāṇātaḥ spaṣṭāu dvau ślokau tasya lekhakena uddhṛtau iyamuddhṛtiḥ yoginā nivṛttimārga praśasatisakāma karma ca pariharati tatrocyate  aṣṭāśītiḥ sahasrāṇi ye prajāmīṣirarṣayaḥ dakṣiṇenāryamṇaḥ panthāna te śmaśānāni bhejire aṣṭāśītisahasrāṇi ye prajā neṣirarṣayaḥ uttareṇāryamṇaḥ panthāna temṛtva hi bhejire iti bṛhadāraṇyakopaniṣadaḥ upari racitāyā ṭīkāyā śaṅkarācāryaḥ uparyuktaślokadvayasya uddhṛti dadau brahmāṇḍapurāṇe ślokadvayamasti viṣṇupurāṇe tathā padmapurāṇe uktau ślokau dṛśyate eva purāṇeṣu tayoryoniḥ praśnātītaḥ āpastambaḥ purāṇāni papāṭhaślokadvaya jajñausvīyalakṣyānusāreṇa svīyagranthe vyavajahāra ca brahmāṇḍapurāṇenaviṣṇupurāṇenapadmapurāṇena sarvaiḥ purāṇaiḥ saha tasya paricaya āsīnnaveti praśna avāstavaḥ āpastambaḥ kintu purāṇebhya ātmana ṛṇa svīcakāra  yāni tasya sammukhe prādhānya labhante sma  sa viṣaya upasahāre vakṣyate api ca tasminnāpastambadharmasūtrenyatra vaya paśyāmaḥ svargatānā pitṛṇā prasageyat te svarga jigyuḥ tathā ca viśvasya vināśa yāvat tatroṣuḥ punaśca sṛṣṭikarmaṇoḥ apariṇate prārambhe te svargasya mūlatva hetutva ca bhejire aya sandeśosmābhiḥ bhaviṣyapurāṇāt prāpyate bhaviṣyapurāṇadaya prasagaḥ sayatnaḥ vicāram apekṣate tena kālena bhaviṣyapurānasyāstitva svīkṛta tathā anumoditam āpastambovaśyameva bhaviṣyapurāṇa papāṭha vyavajahāra ca yadyapi ida tathya yat aya ślokaḥ vartamāne bhaviṣyapurāṇe na dṛśyatetathāpi asya prāmāṇye spardhā na jñātavyā etannāmollekhena vibhinnaśāstreṣu ye bahavaḥ ślokā uddhṛtā babhūvuḥte na dṛśyante kimida sūcayati yat sarve śāstrakārāḥ eva bhrānti gatāḥ eva ca gautamadharmasūtrepi vaya paśyāmo yat itihāsapurāṇapada purāṇapada vā sampūrṇanibandhatvena kṣetradvaye ullikhitam prathame kṣetre gautamaḥ vahuśruta  śabdasyārtha vyākhyātu ciceṣṭe asya śabdasya vyutpatigatorthaḥ hi sa janaḥ yena bahu śruta tathā jñātam gautamasya mate sa eva bahuśruta iti vividyate sa janānā rīti prathā ca samyak jānāti sa vedān ānuṣaṅgikavijñānaṣaṭka ca jānātivākovākyeṣu itihāse purāṇe ca pāṇḍityamarjayati eva bahuśrutasya yogyatāyai itihāse purāṇe ca dakṣatayā prayojanamasti anyatra gautamo manyate yat prajāsu rājñā vyavahāraḥteṣā vedeṣudharmaśāstreṣuānuṣagikavijñāneṣuupavedeṣuavaśiṣṭāpurāṇeṣu ca pāṇḍityena śāsanīyaḥ atrāpi vaya paśyāmaḥ yat purāṇebhyaḥ yathāyatha sammāna pradattam gautamaḥ spaṣṭa vadati yat eṣu sarveṣu śāstreṣu ajñaḥ rājā anupayogī sa kadāpi sāphalya na labhate evamida dṛśyate yat dharmaśāstrairapi purāṇānā prabhāvaḥ svīkṛtaḥ anye sarve prācīnā granthā iva arthaśāstrasyopari likhitā granthā api purāṇebhyaḥ yathāyatha svīkṛti dadati sarveṣu arthaśāstreṣu kauṭilyasyārthaśāstra prasiddhatam kauṭilyena purāṇānā gurutva svīkṛtam yataḥ asmābhiḥ dṛśyate yat viśeṣīkṛtapadatvena purāṇapada tena arthaśāstrasya bahuṣu sthaleṣu prayuktam yadā kaścit nṛpatiḥ prakṛtakarmamārga parihāya duṣṭamārgamavalambatetadā śubhākāṅkṣiṇaḥ mantriṇaśca itihāsasya ca purāṇasya ca dṛṣṭānta darśayitvā ta rājāna pāpamārgāt nivārayeyuḥ prayojanīya paktiyugalamadhaḥ uddhṛtam kauṭilyenoktam  mukhyairavagṛhīta vā rājāna tatpriyāśritaḥ itihāsapurāṇābhyā bodhayet arthaśāstravit iti  ata eva kauṭilyakālīnāni kati purāṇāni ca sadācārarītiprathāviṣayakāni teṣā viṣaya vastūni ca sādhāraṇānā yathā prayojana sādhayanti tathā  rājñā samīpepi tāni hitakarāṇi eva pratibhānti  anyatra dṛśyate yat purāṇānā pāṭhaḥ prātyahikakarmasūcyārambhaviśeṣa iti kauṭilyo jñāpayati yat divasasya prathamārddhe nṛpaḥ gajāśvarathaśāstraviṣayaka paurāṇika pāṭha paṭhetparārddhe ca sa itihāsapāṭhe ātmāna niyojayet  yatra viṣāyāḥ khalu purāṇamitivṛttamākhyāyikāudāharaṇamdharmaśāstramarthaśāstram ca rājānaḥ sundareṇa vetanena purāṇeṣu nipuṇān janān rājakāryeṣu niyojayeyuḥ te paurāṇikāḥ upayukteṣu kāryeṣu niyuktā bhaviṣyanti te vetanatvena paṇānā sahasra grahīṣyanti idamatīva sthūlakāya vetana yat paurāṇikebhyaḥ dīyatetat tathā gurutvabhājā madhye teṣā pada teṣā gurutva dāyitva ca sūcayati anyatra trayītipadasya tātparya vyākhyātu kauṭilyo vadati  sāmaveda ṛgvedo yajurvedaśceti vedatraya trayītyucyate trayī atharvaveda itihāsaścāpi vedatvena parigaṇyate eva kauṭilyasya kāle itihāsasya ca purāṇasya ca vedānāmiva sammāna babhūva tau viṣayau atimūlyavat pāṭhatvena svīkṛti lebhāte bahudharmasahitāsu api vedapāragapadasya tātparya sūcayitu prayatnāḥ kṛtāḥ yasyārthaḥ vedeṣu pāradarśī jana iti tathā kartu pravṛttāḥ etāḥ dharmasahitāḥ sarvā eva eteṣā purāṇānā mahatva svīkurvanti  vyāsasahitāyā vaya paśyāmaḥ yat vedārtha boddhumicchuko jana ānuṣaṅgikavijñānaiḥ saha vedatrayasya adhyayana vināpi purāṇānā sayatnamadhyayana  kuryāt  vyāso manyate  mīmāsate ca yo vedān ṣaḍbhiraṅgaiḥ savistaraiḥ itihāsapurāṇāni sa bhaved vedapāragaḥ iti anyasmin śloke vidyāviśeṣa ullikhitaḥ atra prasage ida lakṣyate yat brāhmaṇāḥ kṣatriyā vaiśyāśceti varṇatraya dvijātitvena paricīyate kevala prāguktavarṇatrayagatānā janānā śrutismṛtipurāṇoktadharmavyāpāreṣu aśagrahaṇasya adhikārosti atra vaidikāya tathā paruāṇikāya dharmāya sadṛśa gauravamarpitam  kenacicchiṣyeṇa vidyāyā arjanasya viṣaye uśanāsahitāyā dṛśyate yat ajñātakulaśīlebhyaḥ janebhyaḥ vedadharmaśāstrapurāṇasakrāntā śikṣā na  deyā  tatrocyate  veda dharma purāṇa ca tathā tattvāni nityaśaḥ savatsaroṣite śiṣye gururjñāna vinirdiśet iti manusahitāyāmapi purāṇāni prasasitāni tatrocyate  svādhyāya śrāvayet pitrye dharmaśāstrāṇi caiva hi ākhyānānītihāsāśca purāṇāni khilāni ca iti vastutaḥ vedagānena yat phala jāyate purāṇagānenāpi tat phala bhavati dharmīyānuṣṭhāneṣu sarvatra vedapāṭhena saha purāṇapāṭhopi sadṛśa gaurava bhajate yājñavalkyaḥ purāṇānā pramukhatvamāha  purāṇanyāyamīmāsādharmaśāstrāṅgamiśritāḥ vedāḥ sthānāni vidyānā dharmasya ca caturdaśa purāṇāni svargavāsinā tathā pitṛlokavāsinā rañjanāyālam yaḥ pratyaha yathāsādhya vākovākyapurāṇāninārāśasīḥgāthāḥitihāsa vidyāśca paṭhatisa devān māsadugdhamadhubhiḥ rañjayatipitṛśca madhudhṛtābhyām atra prasage yājñavalkyasahitāyāmucyate  vākovākya purāṇa ca nārāśasīśca gāthikāḥ itihāsāsthathā vidyā yodhīte śaktitonvaham māsakṣīraudanamadhutarpaṇa sa divaukasām karoti tṛpti ca tathā pitṛṇā madhusarpiṣā iti punaśca lakṣyate tatra  vedātharvapurāṇāni setihāsāni śaktitaḥ japayajñaprasiddhyartha vidyā cādhyātmikī japet ādhyātmikyā vidyāyā vedāntādīnā parigrahaḥ sūcyate vastutaḥ te munayo jagadvyāpi yaśaḥ arjayantiyebhyaḥ sarve vedāḥ purāṇādayaśca utpatanti tathā visarpanti prācīnabhāratīyā prasiddhā dārśanikā yathā śavarasvāmīśakarācāryaḥkumārilabhaṭṭaḥ punaḥ punaḥ purāṇebhyaḥ teṣā yathāyatha prāpyāśa dadāti teṣā prāmāṇya tathā prācīnatva niḥsaśayena svīkṛtam eṣu triṣu śavarasvāmī khalu jyeṣṭhaḥ sa sambhavataḥ  tamāt khṛṣṭābdāt  khṛṣṭābda yāvat samaye samajāyata sa tadīyamīmāsāsūtraṭīkāyā vibhinnayāgasambandhinā devānā prakṛta svarūpa nirdhārayitu yatate kasmiścit prasage sa āha yat asmin bindau itihāsaḥ purāṇa caikamatya poṣayataḥ tasya mate agniprabhṛtayaḥ svargavāsinaḥ khalu devāḥ jaiminisūtrāṇāmupari likhitasya parsiddhiasya tantravārttikamiti granthasya praṇetā hi kumārilabhaṭṭaḥ sa tatra yonitvena pramāṇatvena ca hi purāṇamullikhati tasya mate purāṇeṣu itihāseṣu ca dṛṣṭānā vibhinnānā vṛttāntānā sākṣya niścayenaiva grahītavyam bhaugolikā vibhāgā vṛttāntāścarājakulānā tathā anyavaśānā kālānukramika varṇanavibhinnānā sthānānā tathā yugānā vivaraṇabhāvino vṛttāntāśca sarvadā praśnātītāstathānabhiyuktāḥ pavitre sthāne sampādita karma dharma nayatikintu apavitre sthāne sampādita karma duḥkha janayati eva puṇyasya ca pāpasya ca nirdhāraṇāya jagataḥ pavitrasthānānā prakṛtena jñānena sampūrṇataḥ prayojanamasti brāhmaṇavarṇīyā athavā kṣatriyavarṇīyā mahānto janā kevalamanupreraṇāyāḥ api tu yathāyatha pramāṇyasya hetubhūtāḥ ekasmin sthale kumārila āha yat buddhādayaḥ kecit kaliyuge āvirbhaviṣyanti iti purāṇeṣūcyate te dharmasya anta sādhayiṣyanti kintu bhāgyavaśāt tadipadeśaśravaṇasya janā nagaṇyā eva bhaviṣyanti tenocyate  smaryante ca purāṇeṣu dharmaviluptihetavaḥ kalau śākyādayasteṣā ko vākya śrotumarhati iti ida darśayati yat kumārilasyāvirbhāvādanatipūrvameva purāṇāni bauddhadarśanasya spardhā gṛhītvaiva vartante sma paurāṇikavicārānusāreṇa meruparvatasya pṛṣṭhe uttarasyā diśi svargastiṣṭhati svargapadārdha viśadīkurvan kumārilaḥ ādau tasya sthānam avadhārayitu ceṣṭate sma svargaḥ kīdṛśaḥ api na nakṣatrāṇā grahāṇā vā āśrayaḥ api sa meruparvatasya pṛṣṭhe vartate api sa devalokaḥ cirantanasukhasya ādhāra iti sarve praśnāḥ kumārilenālocitāḥ ida darśayati yat sosmin prasage purāṇānā dhāraṇābhiḥ saha niḥsandehena paricita āsīt asmāka vaktavya samarthayitu vaya tadīyayantravārttikād uddhṛti yacchāmaḥ  sa āha   tathā svargaśabdenāpi nakṣatradeśo vā vaidikapravādapaurāṇikayājñikadarśanena ucyate  yadi vetihāsapurāṇopapanna merupṛṣṭhamathavā  anvayavyatirekābhyā vibhakta kevalameva sukham   anena prakāreṇaiva śaṅkarācāryopi tasya śārīrakabhāṣyasya bahuṣu sthaleṣu na kevala purāṇaśabdam ullikhati sma api tu purāṇānā bahubhiḥ  pāṭhaiḥ saha paricitaḥ āsīt  yadyapi sa nāmnā na kimapi purāṇamullikhati tathāpi tasya vaktavya samarthayitu sa purāṇebhyaḥ ślokānām uddhṛti dadāti te ślokā adyāpi vartamāneṣu purāṇeṣu prāpyante asya vyākhyānāya katibhiḥ dṛṣṭāntaiḥ prayojanamasti ekadā śaṅkarācāryastarkayati yat devānā kiñcit sāmarthyamasti te śārīrikarūpāṇi dadhati iti mantrārthavādetihāsapurāṇebhyaḥ jñāyatesmābhiḥ tathā sāmarthyamapi teṣā sambhavati mantrārthavādetihāsapurāṇalokebhyaḥ vigrahavattvādyadhigamāt sarvāṇi purāṇāni viśeṣeṇa vadanti yat devānā nirdiṣṭa ākāraḥnirdiṣṭamāyatananirdiṣṭa rūpam santi śaṅkarācārya ekadā mantavya cakāra yat brahmā ca jagacca svabhāvena pthaktva vrajataḥ sa tadīyasanatsujātīyabhāṣye muneḥ parāśarāt dvayoḥ ślokayoḥ uddhṛti dadau etau dvau ślokau viṣṇupurāṇe lakṣyete tathā ca ida sphuṭa yat śaṅkarācāryaḥ viṣṇupurāṇāt yathāśabda ślokau jagrāhayena purāṇena saha śaṅkarācāryaḥ sampūrṇataḥ paricita āsīt uktaḥ parāśaraḥ viṣṇupurāṇasya pravaktāpi kiñca tadīyabrahmasūtrabhāṣye śaṅkarācāryaḥ purāṇebhyaḥ katīnā tātparyapūrṇānā tathā gurutvapūṇānā ślokānāmullekha cakāra sosmin prasage purāṇasya nāma ullilekha asyollekhena utsāho jāyate yatkiñcit parivartana parigṛhyāya śloko vāyupurāṇepi dṛśyate brahmasūtrabhāṣyasya sa ślokodha uddhriyate  ataśca sakṣepamima śṛṇudhva nārāyaṇaḥ sarvamida purāṇam sa sargakāle ca karoti sarva sahārakāle ca tadatti bhūyaḥ tasminneva bhāṣyenyatra śaṅkarācāryaḥ saptanarakān varṇayati sa ca ghoṣayati yat duṣṭakarmaprakṛtyanusārataḥ janā vividhān narakān nīyante eteṣā saptavidhānā narakāṇā vistṛta vivaraṇa tathā citravadupasthāpana purāṇeṣu prāpyate  api ca śaṅkarācāryeṇa ālocitā viṣayā nimnarūpāḥ  tathā hi atītānā bhāvinā ca kalpanā parimāṇam brahmaṇā sṛṣṭeḥ prāk cirantanānā sarvavyāpinā  ca vedānā samāgamaḥ brahmaṇaśca tadā sṛṣṭeḥ ārambhaḥsattvānā nāmnā karmaṇā ca prakāśaḥ ityādayaḥ tathā kartu sa vividhaiḥ purāṇaiḥ prabhāvitobhavatpurāṇeṣu ete viṣayā vistareṇālocitāḥ śaṅkarācāryaḥ kāle kāle purāṇebhyaḥ kati vedān uddadhāra vastutaḥ sa vivṛṇoti sa viśvasṛṣṭeḥ prāk svīyakramānusārataḥ sthāvarāṇāmasthāvarāṇā cavināśināmāvināśinā ca sattvānā prayoga nirṇayati teṣā jivānā janma vividhaprakṛtyanusārataḥ nirdhāryate tad yathā ahisā prakṛtiḥsahisā prakṛtiḥkomalā kaṭhinā vā prakṛtiḥsadayā nirdayā vā prakṛtiḥmithyā prakṛtirvā ete viṣayāḥ kūrmapurāṇemārkaṇḍeyapurāṇevāyupurāṇeviṣṇupurāṇe ca lakṣyante eva nāsti sandehāvasaraḥ yat etāni purāṇāni śaṅkarācāryeṇa vistareṇa paṭhitāni tathā prayuktāni atra prasage purāṇānā yāthārtyasya nirṇaye vātsyāyanasya vaktavyamatīva gurutvapūrṇam tasya mate ye nāma mantrabrāhmaṇarūpāṇā vedānā draṣṭāraḥte eva itihāsapurāṇadharmaśāstrāṇā praṇetāro varṇayitāraśca eva vedānāmitihāsapurāṇānā ca madhye samatā vartate yāvat teṣā lekhakāḥ sṛṣṭikarmāṇi ca saśliṣyante avaśyameva teṣā viṣayā vastūni vā vicitratā vrajanti mantrāśca brāhmaṇāni ca yajñaviṣayamālocayanti itihāsapurāṇāni ca tatkālīnākhyānāni varṇayanti tathā ca dharmaśāstrāṇi ālocayanti samājajīvanopayoginiyamaśṛkhalādirakṣāviṣayam  vātsyāyana āha ya eva mantrabrāhmaṇasya draṣṭāraḥ pravaktāraśca te khalu itihāsapurāṇasya dharmaśāstrasya ceti viṣayavyavasthāpanācca yathāviṣaya  prāmāṇyam  yajño mantrabrāhmaṇasya lokavṛttamitihāsapurāṇasya lokavyavahāravyavastāpana dharmaśāstrasya viṣayaḥ nyāyasūtrabhāṣyenyatra anusandhīyate katīnā svīkṛtānā granthānā bhittauyat itihāsaḥ purāṇāni ca atīva prācīnatva bhajanti teṣā yāthārthye na kopi praśnaḥ samudeti ādikāvya rāmāyaṇa ekādhikaiḥ purāṇaiḥ saha tasya paricaya prakaṭayati tasya kaviḥ vālmīkiḥ ekatrāha yat yoginastam purāṇaiḥvedaiḥpañcarātraiḥ pratyaha dhyāyanti tathā ca kratubhiḥ tam pūjayanti katiṣu sthaleṣu sumantraḥ tādṛśajanatvena varṇitaḥ yo janaḥ purāṇāni adhīte sma sa pravaktā babhūva ata eva idameva svābhāvika yat purāṇeṣu sobhijña āsīt purāṇeṣu soyodhyārājasya daśarathasyākhyāna paṭhati sma tatra sa putrahīnatvāt daśarathasya mānasikī daśā jānāti sma mānasikī vedanā dūrikartu nṛpeṇa ki ki kṛta tadapi sumantreṇādhigatamāsīt ata eva īdṛśyāmavasthāyā samāgatāyā sa etā atītā ghaṭanā varṇayati kadāpi purāṇārthe kadāpi vā purātanasyārthe rāmāyaṇamiva mahābhārata na punaḥ punaḥ viśeṣyatvena purāṇapada vyavaharati kintu keṣucit kṣetreṣu nirdiṣṭasāhityakarmatvena padamida prayuktam purāṇena saha mahābhāratasya paricitirāsīt tasya parokṣa sākṣya mārkaṇḍeyapurāṇanāmākite ślokadvayesti yathā  mārkaṇḍeyasamāsyā ca purāṇa parikīrtyate tathā kathā śubhā śrutvā mārkaṇḍeyasya dhīmataḥ vismitaḥ samapadyanta purāṇasya nivedanāt  mahābhārata spaṣṭataḥ vāyupurāṇasya ca matsyapurāṇasya ca viṣayaiḥ caritraiśca saha paricaya darśayati evam  etat te sarvamākhyātamatītānāgata  mayā  vāyuproktamanusmṛtya purāṇamṛṣisammatam api ca tapasā mahatā yuktaḥ sotha sraṣṭu pracakrame sarvāḥ prajāḥ manuḥ sākṣād yathāvat bharatarṣabha ityetan mātsyaka nāma purāṇa parikīrttitam yadyapi eteṣā viṣayāṇā svalpāśa eva varttamāne vāyupurāṇe matsyapurāṇe ca dṛśyatetathāpi idamanasvīkārya yat mahābhāratīyasaśliṣṭhāśaracanāsamaye ukte dve purāṇe prācīnarūpa gṛhītvaiva bahula pracalite āstām kenāpi prakāreṇa mahābhārata purāṇānā pracalitā sakhyā ajñāsīt tataḥ tat mahābhārata viśeṣaṇa varṇayati purāṇāni aṣṭādaśa iti purāṇasāhityaviṣayakamanurūpa cittahāri tathya bharatīyanāṭyaśāstresti tatra auḍramāgadhīpravṛttiprayoga varṇayan bharataḥ pūrvabhāratasya vahūnā bhāgānā nāmāni karoti tathā ca sa vadati yat ete cānye bhāgāśca purāṇeṣu kīrttitāḥ yathā  aṅgavaṅgakaliṅgāśca vatsāścaivoḍramāgadhāḥ pauṇḍranaipālikāścaiva antargirigahirgirāḥ tatra vaṅgasamā jñeyā malacāmallavarṣakāḥ brahmottarapravṛttayo bhārgavā bhargavāstathā prāpautiṣāḥ prāgjyotiṣāḥpulindāśca vaidehāstāmnaliptakāḥ prāgāḥ prāvṛtayaścaiva yuñjanti ddhyoḍramāgadhīm anyepi deśā ebhyo ye purāṇe samprakīrttitāḥ teṣu prayujyate hyeṣā pravṛttistvauḍramāgadhī anyatra bharataḥ karmakṣetratvena bhāratavarṣa varṇayati sa ca vividhānā varṣāṇā deśānāmgirīṇā purāṇasammatamullekha karoti saptaviśedhyāye bharatena bahuvacanopetapurāṇaśabdo vyavahṛtaḥ anena sūcyate yat purāṇāni tadā spaṣṭapurāṇajātīyasāhityakarmatvena svīkṛtāni āsan purāṇasāhityasya prācīnatva bahubhiḥ bauddhaiḥ tathā jainaiḥ granthaiḥ pratipāditam  tathā hi anyatame mudrite saskaraṇe mahāpurāṇatvena kathitaḥ lalitavistaraḥ iti granthaḥ kathayati yat bodhisattvaḥ nigamapurāṇetihāsavedavyākaraṇaprabhṛtiṣu  vidyāsu atīva nipuṇa āsīt  evañca tasmin samaye purāṇasāhityasyāstitva pramāṇitam milindapañhaḥ  yatra grīkarājamināndārasya ca bauddhamunināgasenasya ca madhye salāpo vidhṛta iti pratyayaḥsa granthaḥ nṛpasya mināndārasya śikṣāgatā yogyatā varṇayati yathā  sa vahūni kalāśāstrāṇi vijñānāni ca jajñau  pavitramaitihyamdharmanirpekṣavidhisākhyayoganyāyavaiśeṣikadarśanānigaṇitagītabheṣajatatva vedacatuṣṭaya purāṇāni itihāsa ca  anyatrāya kathayati brāhamaṇaviṣayamadhikṛtya yat brāhmaṇānā ca brāhmaṇāpatyānā ca vṛttiḥ ṛgvedenayajurvedenasāmavedenaatharvavedenaśubhalakṣaṇavijñānenakathābhiḥpurāṇaiḥ kośaiśca saha yujyate ida vaktavya yat dvayoḥ sthalayoḥ madhyenyatarasmin kṣetre purāṇaśabdo bahuvacanena yuktaḥ atrāyamāśayaḥ  sa śabdaḥ vidyāyāḥ śākhā nirdiśati tathā ca ekādhikapurāṇānā tatkālīnamastitva sūcayati naiva bauddhāḥ lekhakāḥjaināḥ saskṛtapurāṇānām anukaraṇena tathā ādarśena bahūni sāhityāni vyaracayaneṣu lekhakeṣu prācīnatamaḥ khalu vimalasūrināmadheyaḥ kaścitjaino muniḥ khṛṣṭābdīyaprathamaśatake sa paumacariyam lilekha sa ekādhikeṣu prasageṣu ida purāṇamiti uvāca ravisenanāmadheyoparo jaino lekhakaḥ  tame khṛṣṭābde saskṛtabhāṣayā padmapurāna lilekha khṛṣṭābdīyanavamaśatake guṇabhadreṇa uttarapurāṇa likhitam  eṣā granthānā nāmataḥ tathā granthanibaddhaviṣayāṇā prakṛtitaḥ ida sphuṭa pañcalakṣaṇānā saskṛtapurāṇānā viṣaye khṛṣṭābdasūcanākalpakālāt  eva jainānāmavagatirāsīt  eva purāṇasāhityasya prakṛti ca prācīnatā cādhikṛtya vedādisāhityebhyaḥ yāni tathyāni asmābhiḥ sagṛhyantetāni sarvāṇyupanyastāni etāni prabhavasthānāni parīkṣya dṛśyate yat khṛṣṭajanmanaḥ katipayavarṣebhyaḥ prāk eva purāṇasāhitya samajāyatatathā ca tasmin purātane kāle eva ekādhikānā purāṇānāmastitvamāsīt vastutaḥ purāṇānā janapriyatva tathā gurutva nāsīdadivasavyāpīmāsavyāpīvā varṣavyāpī viṣayaḥ api tu bahuvarṣavyāpī viṣayaḥ yena purāṇaiḥ janamānaseṣu cirasthāyī prabhāvaḥ sthāptaḥ mantharamapi sudṛḍha purāṇaiḥ janāḥ samākṛṣṭāḥ muninṛpādicaritraviṣāyakamākhyānamviśvasṛṣṭivinaṣṭisamparkita cittākarṣakamupākhyānamviśvasya vividhānā deśānā bhaugolika vivaraṇamsamayaviṣāyako vividhaḥ parimāpastathā vibhāgaḥvividhayugavyāptikālanirṇayaḥapi ca dharmadarśanādayaḥ  ete sarve viṣayāḥ purāṇānā pṛṣṭheṣu upasthāpitāḥ santaḥ janānā hṛdaya jahruḥ ata eva sādhvidamucyate yat purāṇasāhitya khalu svaya prakāśaka purātanamapi nūtanamamūlya prācīnabhāratīya nidhānam  ṣaṣṭhodhyāyaḥ purāṇeṣu karuṇā anubhavajanyajñānaviṣayo hi dharmaḥ aya na kṛtsnaśaḥ tāttviko bhavitumarhati yadyapi na kevala hindudharmasya api tu sarveṣā dharmāṇā kaścidānuṣṭhāniko viṣayostitathāpi prakṛtārthena prayukto dharmo vastutaḥ mūlyajagatā saha pratyakṣa sāvadhānatā sarve ānuṣṭhānikā vyāpārāḥ prāyeṇa nirarthakāḥ te maulikamūlyamahattvapramāṇārtha parokṣamārgāḥ kasyaciddeśasya saskṛtistaddeśīye dharme pratiphalitā bhavanti bhāratīyasaskṛtiviṣayepi kaścana vyatikramo nāsti sarvāsā sabhyatānāmekaikaśo vivartanakendrastiṣṭhati tathā hi  prācīno grīsaḥ kalāyāmanurāgī āsītromaśca rājanītyām  uktasabhyatādvayena saha bhāratīyasabhyatāyāstulanāyā kṛtāyāmida dṛśyate yat dharmanirapekṣatāyā upari pratiṣṭhitā sabhyatā vismṛti yāti kintu bhāratīyā sabhyatā dharmarājanītyādijhañjhāsakule virodhini pariveśepi bhayaśūnyaiva daṇḍāyamānā tiṣṭhati atra hetuḥ  tasyā bhittibhūmiḥ na mithyādharmanirapekṣatāyā śithile saikate sthāpitāapi tucirantanaiḥ dārśanikaistathā naitikairmūlyabodhairviracitā tatra yathākrama kāle kāle bahava ādhyātmikā netāra āgatāḥ te hi saskṛteryathārtha vāhakāḥ  yatra saskṛtau mādhuryasya tathā satyasya samanvayaḥ sādhito bhavati mādhurya svaya sārvalaukika prema prakāśayati satya ca jñānāloka prajvalayati  sa āloko nāmādhyātmikaḥ prabodhaḥ tatkartṛhvāna na kevala jātiviśeṣāya sampradāyaviśeṣāya vā kriyatepi tu samagramānavebhya eva teṣā vāṇī tathā śikṣā na kevala samayaviśeṣe sthānaviśeṣe vā prayujyateapi tu samagre viśve tathā samagre kāle vaidiko dharmaḥ khalu upayogamukhī eva vinimayaprathāviśeṣamabhyasyati  yatra vaidikāḥ purohitā yajñe kañciddeva kāściddevān vā āhūya pūjayantitasmācca athavā tebhyaśca vinimayena pracura vittamicchanti tathāpi ida svīkarttavya yat teṣu vyāvahārikeṣu svārthapareṣu ca kāryeṣu kācinmahatī nītirbabhūva sā khalu satyasyāthavā ṛtasya nītiḥ yat satyamācaraṇānā sādhāraṇeṣu niyameṣu svaya prakaṭitam aya naitiko vyāpāraḥ yaḥ prācīne dharme dṛśate  paravarttini kāle ākāraviśeṣa dadhāra sa ca māhākāvyika paurāṇika ca yugamātya nirdiṣṭasāmājikādarśatvena pariṇato babhūva guṇadoṣayoḥ puṇyapāpayośca vivecanā prāyeṇāsminnādarśevatiṣṭhate tasyātikrame gurupāpamvicāraśca tadanusārī sāmānyataḥnaitikakarttavyatānītau nirdiṣṭānā karttavyānā svīkṛtirasti tāni kartavyāni jātyā sahajīvanasya paryāyeṇa saha saśliṣyante etānyantareṇāpikati sārvalaukikāni karttavyāni santi samājaḥ pārasparikakarmasu niyuktān sarvavidhān lokān gṛhītvā racitaḥ sa na sajātīyānā savṛttīyānā samamanobhāvānā janānā samavāyaḥ ata eva sarveṣā sampradāyānā savṛttīyānā samamanobhāvānā janānā samavāyaḥ ata eva sarveṣā sampradāyānā sarvāsā vā jātīnā kṛte kati niyamā avaśyameva sthāsyanti te niyamāḥ khalu sāmājikavāhanasya samṛddhyā prayojana sādhayantiteṣu kati sarvātiśāyino vyāpārāḥ santi ye sarvebhyaḥ kañcit vyavahāra kāmayante eva parārthamupakāraḥatithisevāgṛhapālitapaśupālanampitṛśca āhutidānam  ityādīni kāryāṇi sarvairavaśya karaṇīyāni āsan evañca jīveṣu yantraṇādhānamanyeṣā sampattiṣu balapūrvakānyāyādhikāraḥityādayo vyāpārā nindanīyāḥ kintu vipadāpannebhyaḥ sahāyatāgurujanebhyaḥ sammānamityādīni karttavyāni sāmājikāstitvasya pakṣe maulikāni kāraṇāni ata eva evakaraṇa hi sārvalaukika karttavyam yaunaśuddhatāstriyai sakṛdvivāhovivāhavidhipālanamete viṣayāḥ vyaktisukhāya tathā sāmājikaikyavidhānāya ca upayogino vivicyante punaśca naitikaviśuddhaye kativiṣayaiḥ prayojanamasti yathā
