niyamayanti jainadharme bauddhadharme ca ahisāmūlo yo dharmaḥ sa vivecanīyamātrayā hindudharma prabhāvita karoti vaidikasāhitye yā cintā pracāra labhatesā cintaiva purāṇānāmapi kintu sā cintā janapriyopāyena ākhyānādimādhyamena pracāritā bhavati ākhyānādīnā mūlagatāḥ nītiḥ karuṇaiva samakālīnabhāvanopayoginī paurāṇikī kathāmālā janapriyaśubhavārttātvena vikhyāyate purāṇairvidhṛtā vibhinnā devatāḥ sādhāraṇajīvanopayogivividhāśākāṅkṣāvidhāyinyaḥ iti kāraṇāt tā priyā devātāḥ sañjātāḥ paurāṇika sāhitya vicitradharmādarśaviśvāsānā saṅgamasthalam sukhabodhyabhāṣayā likhitvāt paurāṇikī vāṇī sudūrasthānīyajanagaṇakarṇasamūhamapi praviśati karuṇātmako mahān guṇaḥ api tatra viśiṣṭa gurutva prāpnoti aya viṣayaḥ kathopakathādibhiḥ tiryak prativimbito bhavatiyeṣā mūlatvena kriyā kurvanti premabhaktiḥdānaśīlacittavṛttiḥsnehaḥkṣamāprativeśisulabhānubhavaḥ ceti sarveṣāmeva kendrabinduḥ eva karuṇā prāguktabhāveṣu anyatamenānuprāṇitāḥ santa upāsakāsteṣāmīpsitānā devatānā prasādalābhārthamāhvāna kurvanti tādṛśamabhigamana vastugatam ida hṛdayasya pelavāśataḥ jāyate ida japtā devatāḥprati yujyate yā devatāḥ karuṇārūpamūrtisatyaḥ bauddhadarśanasya mate sannyāsinaḥ kṣetre karuṇāyāḥ paridhiḥ avaśyameva vistṛto bhavet yadi tasya kopi śatrurbhavati tarhi ta pratyapi sannyāsī karuṇāparāyaṇo bhavet īdṛśaḥ sannyāsī nirvāṇamārgeṇa gacchan sarvavidhapratibandhakebhyaḥ mukto bhavati samādhayenuśīlana śatrubhāvānmukti na dadāti ida kevala hānihīnatāyāmānandānubhavaḥ tathā sarvasmai prītiriti hitāya śatrutā dūrīkaroti gahanadhyānena magnaḥ sannyāsī samavṛttisampanne paryāyevatiṣṭhate manasaḥ evavidhāyā daśāyā na kāpi virodhinī śaktiḥ tamapakartu śaknoti ata eva īdṛśyā daśāyā sannyāsinaḥ pakṣeunnatirodhipāpacintādamanāya mānasikyā śaktyā prayojana na bhavati viśuddhadaśāmupagatasya viśuddhacittasya sannyāsinaḥ unmārgagamanasambhāvanā sampūrṇatayā dūra gacchati tadā sannyāsī dhyānamagnastiṣṭhatu vā svābhāvikadaśāgatastiṣṭhatu vā iti na kopi viṣayaḥ etādṛśaḥ sannyāsī sarvadā karuṇāmayaśca premamayaśca tiṣṭhati sahanaśīla karuṇātmaka citta pratikūladaśāyā pratikriyā na karoti vibhnaśūnyadhyānāya jitendriyāḥ sannyāsinaḥ nyūnatamanamanīyavastubhiḥ santuṣṭā bhaveyuḥ iti gotamasyopadeśaḥ  aparisīmapremamayacittānuśīlana teṣa karttavyam sādhvida jñāta yat paurāṇikā ṛṣayaḥ jīvikāvyāpāre vā jīvanayāpanavyāpāre vā atīva namanīyā  āsan  te āśramajīvanopayoginyūnatamavastubhiḥ kāla yāpayitu śaknuvanti sma teṣā citteṣu dayānubhūtiḥ karuṇānubhūtiḥ vā prācuryeṇāsīt aya mahān āvegaḥ purāṇānā sarvatra prativimbitaḥ devā upāsakebhyo varān dadatite vipadāpannān bhaktān rakṣantivipadaśca tān muñcanti  iti tathya pramāṇīkaroti yat dayādhārā dānadhārā vā teṣu sarvadā sakriyāsīt etadapi ghaṭate yat kadāpi vā vararūpaḥ karuṇānubhavaḥ ayogyeṣu api vastuṣu vistāra yāti ṛṣayaḥ api tatphalabhoga kurvanti ṛṣaya ādhyātmikaprayatnena mahatī śaktimarjayanti janahitāya tacchaktiprayoga prāyeṇa te kurvanti teyācitabhāvenaiva svārthaśūnyā sevā yacchanti janagaṇāya ida pramāṇīkaroti yat tapasyā teṣā citta viśuddhīkaroti tathākaraṇena ca te kārtsnyena svārthaparatāmuktā jāyante svārthaśūnyatva tapasyāyāḥ lakṣyam ya eva etallakṣyamupagacchati sa ātmaupamyena apareṣā duḥkha vā sukha vā anubhavati purāṇāni khalu etaddhāvānuprāṇitaiḥ purāvṛttaiḥ bāhulyena paripūrṇāni brahmapurāṇasya  tamedhyāye kuvarṣerākhyānamasti sa sarveṣā kṣunnivṛttaye varāya prārthanā cakāra anena tasya māhātmya prakaṭitam śunaḥśephākhyāne varuṇasya gabhīrā karuṇā vayamanubhavāmaḥ yajñīyabalirūpasya bālakasya sahāyahīnā daśā varuṇasya manasi sahānubhūti tathā karuṇā jāgarayati sma sa ca ta rarakṣa mahānubhavatāyā bhāvopi nimnaprāṇinā hṛdayeṣu lakṣyate varāhapurāṇasya  tamedhyāye kasmiścidupākhyāne kapotasya pecakasya ca bhāryāyugala sādhāraṇakalyāṇāya iṣṭān devān āhvayati sma vāmanapurāṇasya  tamedhyāye vaśiṣṭhasyātulanīyā tyāgavṛttiḥ varṇitā evañca purāṇeṣu bahavo dṛṣṭāntāḥ santi yatra tyāgamahānubhavatākaruṇāsahānubhavādīnā tejomayo bhāvo vidyate  bauddhaśāstre yathā likhita tathā dṛśyate yat gautamo navadīkṣitān sannyāsina upadiśati yat sannyāsina utthānavicaraṇopaveśanādisamaye samādhyanuśīlanāya  dṛḍhasakalpā bhaveyuḥ  tathā ca te yadi upadeśānanusṛtya karma kurvantitarhi dhyānasamaye virodhiśaktayo niṣprabhā bhaviṣyanti mumukṣuḥ sannyāsī cittamuktaye karuṇābhyāsa kuryāt sannyāsinaḥ pakṣe hṛdaye karuṇābhyāsotīva phalapradaḥ tena abhyāsakārī yasmāt kasmādapi ākramaṇāt avamānād vā rakṣaṇāya śaktimarjayati kiñca upāsanālaye sannyāsinaḥ ekatra śānta śātu śaknuvanti yataḥ hṛdayeṣu karuṇānuśīlanatvāt teṣā hṛdayāni komalāni bhavanti tathā ca ekaḥ aparasya uttamaḥ sahacaraḥ bhavati nirvāṇalābhāya premakaruṇādhyāna prathamaḥ paryāyo bhūmikāsvarupaḥ tathāpi nirvāṇalābhāt paramapi bhūmikāvasthānatvādeva pramaparimalaḥ pareṣā hitāya avaśiṣṭo vartate ādhyātmikapragataye sannyāsinaḥ anyonyasahāyā bhaveyuḥ eṣāvasthā parokṣabhāvenāparānupakurvanti yaḥ sannyāsī pārthiva sukha jahāti sa eva prakṛtaḥ sannyāsī sa svīyakarmaṇāparān prabhāitān karoti gautamasya mate abhyāsakārī hṛdayena dhīratāhisākaruṇākomalatābhāvānuśīlanena ātmani hṛdaye sahanaśīlatā poṣayati ida guṇatrayasyārthaḥ sārvalaukikaḥ premā abhyāsakārī yadā sampūrṇa gūḍhadhyānamagnastiṣṭhati tadā guṇatrayamatīva śaktipūrṇa tathā phalapradam asmin paryāye abhyāsakārī sarvavidhaduṣṭakarmacintābhyo mukto bhavatitadā sa bhavacakrād vicchinno jāyate yathārthataḥ asmin paryāye abhyāsakāriṇo manaḥ mukta tiṣṭhati aya vyāpāraḥ kiyatāpyaśena yājakīyaḥatra abhyāsakārī kevala svārtha ceṣṭatekintu sahānubhūtau harṣaḥ parasukhasajātajarṣa sūcayati uktaprasage parārthaparatā gautamasya upadeśeṣu na sūcyatetathāpi ida niścita yat gūḍhadhyānamīdṛśaguṇāya sampadyate purāṇānā kathāsu īdṛśasvārthahīnasevāsambandhidṛṣṭāntāḥ itastataḥ varttante purāṇeṣu svārthaśūnyasevāyā mahatī maryādāstisevādharmo hi paramaguṇatvena vivicyate purāṇeṣu aya guṇaḥ na kevala sādhūnā citteṣu api tu nimnaprāṇinā hṛdayeṣu vartate karttavyabodhena saha ātithyādisevā sarveṣā hindūnā sādhāraṇaguṇatvena vivicyate kartavyabodho jāyate dayākaruṇānubhavāt aya bodho na svalpasthāyīkintu hinducaritrevicchedyo guṇaḥ atra hindūnā mūlyabodhaḥ pratiphalito bhavati pūrvapuruṣāṇā muktaye bhagīrathasya sahanaśīlatā tathā dhīratā svārthaśūnyasevāyāḥ karttavyabodhasya ca ādarśa sthāpayati atra sādhusulabhe dayā ca karuṇā ca vartete brahmāṇḍapurāṇasya  tamedhyāye naitikamūlabodhamavalambya nītikathā dṛśyate avarajīvānā hṛdayeṣu api kartavyabodhaḥ karuṇābhāvaśca śanaiḥ śanaiḥ praveśa labhete  sā ghaṭanā atīva vismayāvahā ca marmasparśinī ca yadā vaya paśyāmaḥ  yo vyādhaḥ vihagamithuna pāśabaddhamakarot tasyaiva kṣudhāyai puruṣo  vihagaḥ ātmāhūti dātumudyatobhavat  samagravyāpāramavalokya sa niṣādo nirvāk tathā āścaryānvitobhavat asmin paryāye sādhāraṇānāmapi janānāmīdṛśaḥ svabhāvaḥ sādhāraṇa eva bauddhaśāstrasya mate cittamuktiḥ katipayaguṇasamūhāya bhavati yo bhikṣuḥ sādhuḥ arthāt yasya citta sampūrṇa mukta sa kati guṇānarjayati sośubha svapna na paśyatisa gāḍhanidrā gacchati sa bhayaśūnyo bhavatina kopi naraḥ vā paśuḥ vā tamapakartu śaknotidevāsta rakṣanti tatra daivānugrahe snehabhāvo vartate agnista dagdhu na śaknotisa paramopalabdhi vinaiva maraṇāt para brahmapada labhate sarvopari sahānubhūtiḥ karuṇā ceti guṇadvaya dūḍhadhyānena saha samparkitamtathāpi taddvaya dhyānamagnatāyā na phalam yasyātmopalabdhiḥ sañjātā sa bhavacakrāt punarjanmmo vā muktaḥ asya paryāyasya lābhāya karuṇā hi avyavahito hetuḥnirāsaktiśca ānuṣaṅgikahetutva vrajati karuṇā gūḍhadhyānasyāparā mūrttiḥ kintu abhyāsakārī yadā tapasyāyā kramaśaḥ unnati sādhayati tadā tasya hṛdaye karuṇābhāvo jāyate antime paryāyerthāt nirvāṇasya paryāye sannyāsī sāmpūrṇyena niṣkāmo bhavati jāgatikasya vastusamūhasya kṣaṇikatāyā tathā asāratāyā sa sacetano jāyate asmin samaye abhyāsakārī pratikūladṛśyaghaṭanācaritrādiṣu pratikriyā na karoti yo janmasūtreṇa asīma prema labhatethavā yasya premamaya hṛdayamasti sa svalpakālena duṣṭamanobhāva niyantu śaknoti tataśca yadi sa yatatesa kramaśa unnati kartu śaknoti cāndrāyaṇavratadineṣu mahātmanaḥ guroḥ śiṣyā manasi sarveṣā jīvānā kṛte premakaruṇāmaya hṛdaya poṣayanti muktikarṣaṇāt manaḥ virodhiśaktiprabhāvāt mukta jāyate manasa īdṛgdaśāyā manaḥ kartsnyena mālinyamukta tiṣṭhati tādṛśe manasi karuṇāsahānubhūtaḥānandaḥsamavṛttitā cetyādayaḥ guṇā virājante tadā brahmasājuyya sambhavati karuṇāyā dhyātmaka karṣaṇa kṣatikarapariveśe pratikriyākaraṇāya viśeṣeṇa phalapradam premṇo dhyānātmaka karṣaṇa krodha pratihata kartu viśeṣata upayogi samavṛttitāyāḥ dhyātmaka karṣaṇa tṛṣṇāyā viruddhe pratikriyākaraṇāya viśeṣeṇa prayojanatva vrajati ete upadeśāḥ sāmājikakalyāṇasādhanāya anupreraṇā dadati sādhāraṇā janāḥ vṛkṣaropaṇāyasetunirmāṇāyakṛpakhananāya gṛhahīnebhya āśrayasya dānāya upadiśyante atra karuṇā duḥkhārtatāyāḥ kṛpāyāśca vicchinnā bhavet arthāt dhyātā puruṣaḥ kadāpi na paraduḥkheṣu kṛpānubhavenānupreritaḥ bhavetyena sa paraduḥkha vā parakaṣṭa dūrīkartumagrasaro bhavati dhyātuḥ pakṣe karuṇāyā aya bhāvaḥ satata svābhāviko bhavet yainānupreritaḥ san sannyāsī apareṣā duḥkha dūrīkartumāgacchati dhyātuḥ svābhāvikī pravṛttiḥ prāyeṇa rakṣayituḥ pravṛttiriva bhavet paurāṇikakathākārāṇā sādhūnāmiya svābhāvikī pravṛttirāsīt te kadāpi kutrāpi vā svābhāvikapravṛttiviruddha karma nākurvan teṣāmāsīt dhyānātmikī tathādhyātmikī śaktiḥ tayā tedbhuta karma kartu samarthā āsan tathāpi te tacchakteḥ apaprayoga na cakruḥ te janahitāyaiva alaukika karma kṛtavantaḥ teṣā komala hṛdaya snehabhāvasya āśrayasthalam snehaḥ eva tebhyo janasevāyai preraṇā dadāti svecchā tiṣṭhatu vā na tiṣṭhatu vā te karuṇātmakapravṛttivaśāt janahitakara kārya sādhayanti muneḥ saubhareḥ ākhyāne snehabhāva sahānubhūtiśca nirdiśyete taddvayaprabhāvāt sa svaya sundarataruṇarūpa dhṛtvā pakṣapātahīnavyavahāreṇa sarvāsā bhāryāṇā tṛpti vidhadhāti sma skandapurāṇasya kasmiścidākhyāne putrāya kārttikeyāya pārvatyāḥ apūrvamātṛsnehosmābhiḥ dṛśyate viṣṇupurāṇe vaya paśyāmo yat kena prakāreṇa bhagavān viṣṇuḥ snehāt garuḍasyācaraṇa svābhāvikamakarot bauddhānā mate dhyātuḥ sahānubhūta ānandaḥpremakaruṇā ca tadaiva nirdoṣatva vrajanti yadā dhyātā nirvāṇamārgasya caturtha paryāyamaupagacchati asmin paryāye samavṛttitā dhyātuḥ pakṣe atīva vāstaviko vyāpāraḥ antardṛṣṭikarṣaṇena krodhātśatrubhāvātasantoṣāt lobhāt ca muktiḥ jāyate purāṇamapi ātmopalabdhaye dhyānasyopari gurutva sthāpayatianyavidhayā praceṣṭayā prayojana na bhavati bauddhaśāstre upadeśo dīyate yat ācāryasyopadeśaiḥ dhyātāraḥ teṣāmindriyāṇā śakti vardhayiṣyanti tataśca samādhiyogena antardṛṣṭiḥ puṣṭi gacchati premasamavṛttitādīnām īpsitavastūnā siddhiḥ asthāyinī kintu yadā dhyātā dhyānayogena antardṛṣṭeḥ upari sthāpyate tadā krodhatṛṣṇādivirodhibhāvā svata eva dūra gacchanti manmayī upalabdhiḥ śreṣṭhatvasyāsane sthāpitā yadyapi bauddhaśāstreṣu navadīkṣitānā kṛte tanmayī praceṣṭā upadiśyatetathāpi teṣā pakṣe manmayī upalabdhiḥ api upayogitva vrajati aya vyāpāraḥ sampūrṇa navadīkṣitasya mānasikī sthiti tathā jīvana prati tasya manobhāvamapekṣate kintu sarvadaiva karuṇākarṣaṇamavaśyameva karttavyam sattāsu manaḥsthāpane tathā manaḥpoṣaṇe karuṇābhāvasya antarbhuktistiṣṭhati asya bhāvasya siddhau ānandamayaḥ rasa āvirbhāvati antardṛṣṭi vinā sthāpana poṣaṇa tathā ānandānubhavanamiti sahāvasthitamānasikakarmatraya manasi apṛthaktvena avibhājanīyatvenānubhūyateantardṛṣṭau satyā mānasikavyāpāratrayamadaḥ pṛthak pṛthak prakāśatepṛthak pṛthak ca kārya karoti sacetanamānasakṣetrasya gatiśīlatayā aya vyāpāraḥ sambhavati yadā etattraya dhyānayogena samanvitabhāvena prativimbita bhavati tadā sthirapariveśasya kṣaṇikatābhaṅguratāasthiratā ca upalabhyante sarve viṣayāstadā duḥkhamayāḥ kaṣṭamayāḥ svatantrāḥ śūnyamayā iva yoginaḥ nikaṭe pratibhānti asmin paryāye svārthaśūnyaḥ san yogī sampūrṇā muktimicchati sa tā mukti paśyati nirvāṇadaśāyāmeva tannirvāṇa punarjanmaśṛkhalāt dūre tiṣṭhati tadā sa sampūrṇakaruṇāyā sthāpito bhavati idameva mūla tattva bauddhadarśanasya paurāṇikasādhūnā karuṇāsahānubhūtimahattvādayo guṇāḥ āsan evavidhā bahavo dṛṣṭāntā asmābhiḥ dṛśyante sādhāraṇataḥsahānubhavasya mahatī anubhūtiḥ tīvrātmīyatābodhājjāyate kintu ṛṣīṇā kṣetreṣu svata eva tādṛśīpekṣikatā phalavatī na bhavatiyataḥ ṛṣaya ātmāna jānantijagataḥ prakṛtā sattā pratyakṣīkarvantitathā ca te teṣā pṛthagastitva vismaranti phalaśrutau te sarvābhiḥ sattābhiḥ saha ātmamatā svīkṛtya aparānubhūta duḥkha nijavadanubhavanti karuṇāsahānubhūtisamparkitopūrvo dṛṣṭāntaḥ matsyapurāṇe dṛśyate tatra kumbhīrākrāntabālaka prati śivabhāryāyā umāyāḥ sahānubhūtiḥ karuṇā ca prativimbite rājarṣīṇā bharatenāpi avarajīvān prati karuṇā kṛtā vayametadākhyāna viṣṇupurāṇe paśyāmaḥ abhiyojanasya bhāvāt kṣamānubhavo jāyate  yā kṣamā aparādhina janamuddiśya kriyate purāṇeṣu ṛṣibhiḥ aparādhina prati dayāyāstathā kṣamāyāḥ pradarśanamadhikṛtya vṛttāntā bāhulyena dṛśyante purāṇānāmākhyāne vaya paśyāmo yat kaścidṛṣiḥ karuṇāvaśāt uccāritamabhiśāpamapanayati kūrmapurāṇe kasmiścidākhyāne vaya paśyāmo yat muninā gautamena uccāritaśāpasambhūtadaṇḍasya hrāsaḥ kṛtaḥ eva vaya paśyāmaḥ  vaidikasya tathā paurāṇikasya darśanasya mataiḥ saha bauddhadarśanasya matānā niviḍa sānnidhya vartate tat sānnidhyamubhayordarśanayormadhye anyonyātmīyatva sūcayati ubhayordarśanayormadhye asmin cāritrike sambandhe sati hindubhiḥ daśāvatāreṣu anyatamāvatāratvena buddhadevaḥ svīkṛtaḥ iti
